<s> The old Kendrick place sat back in its grassy yard and concealed behind voluminous chinaberry trees such shabbiness as time had brought it but on the corner the home of Ezra Jackson perched proudly above its stone wall and added a considerable touch of elegance to the street </s>
<s> It was in the early eighties and the Queen Anne style of architecture was just coming into great popularity in the South </s>
<s> Jackson who could well afford it had let an architect have full sway in producing for him a dwelling in the new mode </s>
<s> Ezra Jackson a fullblooded negro born a slave had been a teamster on his master's Georgia plantation and after the war that master who still maintained friendly relations with his exslaves gave him a start in life with a mule and a dray </s>
<s> From this the honest industrious and enterprising man had built up a transfer business which was the best of its sort in town </s>
<s> There were many teams and drivers now and Ezra could walk in the garb of other men of means about him yet he still wrote his name in the manner of the kings of oldhe produced it as a sort of landscape effect without any idea of what the separate characters meant </s>
<s> He was a good citizen a dignified man and except for his black skin he would have been an acceptable neighbor to the Kendricks and a desirable resident in their quarter of town </s>
<s> The young wife whom he had married rather late in life and to whose taste the Queen Anne house catered had a good grammarschool education gained from those first devoted teachers that the Freedman's Bureau sent to the Southern negroes in the years immediately following the war </s>
<s> At first she had kept his books and made out his bills and she always insisted on the best of schooling for their children </s>
<s> Of these latter only Mary Louise concerns this history since she chanced to be very near the age of Ellen Kendrick and had become a necessity in the life of that peevish little invalid </s>
<s> The negro girl had smooth features and her mother saw to it that she was always spotlessly dressed and that her manners were perfect </s>
<s> The children of her race take to good manners very readily being usually amiable and eager for approbation </s>

<s> So that existence to Ellenthe pleasant part of it anyhowmeant a great deal of Ma'Lou and there was scarcely an object in her room a game or a pursuit of her days that was not associated with the brown girl </s>
<s> The pair grew up in a companionship closer than that of some born sisters </s>
<s> The mere fact of this intimacy was not regarded by the Kendricks with any disfavor whatever </s>
<s> Scott and Fanny both had played with negro children both had been reared by negro mammies </s>

<s> II As they grew older the association of the two girls in spite of the affection between themperhaps because of itbegan to present almost daily problems and embarrassments </s>
<s> Ellen's health was worse her nerves were shattered and she clung with more and more insistence to this one healthy companion who responded with a tireless devotion </s>

<s> Finally she walked as well as other girls and hastily made up her arrears of education as best she might at a private school in Watauga </s>
<s> She would always be frail the invalid habit had gotten into both mind and body she would continue dependent demanding and somewhat irritable yet there was a fragile prettiness about her and her very childishness had its own charm </s>
<s> Mary Louise Jackson passed one of two vacations at home but as time went on there were opportunities for her to have trips of an educational nature and one summer was spent at a Chautauqua taking a special course so that after the first break in their association the two girls saw almost nothing of each other till they were women grown </s>
<s> There had been some letters yet what the white girl had always demanded and received from her friend could not come through the mails and the neglected correspondence finally died a natural death </s>
<s> There was one person in Watauga however to whom Mary Louise wrote and from whom she received letters regularlyUlysses Grant Payson the washerwoman's son with whom she had gone to school </s>
<s> Grant Payson was a sober ambitious industrious fellow who seemed to feel from childhood the weight of responsibility for his people </s>
<s> A widow's only boy he had worked hard and studied hard </s>
<s> With a very fair mental endowment he was able to get what the Watauga public schools could give him secure a few years training at Nashville then read law </s>
<s> And when after her graduation Mary Louise returned to her father's home a very welleducated young lady indeed wearing glasses and looking older than her years she found Grant established in a good practice and with some other prospects that were for a colored man flattering </s>
<s> Both families knew that Grant wanted Ma'Lou </s>
<s> Whether the girl would marry him and settle down in Watauga had been a matter of anxiety often talked over between the two mothers </s>
<s> For they also knew of and discussed Ma'Lou's opportunity to take a position as private secretary to one of the instructors in her college </s>
<s> They understood that it was a situation which would pay fairly well and give her associates who gained an added glory in the minds of these humble folk by their distance </s>
<s> In short it would be a foothold in the white people's world and Grant Payson's mother trembled for her son while the mother of Mary Jackson feared to lose once for all her daughter </s>
<s> The two Southernbred black women could see in such things as the girl reported only the wiping out of all race barrier the sudden achievement of equality </s>
<s> Had Mary Louise been asked no doubt she could have told them of a social ban at the North quite as definite as that in Watauga if different but her father's daughter kept a silence that was not without dignity over what she found irremediable in the North as in the South </s>
<s> To warmhearted Mary Louise Watauga meant of course father and mother but directly after themperhaps before them in the calendar of youthit meant Ellen Kendrick and Grant Payson </s>
<s> And the colored elders looking on felt that as these twin idols of the girl turned out so rose or fell the chances of keeping her with them in Watauga </s>
<s> Grant instituted at once a courtship as ardent and eager as it was open and avowed </s>
<s> His people florid and colorful in temperament are natural wooers free of the language of affection and adroit in its use </s>
<s> Grant was very much in love with the girl and she meant even more to him than that since in aspiring to her his ambition stepped hand in hand with his affections </s>
<s> Mary Louise received his advances with curious reservations as though there were positions and premises she defended against him </s>
<s> It was when the girl's visit was three weeks old that the finelooking broadshouldered young colored man in his wellfitting business suita goodly figure in the eyes of the mother watching from her own room across the hallleft the parlor where he and Mary Louise had been sitting all evening with so doleful a countenance that the older woman had a quickly suppressed impulse to go to him and speak </s>
<s> She did open the subject to the girl next morning approaching it obliquely </s>
<s> In her own day a very progressive person she felt that her daughter had far outstripped her and she offered advice but timidly to this tall perfectly dressed young woman who seemed so competent in all the affairs of life and who knew so much more than she did upon many subjects </s>
<s> But after a little profitless skirmishing she came out with Looks like you must have said something hard to Grant last nighthe never came in to say goodby to me </s>

<s> Like so many others of her class Stella Willoughby was a satisfied confident woman placidly aware of the station her husband's money assured to her </s>
<s> For Willoughby was accounted wealthy even in this lake town where riches were so much in evidence and if the wife betrayed a cool superiority because of his money it was only natural perhaps since she and most of her associates knew no other means of gauging success or worth or the individual's place in life </s>
<s> Looking over her shoulder now she glanced nonchalantly across the club diningroom </s>
<s> You mean those peoplethe Severances Mrs. Kinsman </s>

<s> Queer they should come back here isn't it </s>

<s> In the hall while the maid was putting on her wraps she turned and looked back still idly as before </s>
<s> Her eyes traveling about rested a moment on the man sitting at the distant table and then when he half rose from his place as if to bow they journeyed on again coolly unconcerned </s>
<s> A moment later smiling gayly she walked down the steps to her carriage and with her guests was driven away to the theatre </s>
<s> Yet somehow in spite of this sureness of speech and manner the sight of her oldtime suitor had wakened in Mrs. Willoughby the subtle discontent that occasionally affected herthe discontent of women who have only themselves to think about </s>
<s> One might have said that at these times she was subconsciously wearied of her form of life that in so many words though ignorant of the fact though consciously her vacuous life immensely satisfied her she was BORED </s>
<s> But today bluntly speaking it was about her husband that her vague dissatisfaction centered and when she had glanced coolly at her former suitor it was for the purpose of comparison </s>
<s> Willoughby was a fair type of the moneygetter </s>
<s> Furthermore what he had built had been raised by his own hands unaided he was a selfmade man whose one boast was that he owed nothing to any one not even so little as a debt of gratitude </s>
<s> One realized the fact too in the way he carried on his affairs for in his business he was alert and determined implacably pursuing his moneymaking as if it were a warfare and considerate of none but those joined with him in the moment's harvesting venture </s>
<s> Perhaps his reasons were sufficientwho knows </s>
<s> Perhaps Willoughby was as well aware as they that the friends of today might reasonably become the enemies of tomorrow </s>
<s> But at home the money gathered so ruthlessly elsewhere was thrown about with a lavish hand </s>
<s> Nothing that wealth could provide was denied Mrs. Willoughby or her boy and though she had been poor when she married money in the mere crudity of having it to spend had long since lost its novelty </s>
<s> Today beyond the pride of having it and beyond the luxury and ostentation it could buy money possessed for her a far greater significance in its power to make one powerful </s>
<s> In that she had already tasted the illogical enjoyment of one that can obtain power in no other way </s>
<s> And it was because of this place that his money had bought her that Mrs. Willoughby began to look on her husband with a critical eye </s>
<s> For she was an ambitious woman though one with definite limitations </s>
<s> Among different surroundings and in an atmosphere less sordidly striving and commonplace she was fitted to have become with some encouragement an admirable and utterly inconspicuous wife and mother </s>
<s> But here in this narrow moneygetting environment many things prevented among them primarily the way in which she had been brought up </s>
<s> For her father too had been driven by this lust for riches and though he had failed to the last he had been goaded on by his one eager grasping hope </s>
<s> He had drummed into her head the single lesson that without money one is nothing </s>
<s> In itself it suggested to the few a plausible reason why she had married Willoughby </s>
<s> There had been nothing openly unhappy in their life together </s>
<s> Still as others saw Willoughby was much older than his wife radically without her social instincts and furthermore when she had accepted him it had been pretty generally understood that Severance had won her heart </s>

<s> Vol. XXIII No.1 JULY 1910 The Painter of Diana of the Tides pages 95103 By WALTER PRICHARD EATON Author of The American Stage of Today etc </s>
<s> Given nearly three hundred square feet of blank wall space and it takes something of an artist to fill it up with interesting paint </s>
<s> Probably you would not pick a miniature painter for the task </s>
<s> Yet curiously John Elliott creator of Diana of the Tides the great mural painting which adorns the large gallery to the right of the entrance of the new National Museum at Washington also paints on ivory </s>
<s> He works likewise in silver point that delicate and difficult medium he draws pastel illustrations for children's fairy tales he works in portraiture with red chalk or oils </s>
<s> And when the need comes he has shown that he can turn stevedore carpenter and architect to slave with the relief party at Messina finally to help design and build in four months an entire village for the stricken sufferers including a hotel a hospital three schoolhouses and a church </s>
<s> The too frequent scorn of the practical man of affairs for the artist and dreamer the world's sneaking tolerance for the temperament which creates in forms of ideal beauty rather than in bridges or factories or banks finds in the life and work of such a man as John Elliott such complete if unconscious refutation that his story should have its place in the history of the day </s>
<s> John Elliott was born on Good Friday 1859 one of a famous Scottish border family </s>
<s> His residence is now in Boston Massachusetts at the home of his motherinlaw </s>
<s> Mrs. Julia Ward Howe </s>
<s> Robert Louis Stevenson had Elliott blood in his veins </s>
<s> Parts of me he once wrote have shouted the slogan of the Elliotts in the debatable land </s>
<s> If Stevenson's Homeric account of the Four Black Elliotts in Weir of Hermiston is historically veracious we might fancy that one of their descendants would feel his activities somewhat cramped on Beacon Street Boston </s>
<s> The Elliotts were a wild lot and some of them did not escape the hangman </s>
<s> Their family tree appears to have been the gallows </s>
<s> But Stevenson tells us they were noted for their prayers and at least one of them wrote poetry and declaimed it drunk to Walter Scott who retaliated in kind </s>
<s> But the present John Elliott artist though he is of the kin of Stevenson and bears the dark hair and rather prominent melancholy eyes of the traditional Elliott stock yet physically much more closely resembles Edgar Allan Poe </s>
<s> If you press him hard he will confess that he began life by studying for the stage and almost played Romeo before painting drew him away </s>
<s> Reaching Italy he aspired to enter the studio of Don Jose di Villegas now director of the Prado Museum in Madrid but then in Rome </s>
<s> Villegas took no pupils </s>
<s> But Jack Elliott is Scotch </s>
<s> He made a bargain </s>
<s> He would teach the master English in return for instruction in painting </s>
<s> At the end of two years young Elliott had learned much about art but the master he says had acquired only one English phraseI haf no money </s>
<s> At the end of two years Elliott wished to leave because he despaired of painting like his master </s>
<s> That is why I keep you said Villegas you have retained your own manner and choice of subjects </s>
<s> So the pupil stayed on in Rome for five years sharing his studio later with Aristide Sartorio now a leading Italian painter </s>
<s> Here in the Via Flaminia he painted his first important mural decoration for the dining room of Mrs. Potter Palmer's Chicago Lake Shore mansion </s>
<s> This work called The Vintage is decorously inebriate a vinous riot of little cupids </s>
<s> It led shortly after his marriage in 1887 to Miss Maud Howe a daughter of Mrs. Julia Ward Howe to his establishing himself in Chicago where he did many decorations and portraits </s>
<s> In 1894 he went back to Rome to execute a commission for a huge ceiling piece for the Boston Public Library </s>
<s> The piece was for a room later converted into a children's room and after the canvas was placed in 1901 the incongruity of the adult painting and the purposes of the room caused unfavorable comment </s>
<s> But the room has been recently readjusted </s>
<s> It is now lined with high oak shelves almost to the cornice filled with musty old books of a beautiful brownperhaps the most effective decoration in the worldand the ceiling tells at its true value </s>
<s> This ceiling fifty feet square divided into two equal panels represents the twenty Christian centuries as horses led by the hours winged female figures out of the mists of the past into the illumination of the present </s>
<s> The models for the horses were the undersized nags of the Roman Campagna which are small but decorative beasties as Mr. Elliott puts it and lend themselves to a slightly conventional treatment </s>
<s> They sweep two by two out of a cool mistiness round the ceiling past the suggestion of a pale moon into the full radiance of the golden orb of the sun </s>
<s> The triumph of the picture is its handling of the problem of light </s>
<s> This golden daybreak pierces the mists whereon the horses gallop touches here a flank there a wing feather on one of the hours and warms to rosy glow the tip of a cloud </s>
<s> It appears in unexpected places grows where only shadow seemed to be and surprises you anew each time you look up </s>
<s> Painted in the flatthat is with no part of the picture telling as farther from the eye than another to distort the proportions of the roomthe ceiling yet has great depth distance airy lightness </s>
<s> It is a true decorative painting </s>
<s> While at work upon it Mr. Elliott painted many portraits including the wellknown red chalk heads of the Soldiers Three Lord Ava the Marquis of Winchester and General Wauchope the portrait of His Royal Highness the Duke of Cambridge and that of Lady Katherine Thynne now Lady Cromer a celebrated English beauty </s>
<s> Indeed he made her the model for the second hour in the Boston ceiling the figure next to the leader in the procession </s>
<s> Three studies of her head for this figure well known from reproduction are now in the possession of Thomas W </s>
<s> Lawson </s>
<s> In Rome the Elliotts occupied for some time the apartments of Mrs. Elliott's cousin the late F </s>
<s> Marion Crawford in the Palazzo Santa Croce </s>
<s> In writing With the Immortals Mr. Crawford had collected many death masks including one of Dante which fascinated Mr. Elliott </s>
<s> Two pictures of Dante in Exile were the result </s>
<s> One of them now hangs in the living room of Queen Margherita of Italy the other in the house of Mrs. J </s>
<s> Montgomery Sears of Boston </s>
<s> A third pastel study was made an unfinished head of the poet and thrown into a wastebasket </s>
<s> By a curious fatality it is now better known than either of the paintings </s>
<s> Mrs. Elliott rescued the drawing smoothed it out framed it and was allowed to hang it in her chamber </s>
<s> Later it was seen and purchased by Mrs. David Kimball of Boston and in reproduction has gone all over the world receiving honors in Japan and the higher honor of a place over the desk of many Dante students </s>
<s> Yet few who possess the reproduction know anything of the artist </s>
<s> Mr. Elliott receiving his commission to do a great mural painting for the new National Museum in Washington again went to Rome four years ago </s>
<s> Diana of the Tides was completed and signed on Christmas day 1908 </s>
<s> Three days later came the awful news of the Messina earthquake and the Hon </s>
<s> Lloyd Griscom then American Ambassador to Italy at once called for volunteers for his relief expedition </s>
<s> John Elliott was among the first to respond </s>
<s> He went south officially as an interpreter </s>
<s> Actually he played the part of stevedore as well for ten days on the relief ship </s>
<s> I have dropped my last knuckle down the hold this morning he wrote back and I have only two fingers left that I can wash </s>
<s> After a few weeks he hastened back to Rome to give a promised public exhibition of Diana of the Tides and as soon as the exhibition was over rushed down to Messina again </s>
<s> There Commander Belknap who was at the head of the American relief forces put him to work as architect on the erection of the American village in the lemon groves on the outskirts of the stricken city </s>
<s> I had never been trained as an architect he says but I once made over a house up in Cornish New Hampshire and that gave me a practical experience which came in remarkably handy </s>
<s> Most of the lumber had been cut for the erection of small houses and the door and window frames were stock pieces </s>
<s> It became his task to design and build as quickly as could be done not only comfortable houses for many thousand people but a church a hotel three schools a hospital all out of these small lumber units </s>
<s> He combined the units for the larger buildings so grouping the small stock window frames as to give a pleasing effect of size even constructing a kind of rose window for the church </s>
<s> He helped lay out the streets in such a way as to preserve all the trees possible </s>
<s> And in spite of the haste with which the work had to he done and the sixteenhouraday strain under which the workers labored the Zona Americana emerged an attractive and sanitary as well as practical village </s>
<s> Queen Helena as soon as the American village was under way got Mr. Elliott to go over the drafts for the plans of the American quarter in her village near by working them up along the same lines </s>
<s> So in four months he designed and superintended the erection of houses churches schools and hospitals for a town of several thousand inhabitants </s>
<s> Commander Belknap's report spoke of him as the first to volunteer and the most devoted worker sharing every hardship with unfailing good humor and leaving his beautifying touch on every part of the work </s>
<s> On June 12 1908 having built his town and recovered his lost knuckles John Elliott returned to Rome where the soil did not rock and set quietly about making twentyfour small pastel drawings to illustrate a fairy story </s>
<s> From building houses for the wretched homeless sufferers he turned to the play tales of childhood </s>
<s> He laid down the T square and the hammer for a piece of pastel crayon </s>
<s> But he had triumphantly refuted the scorn of the practical man for the artist </s>
<s> He had shown the stuff that dreams are really made of </s>
<s> Incidentally he had won for himself a decoration from the King of Italy and the medal of the American Red Cross Association </s>
<s> Diana of the Tides which now covers the end wall of the righthand gallery of the new National Museum at Washington is akin to the Boston Library ceiling in its employment of horses symbolically its light luminous color and its subtle play of illumination </s>
<s> This charm of illumination is unfortunately lost in reproduction </s>
<s> Mr. Elliott has made symbolic use of Diana the Moon Goddess </s>
<s> in a way obvious enough but hitherto oddly untried by artists </s>
<s> It is a way singularly appropriate in a museum of scientific charactera combination of ancient myth and modern science </s>
<s> As the Moon Goddess Diana controls the four tides which in the shape of horses draw her erect and jubilant figure on a great seashell </s>
<s> They are without guiding reins and harness to suggest the unseen channels of her sway </s>
<s> If the reader will note an advancing wave he will see that just before the crest curls over the foam is tossed back </s>
<s> Then the wave bows and breaks </s>
<s> So the nearest horse raises his head slightly the next higher the third tosses his head back and the last has bowed his neck </s>
<s> In their motion and grouped attitudes </s>
<s> as they gallop up on the beach is the rhythm of an oncoming wave </s>
<s> Farther than that Mr. Elliott wisely did not go </s>
<s> Let them suggest more obviously a wave he says and you have a trick picture </s>
<s> After a while you wouldn't see anything in it but the trick </s>
<s> The wave motion is repeated on a comber out at sea and to the left against a rock on the shore </s>
<s> Diana stands behind the horses against the great golden moona radiant halo </s>
<s> She has just unloosed an arrow from her bow </s>
<s> Her draperies are of indefinite color the rose and lilac and amber of sunset </s>
<s> Her face it will be noted though she stands against the moon is lighted from in front </s>
<s> In that fact lies the secret of the illumination </s>
<s> For this picture was supposedly painted at that one Byronic hour of the year when The sun was setting opposite the moon </s>
<s> Turner in a small water color has worked out a similar problem with the cool copper of the harvest moonlight bathing one side of an old stone tower the warm rose of sunset the other </s>
<s> In Mr. Elliott's great canvas the mutual lights kill all shadows and out toward the great yellow disk of the moon the invisible sun floods its lilac and pink kindling the waves the draperies of the goddess the wet flanks of the horses and suffusing the whole painting with its delicate bright warmth which is yet kept too cool for gaudiness by the twilight of the moon </s>
<s> While this canvas was being unpacked in Washington last winter Mr. Elliott was exhibiting in Boston his portrait of his motherinlaw Mrs. Julia Ward Howe </s>
<s> It was begun and nearly finished at Newport four or five years ago but Mr. Elliott has not cared to complete it for during the interval the Grand Old Lady has considerably changed in appearance </s>
<s> She is now more than ninety years old </s>
<s> When the sittings began Mrs. Howe had just recovered from an illness and could read or talk only for brief periods </s>
<s> Mostly she sat looking out of her window at a bird which had a nest in a nearby tree </s>
<s> In this attitude the eyes raised the face quiet yet alert the artist has caught her calm patient but with one hand characteristically clenched on the arm of her chair showing a touch of hidden force and commanding will </s>
<s> She is dressed in light green </s>
<s> The background is an indistinguishable brown </s>
<s> Her eyes have that very delicate light blue of advanced age wistful yet prophetic </s>
<s> The skin too has the rare ivory delicacy of old age of old age gently dealt with and protected </s>
<s> The light is unobtrusive yet luminousmorning sunshine </s>
<s> The picture is utterly simple the more so for its touch of incompleteness </s>
<s> The masses are broad artless </s>
<s> It is tender reverential a sweet and solemn glorification of old age and of the old age of a distinguished spirit </s>
<s> And at the exhibition in Boston one of the women visitors complained to the artist But you know Mr. Elliott when Mrs. Howe comes to the Woman's Club she always looks so bright and animated and always has something smart to say </s>
<s> To which the artist replied No doubt my dear lady </s>
<s> But I was not painting a president of the New England Woman's Club but the author of `The Battle Hymn of the Republic.' Queen Margherita of Italy made a truer comment when she saw the portrait in Mr. Elliott's studio in Rome </s>
<s> That portrait deserves to go into any collection in the world she said not because it is a good portrait of a distinguished old woman but because it is a portrait of Old age as it ought to be </s>
<s> Can it be that a mere Continental Queen is a better judge of art than a member of a Boston Woman's Club </s>
<s> Such thoughts are very disturbing </s>
<s> Queen Margherita ever since she first visited Mr. Elliott's studio in Rome ten years ago has been his warm patron </s>
<s> It was for her he made his well known silverpoint portrait of the late King Humbert which she carries with her on all journeys </s>
<s> It has indeed the boldness of line inseparable from good silverpoint drawing where a stroke once laid on is indelible and no working over is possible </s>
<s> When Diana of the Tides was exhibited in Rome in February 1909 the Queen was one of the first visitors </s>
<s> She was not the first the Chinese Minister arriving ahead of all others on the stroke of tenthe opening hourattended by all his suite to signify his profound Celestial veneration for the Fine Arts </s>
<s> The Queen seeing the picture expressed delight and volunteered to tell her son King Victor Emmanuel about it </s>
<s> A few days later at seven thirty in the morning there came a knocking at the door with the announcement A message from the King </s>
<s> The King said the messenger would follow in an hour </s>
<s> Presumably there was some hurry of preparation in the Elliott family </s>
<s> A New York artist at any rate at seven thirty A </s>
<s> M. would be in no condition to receive a crowned heador any other </s>
<s> Promptly at eight thirtypunctuality being a royal virtueKing Victor Emmanuel drove up in a motor car with two aides </s>
<s> He remained half an hour </s>
<s> Being fond of horses he found much in the picture genuinely to interest him </s>
<s> The artist accompanied the monarch to the door of his car where he thanked him for the honor of his visit </s>
<s> Not at all said the King in his excellent English </s>
<s> My mother told me to come </s>
<s> Which shows at least that the Fifth Commandment is honored in Italy </s>
<s> The twentyfour pastel drawings made to illustrate Mrs. Anderson's fairy tale The Great Sea Horse were also exhibited in America last winter </s>
<s> Made immediately after Mr. Elliott's heartbreaking labor on the rocking soil of Sicily they are none the less quiet childish and fanciful in their charm </s>
<s> Only one of them might have been inspired by the turning over in his uneasy sleep of the giant buried beneath Etnathe picture of the naked giant sitting on a headland and emptying his hot pipe ashes into the sea where they form a volcano </s>
<s> The grim grotesque old fellow is carefully drawn with a fine rhythm of line in the seated limbs </s>
<s> His bulk dwarfs the headland and his head and shoulders grow blue and pale in the sky </s>
<s> One questions why the ashes do not fall farther out to sea they seem to lie in the shallow tide water on the beach </s>
<s> Barring this note of smallness the picture is a true grotesque in miniature </s>
<s> Mr. Elliott also works in genuine miniature </s>
<s> He has painted several portraitsof Mrs. Potter Palmer the Chanler sisters of New York and many more </s>
<s> He has painted landscapes as well </s>
<s> Professor Barrett Wendell possesses a charming example </s>
<s> Most recently he has been engaged on a large mural decoration best fitted perhaps for a music room showing Pan seated on a tree trunk by a lake making into a pipe the broken reeds in his hand after Syrinx eluded him </s>
<s> No horizon line shows </s>
<s> Pan and his tawny leopard skin his automobile coat the artist calls it tell against the high purple banks across the lake </s>
<s> The god is making the best of his lossmaking music of it in fact </s>
<s> He was the eternal boy before Mr. Barrie rediscovered him and surnamed him Peter </s>
<s> And there is something of the eternal boy about John Elliott </s>
<s> He plays with a paint box on a fiftyfoot ceiling or a twentyseven foot end wall turns aside to paint a miniature on ivory drops all his paints when a great national calamity comes and is converted into an architect overnight building a whole town in four months and making it as beautiful as he can in the process though the practical man would say that utility alone was demanded and then when this work is over turning blithely back again to make pictures for a fairy book </s>
<s> He is strong through his fresh imagination to combine ancient myth with modern science in a huge decorative canvas to reflect the dignity and loveliness and spiritual power of an exalted old age to do practical work in a practical crisisand to joy at the same time with the moon baby dancing on the beach </s>
<s> Jack Elliott they will tell you who know him has an artistic temperament </s>
<s> Well if this be the artistic temperament what a pity there is not more of it in the world </s>
<s> It is not the temperament that is selfcentered whining ineffectual </s>
<s> It is the temperament that does whatever comes to hand as well as it can for sheer love of the task and of beautiful workmanship that through imagination wins to sympathy and through imagination grasps the opportunity to do practical work beautifully where others would only do it practically </s>
<s> It is the temperament eternally boyish and buoyant which is on the side of sweetness and light </s>
<s> Perhaps it is not what the world means by the artistic temperament </s>
<s> But it is the temperament of the true artist </s>
<s> Never do a potboiler said Mr. Elliott to a young painter the other day </s>
<s> Let one of your best things go to boil the pot </s>
<s> In these words is a rule of conduct that all of usartists or artisans brokers or clerks men or womenmight well walk by toward the light of a more beautiful and cooperative society </s>
<s> Vol. XXIII No.2 AUGUST 1910 THE HEATHEN page 193204 By JACK LONDON Author of The Call of the Wild Martin Eden etc </s>
<s> I met him first in a hurricane </s>
<s> And though we had been through the hurricane on the same schooner it was not until the schooner had gone to pieces under us that I first laid eyes on him </s>
<s> Without doubt I had seen him with the rest of the Kanaka crew on board but I had not consciously been aware of his existence for the Petite Jeanne was rather overcrowded </s>
<s> In addition to her eight or ten Kanaka sea men her white captain mate and supercargo and her six cabin passengers she sailed from Rangiroa with something like eightyfive deck passengersPaumotuans and Tahitians men women and children each with a tradebox to say nothing of sleepingmats blankets and clothesbundles </s>
<s> The pearling season in the Paumotus was over and all hands were returning to Tahiti </s>
<s> The six of us cabin passengers were pearlbuyers </s>
<s> Two were Americans one was Ah Choon the whitest Chinese I have ever known one was a German one was a Polish Jew and I completed the halfdozen </s>
<s> It had been a prosperous season </s>
<s> Not one of us had cause for complaint nor one of the eightyfive deck passengers either </s>
<s> All had done well and all were looking forward to a restoff and a good time in Papeete </s>
<s> Of course the Petite Jeanne was overloaded </s>
<s> he was only seventy tons and she had no right to carry a tithe of the mob she had on board </s>
<s> Beneath her hatches she was crammed and jammed with pearl shell and copra </s>
<s> Even the traderoom was packed full of shell </s>
<s> It was a miracle that the sailors could work her </s>
<s> There was no moving about the decks </s>
<s> They simply climbed back and forth along the rails </s>
<s> In the nighttime they walked upon the sleepers who carpeted the deck two deep I'll swear </s>
<s> Oh and there were pigs and chickens on deck and sacks of yams while every conceivable place was festooned with strings of drinking cocoanuts and bunches of bananas </s>
<s> On both sides between the fore and main shrouds guys had been stretched just low enough for the foreboom to swing clear and from each of these guys at least fifty bunches of bananas were suspended </s>
<s> It promised to be a messy passage even if we did make it in the two or three days that would have been required if the southeast trades had been blowing fresh </s>
<s> But they weren't blowing fresh </s>
<s> After the first five hours the trade died away in a dozen gasping fans </s>
<s> The calm continued all that night and the next dayone of those glaring glossy calms when the very thought of opening one's eyes to look at it is sufficient to cause a headache </s>
<s> The second day a man died an Easter Islander one of the best divers that season in the lagoon </s>
<s> Smallpox that is what it was though how smallpox could come on board when there had been no known cases ashore when we left Rangiroa is beyond me </s>
<s> There it was though smallpox a man dead and three others down on their backs </s>
<s> There was nothing to be done </s>
<s> We could not segregate the sick nor could we care for them </s>
<s> We were packed like sardines </s>
<s> There was nothing to do but diethat is there was nothing to do after the night that followed the first death </s>
<s> On that night the mate the supercargo the Polish Jew and four native divers sneaked away in the large whaleboat </s>
<s> They were never heard of again </s>
<s> In the morning the captain promptly scuttled the remaining boats and there we were </s>
<s> That day there were two deaths the following day three then it jumped to eight </s>
<s> It was curious to see how we took it </s>
<s> The natives for instance fell into a condition of dumb stolid fear </s>
<s> The captainOudouse his name was a Frenchmanbecame very nervous and voluble </s>
<s> The German the two Americans and myself bought up all the Scotch whisky and proceeded to drink </s>
<s> The theory was beautifulnamely if we kept ourselves soaked in alcohol every smallpox germ that came into contact with us would immediately be scorched to a cinder </s>
<s> And the theory worked though I must confess that neither Captain Oudouse nor Ah Choon was attacked by the disease either </s>
<s> The Frenchman did not drink at all while Ah Choon restricted himself to one drink daily </s>
<s> We had a week of it and then the whisky gave out </s>
<s> It was just as well or I shouldn't be alive now </s>
<s> It took a sober man to pull through what followed as you will agree when I mention the little fact that only two men did pull through </s>
<s> The other man was the Heathenat least that was what I heard Captain Oudouse call him at the moment I first became aware of the Heathen's existence </s>
<s> But to come back </s>
<s> It was at the end of the week that I happened to glance at the barometer that hung in the cabin companionway </s>
<s> Its normal register in the Paumotus was 29.90 and it was quite customary to see it vacillate between 29.85 and 30.00 or even 30.05 but to see it as I saw it down to 29.62 was sufficient to chill the blood of any pearlbuyer in Oceania </s>
<s> I called Captain Oudouse's attention to it only to be informed that he had watched it going down for several hours </s>
<s> There was little to do but that little he did very well considering the circumstances </s>
<s> He took off the light sails shortened right down to storm canvas spread lifelines and waited for the wind </s>
<s> His mistake lay in what he did after the wind came </s>
<s> He hove to on the port tack which was the right thing to do south of the Equator IFand there was the rubIF one were NOT in the direct path of the hurricane </s>
<s> We were in the direct path </s>
<s> I could see that by the steady increase of the wind and the equally steady fall of the barometer </s>
<s> I wanted to turn and run with the wind on the port quarter until the barometer ceased falling and then to heave to </s>
<s> We argued till he was reduced to hysteria but budge he would not </s>
<s> The worst of it was that I could not get the rest of the pearlbuyers to back me up </s>
<s> Who was I anyway to know more about the sea and its ways than a properly qualified captain </s>
<s> Of course the sea rose with the wind frightfully and I shall never forget the first three seas the Petite Jeanne shipped </s>
<s> She had fallen off as vessels do when hove to and the first sea made a clean breach </s>
<s> The lifelines were only for the strong and well and little good were they even for these when the women and children the bananas and cocoanuts the pigs and tradeboxes the sick and the dying were swept along in a solid screeching groaning mass </s>
<s> The second sea filled the Petite Jeanne's decks flush with the rails and as her stern sank down and her bow tossed skyward all the miserable dunnage of life and luggage poured aft </s>
<s> It was a human torrent </s>
<s> They came headfirst feetfirst sidewise rolling over and over twisting squirming writhing and crumpling up </s>
<s> Now and again one or another caught a grip on a stanchion or a rope but the weight of the bodies behind tore such grips loose </s>
<s> I saw what was coming sprang on top the cabin and from there into the mainsail itself </s>
<s> Ah Choon and one of the Americans tried to follow me but I was one jump ahead of them </s>
<s> The American was swept away and over the stern like a piece of chaff </s>
<s> Ah Choon caught a spoke of the wheel and swung in behind it </s>
<s> But a strapping Rarotonga vahine[1]she must have weighed two hundred and fiftybrought up against him and got an arm around his neck </s>
<s> He clutched the Kanaka steersman with his other hand </s>
<s> And just at that moment the schooner flung down to starboard </s>
<s> The rush of bodies and the sea that was coming along the port runway between the cabin and the rail turned abruptly and poured to starboard </s>
<s> Away they went vahine Ah Choon and steersman and I swear I saw Ah Choon grin at me with philosophic resignation as he cleared the rail and went under </s>
<s> [1] woman The third seathe biggest of the threedid not do so much damage </s>
<s> By the time it arrived nearly everybody was in the rigging </s>
<s> On deck perhaps a dozen gasping halfdrowned and halfstunned wretches were rolling about or attempting to crawl into safety </s>
<s> They went by the board as did the wreckage of the two remaining boats </s>
<s> The other pearlbuyers and myself between seas managed to get about fifteen women and children into the cabin and battened down </s>
<s> Little good it did the poor creatures in the end </s>
<s> Wind </s>
<s> Out of all my experiences I could not have believed it possible for the wind to blow as it did </s>
<s> There is no describing it </s>
<s> How can one describe a nightmare </s>
<s> It was the same way with that wind </s>
<s> It tore the clothes off our bodies </s>
<s> I say TORE THEM OFF and I mean it </s>
<s> I am not asking you to believe it </s>
<s> I am merely telling something that I saw and felt </s>
<s> There are times when I do not believe it myself </s>
<s> I went through it and that is enough </s>
<s> One could not face that wind and live </s>
<s> It was a monstrous thing and the most monstrous thing about it was that it increased and continued to increase </s>
<s> Imagine countless millions and billions of tons of sand </s>
<s> Imagine this sand tearing along at ninety a hundred a hundred and twenty or any other number of miles per hour </s>
<s> Imagine further this sand to be invisible impalpable yet to retain all the weight and density of sand </s>
<s> Do all this and you may get a vague inkling of what that wind was like </s>
<s> Perhaps sand is not the right comparison </s>
<s> Consider it mud invisible impalpable but heavy as mud </s>
<s> Nay it goes beyond that </s>
<s> Consider every molecule of air to be a mudbank in itself </s>
<s> Then try to imagine the multitudinous impact of mudbanksno it is beyond me </s>
<s> Language may be adequate to express the ordinary conditions of life but it cannot possibly express any of the conditions of so enormous a blast of wind </s>
<s> It would have been better had I stuck by my original intention of not attempting a description </s>
<s> I will say this much The sea which had risen at first was beaten down by that wind </s>
<s> Moreit seemed as if the whole ocean had been sucked up in the maw of the hurricane and hurled on through that portion of space which previously had been occupied by the air </s>
<s> Of course our canvas had gone long before </s>
<s> But Captain Oudouse had on the Petite Jeanne something I had never before seen on a South Sea schooner a seaanchor </s>
<s> It was a conical canvas bag the mouth of which was kept open by a huge hoop of iron </s>
<s> The seaanchor was bridled something like a kite so that it bit into the water as a kite bites into the airbut with a difference </s>
<s> The seaanchor remained just under the surface of the ocean in a perpendicular position </s>
<s> A long line in turn connected it with the schooner </s>
<s> As a result the Petite Jeanne rode bowon to the wind and to what little sea there was </s>
<s> The situation really would have been favorable had we not been in the path of the storm </s>
<s> True the wind itself tore our canvas out of the gaskets jerked out our topmasts and made a raffle of our running gear but still we would have come through nicely had we not been square in front of the advancing stormcenter </s>
<s> That was what fixed us </s>
<s> I was in a state of stunned numbed paralyzed collapse from enduring the impact of the wind and I think I was just about ready to give up and die when the center smote us </s>
<s> The blow we received was an absolute lull </s>
<s> There was not a breath of air </s>
<s> The effect on one was sickening </s>
<s> Remember that for hours we had been at terrific muscular tension withstanding the awful pressure of that wind </s>
<s> And then suddenly the pressure was removed </s>
<s> I know that I felt as though I were about to expand to fly apart in all directions </s>
<s> It seemed as if every atom composing my body was repelling every other atom and was on the verge of rushing off irresistibly into space </s>
<s> But that lasted only for a moment </s>
<s> Destruction was upon us </s>
<s> In the absence of the wind and its pressure the sea rose </s>
<s> It jumped it leaped it soared straight toward the clouds </s>
<s> Remember from every point of the compass that inconceivable wind was blowing in toward the center of calm </s>
<s> The result was that the seas sprang up from every point of the compass </s>
<s> There was no wind to check them </s>
<s> They popped up like corks released from the bottom of a pail of water </s>

<s> They were not seas at all </s>
<s> They resembled no sea a man had ever seen </s>

<s> They were more than eighty </s>
<s> They went over our mastheads </s>
<s> They were spouts explosions </s>
<s> They were drunken </s>
<s> They fell anywhere anyhow </s>

<s> They rushed together and collapsed upon one another or fell apart like a thousand waterfalls all at once </s>

<s> It was confusion thrice confounded </s>
<s> It was anarchy </s>
<s> It was a hellpit of sea water gone mad </s>
<s> The Petite Jeanne </s>
<s> I don't know </s>
<s> The Heathen told me afterward that he did not know </s>

<s> The wind was blowing again the sea was much smaller and more regular and I knew that I had passed through the center </s>

<s> The hurricane had dissipated the ravenous horde that had surrounded the death ship </s>
<s> It was about midday when the Petite Jeanne went to pieces and it must have been two hours afterward when I picked up with one of her hatchcovers </s>
<s> Thick rain was driving at the time and it was the merest chance that flung me and the hatchcover together </s>
<s> A short length of line was trailing from the rope handle and I knew that I was good for a day at least if the sharks did not return </s>
<s> Three hours later possibly a little longer sticking close to the cover and with closed eyes concentrating my whole soul upon the task of breathing in enough air to keep me going and at the same time to avoid breathing in enough water to drown me it seemed to me that I heard voices </s>

<s> I never had a brother but from what I have seen of other men's brothers I doubt if any man ever had one who was to him what Otoo was to me </s>

<s> It began in Papeete immediately after his announcement that he was going with me over all the sea and the islands in the midst thereof </s>
<s> There was a club in those days in Papeete where the pearlers traders captains and South Sea adventurers foregathered </s>

<s> Then I told him flatly I stood in need of no wetnursing </s>

<s> What could I do </s>
<s> I know what I did do </s>
<s> Insensibly I began to keep better hours </s>

<s> Yet he was not straitlaced </s>
<s> And he knew nothing of common Christian morality </s>
<s> All the people on Bora Bora were Christians </s>
