<s> The dipping of them into the melted mass in the kettle </s>
<s> Patience in keeping on dipping them </s>
<s> Pupils taking this course are required to report each morning at five o'clock </s>
<s> 2 </s>
<s> A course in Wax Candles </s>
<s> The use of molds </s>
<s> These departments might give a girl a pretty fair education of the hand and a pretty fair acquaintance with the technique and organization of the working world but we haven't yet mentioned the biggest and hardest department of all </s>
<s> Before mentioning it we call attention to a picture reproduced in this article from a book published in the year 1493 </s>
<s> The book was a French translation of Boccaccio's collection of stories called Noble Women </s>
<s> The picture shows a woolen mill being operated in the grounds of a palace by a queen and her ladiesinwaiting </s>
<s> It summons back the days when even the daughters of kings and nobles could not help acquiring a knowledge of the working world because they were in it </s>
<s> One of the ladies inwaiting is straightening out the tangled strands of wool with cardingcombs </s>
<s> The other has taken the combed and straightened strands and is spinning them into yarn </s>
<s> The queen being the boss has the best job </s>
<s> She is weaving the yarn into cloth on a loom </s>
<s> The daughters of the Emperor Charlemagne who was a very rich man learned how to card and spin and weave </s>
<s> Noble women had to boss all that kind of thing on their estates </s>
<s> They lived in the very midst of Industry of Business </s>
<s> So it was with those early New England women </s>
<s> And therefore whether welltodo or indigent they passed on to their sons as well as to their daughters a steady daily lesson in the world's work </s>
<s> The most intelligent mother in the United States today let her be kindergartner and psychologist and childstudyspecialist as much as she pleases cannot give her children that broad early view of the organization of life </s>
<s> The only place where her children can get it now is in the school </s>
<s> On the first of January of this year Mrs. Ella Flagg Young superintendent of schools in Chicago took algebra out of the eighth grade of the elementary schools and in its place inserted a course on Chicago </s>
<s> Large parts of what was once the Home are now spread out through the Community </s>
<s> The new course will teach the life of the community its activities and opportunities civic aesthetic industrial </s>
<s> Such a course is nothing but Home Training for the enlarged Home </s>
<s> But we must go back for a moment to that biggest and hardest department of all in the old homes of New England </s>
<s> Deceit weeping spinning God hath give To women kindly that they may live said Chaucer in a teasing mood </s>
<s> But spinning was a very small part of the Department of Textiles </s>
<s> We forbear to dilate on the courses of instruction which that department offered </s>
<s> We confine ourselves to observing that First </s>
<s> In the SubDepartment of Flax after heckling that flax with combs of increasing degrees of fineness till the fibers lay pretty straight after spinning it into yarn on her spinningwheel after reeling the yarn off into skeins after bucking the skeins in hot lye through many changes of water and after using shuttle and loom to weave the stuff into cloth the home woman of those days had to accomplish some twenty subsequent processes of bucking rinsing possing drying and bleaching before the cloth was ready for use </s>
<s> Second </s>
<s> In the SubDepartment of Wool in addition to being carders spinners and weavers women were dyers handling all the color resources of the times boiling pokeberries in alum to get a crimson using sassafras for a yellow or an orange and producing a black by boiling the fabric with fieldsorrel and then boiling it again with logwood and copperas </s>
<s> We pass over as trivial the making of flax and wool stuffs into articles of actual use </s>
<s> We say nothing about the transformation of cloth into clothes tablecovers napkins nothing about the weaving of yarn on little lap looms into the narrow fabrics for hairlaces gloveties belts garters and hatbands nothing about the incessant knitting of yarn into mittens and stockings nothing about a host of other details </s>
<s> They were for idle moments </s>
<s> Sweet domestic days when girls stayed at home and helped their mothers and let father support the family </s>
<s> It seems as if even Rip Van Winkle in his most shiftless mood ought to have been able to support a large number of daughters under such conditions </s>
<s> Does it astonish you that they matured young </s>
<s> There all about them from babyhood were the basic processes by which the world was sheltered clothed and fed </s>
<s> Those processes were numerous but simple </s>
<s> Boys and girls observed them absorbed them through eyes through fingertips all through those early years when eyes and fingertips are the nourishing points of the intellect </s>
<s> John Winthrop the first governor of Massachusetts Bay Colony was married at seventeen </s>
<s> His parents were not only willing but aiding and abetting </s>
<s> They considered him a man </s>
<s> Mercy Otis in Revolutionary days in Massachusetts the wife of the patriot James Warren and Abigail Smith the wife of the future president John Adams both married before twenty </s>
<s> A study of their lives will show that at that age they were mature </s>
<s> Today in Boston a woman of twenty is considered so immature that many of the hospitals will not admit her even to her preliminary training for the trade of nurse till she has added at least three years more to her mental development </s>
<s> Who has thus prolonged infancy who has thus postponed maturity </s>
<s> No individual </s>
<s> Science has done part of it </s>
<s> By the invention of powerdriven machines and by the distribution of the compact industries of the home through the scattered innumerable business enterprises of the community Science has given us in place of a simple and near world a complicated and distant one </s>
<s> It takes us longer to learn it </s>
<s> Simultaneously by research and also by the use of the printingpress the locomotive and the telegraph wire which speed up the production as well as the dissemination of knowledge Science has brought forth in every field of human interest and of human value a mass of facts and of principles so enormous and so important that the labors of our predecessors on this planet overwhelm us and we grow to our full physical development long before we have caught up in any degree with the previous experience of the race </s>
<s> And till we have done that to some degree we are not mature </s>
<s> With this postponement of personal maturity there is an even greater postponement of what might be called technical maturity </s>
<s> The real mastery of a real technique takes longer and longer </s>
<s> The teacher must not only go to college but must do graduate work </s>
<s> The young doctor after he finishes college and medical school is found as an interne in hospitals as an assistant to specialists as a traveler through European lecturerooms </s>
<s> The young engineer the young architect the young specialist of every sort finds his period of preparation steadily extending before him </s>
<s> What is left undone by Science in keeping us immature is finally accomplished by System </s>
<s> The world is getting organized </s>
<s> Except in some of the professions and often even in them we most of us start in on our life work at some small subdivided job in a large organization of people </s>
<s> The work of the organization is so systematized as to concentrate responsibility and remuneration toward the top </s>
<s> In time from job to job up an ascent which grows longer as the organization grows bigger we achieve responsibility </s>
<s> Till we do we discharge minor duties for minimum pay </s>
<s> This is just as true of the boy from a middle class family as it is of the boy from a working class family </s>
<s> There follows however a most important difference between them </s>
<s> The middle class boy will have to work longer and go farther than the working class boy in order to rise to the financial standards of his class </s>
<s> In this respect the working class boy will be a man ready for marriage long before his middle class fellowworker </s>
<s> It is among middle class boys then that the period of infancy is most prolonged </s>
<s> They get a good deal of schooling </s>
<s> The stores of human knowledge are put in their hands to some extent and to some extent they catch up with the experience of the race </s>
<s> This takes a longer and longer effort particularly if real mastery of any real technique is attempted </s>
<s> Then on going to work they find that System supplementing Science has perfected such an organization of the world of work that they must stay for quite a while in the ranks of the organization </s>
<s> They will not soon be earning what is regarded among their friends as a marrying income </s>
<s> In money as well as in mind they approach marriage with increasing tardiness </s>
<s> Their prolonged infancy is financial as well as mental </s>
<s> They say that college girls marry late </s>
<s> It is true enough </s>
<s> But it isn't properly stated </s>
<s> The girls in the kind of family which college girls come from marry late </s>
<s> It can be definitively established by statistics here considerately omitted that the age of marriage of college girls is no later than the age of marriage of their noncollege sisters and acquaintances </s>
<s> College is not a cause </s>
<s> It is a symptom </s>
<s> Out of the prolongation of infancy in the middle class has come the conquest by women of the intellectual freedom of the world </s>
<s> It was by no vagary of chance that the demand of women for the higher education came simultaneously with the change from the old industrial home to the new more purely domestic home </s>
<s> It may be a higher nobler type of home </s>
<s> We are not here discussing that point </s>
<s> As the home ceased to provide its daughters with adequate education and with adequate employment what was their situation </s>
<s> In the working class it was simply this That they went into factories and that their sweethearts married them somewhat later than had previously been the case because their share as wives in the support of the family was increasingly smaller </s>
<s> But the working class man soon reaches his maximum earning capacity in his craft and stays there </s>
<s> His financial infancy is short compared with that of the middle class man </s>
<s> He therefore marries younger </s>
<s> In the middle class however Science and System began to lengthen the mental and financial infancy of the men to such an extent that the old maid of twentythree became common </s>
<s> What were the girls in the middle class to do while the boys were growing up to be men in mind and in money </s>
<s> The father of Frederick the Great used to go about his realm with a stick and when he saw a woman in the street he would shake the stick at her and say Go back into the house </s>
<s> An honest woman keeps indoors </s>
<s> Probably quite sensible </s>
<s> When she went indoors she went in to a job </s>
<s> The middle class daughter of today if her mother is living and housekeeping goes indoors into a vacuum </s>
<s> Out of that vacuum came the explosion which created the first woman's colleges </s>
<s> There was plenty of sentiment in the explosion </s>
<s> That was the splendid blinding part of it </s>
<s> That was the part of it which even today makes us veil our eves before the nobility of such women as Emma Willard and Mary Lyon </s>
<s> They made Troy Female Seminary in the twenties and Mount Holyoke in the thirties in the image of the aspirations as well as in the image of the needs of the women of the times </s>
<s> But the needs were there the need to be something the need to do something selfrespecting self supporting </s>
<s> The existence of these needs was clearly revealed in the fact that from the early women's colleges and from the early coeducational universities there at once issued a large supply of teachers </s>
<s> This goes back to the fountainhead of the higher education of women in this country </s>
<s> Emma Willard even before she founded Troy Female Seminary back in the days when she was running her school in Middlebury Connecticut was training young women to TEACH and was acquiring her claim which she herself subsequently urged to being regarded as the organizer of the first normal school in the United States </s>
<s> From that time to this most college women have taught school before getting married </s>
<s> The higher education of women has been in economic effect a trade school for training women for the trade of teacher </s>
<s> But isn't it the purpose of the colleges to avoid training their pupils for specific occupations </s>
<s> Isn't it their purpose to give their pupils discipline and culture pure and broad unaffected by commercial intention </s>
<s> Isn't that what colleges are and ought to be for </s>
<s> On the shore of this vast and violent controversy we discreetly pause and stealthily sidle off taking note of just three reefs of solid fact which unsubmergably jut out above the surface of the raging waters </s>
<s> First </s>
<s> The colleges instruct their pupils in the subjects which those pupils subsequently teach </s>
<s> Second </s>
<s> The pupils specialize in the subjects which they are going to teach </s>
<s> Third </s>
<s> The colleges besides providing the future teachers with subjects almost always offer to provide them with instruction in the principles of education and frequently offer to provide them with instruction in the very technique of classroom work </s>
<s> Our verdict therefore which we hope will be satisfactory to counsel on both sides is that the college is by no means a trade school but that if the woman who is going to earn her living will choose the one trade of teaching she can almost always get a pretty fair trade training by going to college </s>
<s> We are more interested in observing that the amount of trade training which a teacher is expected to take is increasing year by year </s>
<s> In teaching as in other trades the period and scope of preliminary preparation continue to expand </s>
<s> In the last calendar of Bryn Mawr College the Department of Education in announcing its courses makes the following commonsense remarks It is the purpose of the department to offer to students intending to become teachers an opportunity to obtain a technical preparation for their profession </s>
<s> Hitherto practical training has been thought necessary for teachers of primary schools only but similar training is very desirable for teachers in high schools and colleges also </s>
<s> Indeed it is already becoming increasingly difficult for college graduates without practical and theoretical pedagogical knowledge to secure good positions </s>
<s> In addition to the lectures open to undergraduates courses will be organized for graduate students only conducted with special reference to preparation for the headship and superintendence of schools </s>
<s> But the teaching trade is getting choked </s>
<s> There is too much supply </s>
<s> Girls are going to college in hordes </s>
<s> Graduating from college looking for work there is usually just one kind of work toward which they are mentally alert </s>
<s> Their college experience has seldom roused their minds toward any other kind of work </s>
<s> They start to teach </s>
<s> They drug the market </s>
<s> And so the teaching trade the great occupation of unmarried middle class women ceases to be able to provide those women as a class with an adequate field of employment </s>
<s> It is a turning point in the economic history of the class </s>
<s> At the 1909 annual convention of the Association of Collegiate Alumnae in Cincinnati Miss Susan Kingsbury acting for a committee of which Mrs. Richards of the Massachusetts Institute of Technology and Miss Breckenridge of the University of Chicago were members read a real essay on The Economic Efficiency of College Women </s>
<s> This essay was not written till detailed reports on income and expenditure from 377 selfsupporting college graduates had been got together </s>
<s> Out of these 377 there were 317 who were teachers </s>
<s> There were 183 who had followed up their regular college course with from one to eight years of graduate study </s>
<s> The capital invested in education was from 2500 to 3500 and often amounted to 7000 because of advanced work and travel </s>
<s> After all this preparation the average income achieved may be sufficiently disclosed in the one fact that among those graduates who had been at work for from six to eight years more than seventy per cent </s>
<s> were still earning less than 1100 </s>
<s> After drawing a complete statistical picture of the case Miss Kingsbury concluded with certain questions and recommendations here condensed which show the new economic needs of middle class women knocking at the door of present middle class education Should not the oversupply of teachers be reduced by directing many of our graduates into other pursuits than teaching </s>
<s> This will place upon the college just where the responsibility is due the obligation of discovering what those opportunities are and what preparation should be given </s>
<s> This organization should endeavor to arouse in our colleges a sense of responsibility for knowing the facts with regard to their graduates both social and economic and should also endeavor to influence our colleges through appointment secretaries to direct women according to fitness into other lines than teaching </s>
<s> Should not courses be added to the college curriculum to give women the fundamental principles in other professions or lines of industry or commerce than teaching </s>
<s> May not required courses be added to the college curriculum to inculcate business power and sense in all women </s>
<s> This philosophy seems to aim at making the modern school as informative about modern industry as the primitive home was about primitive industry </s>
<s> It seems to be the same educational philosophy which produced the course on Chicago in the Chicago elementary schools which produced the Manhattan Trade School in New York which produced the School of Salesmanship at the Women's Educational and Industrial Union in Boston </s>
<s> At that Women's Educational and Industrial Union at 264 Boylston Street you may see the evolution toward the age of trained women proceeding at all levels of educational equipment </s>
<s> There before you at one level are the Trade School Shopsa shop in handwork and a shop in millinery </s>
<s> The pupils are graduates of the Boston Trade School for Girls </s>
<s> They have had one year of training </s>
<s> They are now taking another </s>
<s> Florence Marshall made the Boston Trade School with a committee of women to help her </s>
<s> It has now been taken over by the public authorities and merged into the publicschool system </s>
<s> What looked like a private fad has become a public function </s>
<s> The training of women for selfsupport has been recognized as a duty of the state </s>
<s> The Trade School Shops at the Women's Educational and Industrial Union were started for the express purpose of supplementing the work of the Boston Trade School for Girls </s>
<s> One year was not enough </s>
<s> In the Trade School the prospective milliner had spent four months on plain sewing four months on summer hats four months on winter hats </s>
<s> She had also taken short courses in Personal Hygiene Business Forms Spelling Business English Color Design Textiles Industrial Conditions </s>
<s> These latter courses were not strictly speaking technical </s>
<s> They were vocational </s>
<s> They were in the middle ground between general and technical training </s>
<s> They went beyond the general training of the elementary schools and furnished the girl with the background of her future vocation </s>
<s> But she often needed a little more of the foreground a little more of actual trade technique </s>
<s> Thus does her education divide itself up into periodsgeneral vocational technical </s>
<s> The Trade School Shops are designed to give the girl her final technical finish </s>
<s> They are really more like a factory than like a school </s>
<s> Although the object of them is to convey a broad instruction the pupil gets wages the stuff she makes is sold and the organization is that of a commercial establishment </s>
<s> So at the end of two years from the time she left the elementary school the young milliner is ready to go out into the world organization </s>
<s> She is better fitted for her world than many a college girl is for hers </s>
<s> On a different level of educational equipment from the Trade School Shops stands the School of Salesmanship </s>
<s> It gets many high school girls and even occasionally a girl who has been to college </s>
<s> Finally there is the Appointment Bureau for college girls in particular </s>
<s> This Appointment Bureau is the most extraordinary employment agency ever organized </s>
<s> Its object is not merely to introduce existing clients to existing jobs which is the proper normal object of employment agencies but to make forays into the wild region of occupations other than teaching and find jobs and then find girls to fit those jobs </s>
<s> In other words it is a kind of Company of Adventurers Trading into Hudson's Bay for the purpose of exploring surveying developing and settling the region of occupations other than teaching on behalf of college women </s>
<s> It is managed by Miss Laura Drake Gill President of the National Association of Collegiate Alumnae and former Dean of Barnard College </s>
<s> She is assisted by an Advisory Council of representatives of nearby collegesRadcliffe Wellesley Simmons Mount Holyoke Smith and Brown </s>
<s> There is no more important work being done for women today </s>
<s> In connection with it the Women's Educational and Industrial Union has just issued a handbook of three hundred pages entitled Vocations for the Trained Woman </s>
<s> It is an immense map of the occupational world for middle class women in which every bay and headland every lake and hill is drawn to scale from Poultry Farming to Department Store Buying from LunchRoom Management to State ChildSaving </s>
<s> The responses made to this movement by certain educational institutions including particularly Simmons College will be observed in a future article </s>
<s> Just one response from an unexpected quarter must be noticed here </s>
<s> In a small Illinois city there is a woman's college founded as a Preparatory School in the forties and soon advanced to be a Seminary which with Anna P </s>
<s> Sill for its first head Jane Addams for its bestknown graduate and Julia Gulliver for its present president has come to be a college of standing and of leading </s>
<s> Only Troy Female Seminary and Mount Holyoke Seminary preceded it in date of foundation among the important women's institutions </s>
<s> Rockford College is ranked today by the reports of the United States Commissioner of Education in rank oneamong the sixteen best women's colleges in the United States </s>
<s> It hasn't risen to that rank by any quick moneyspurred spurt </s>
<s> It brings with it out of its far past all the traditions of that early struggle for the higher education which by friction kindled among women so flaming an enthusiasm for pure knowledge </s>
<s> It remains collegiate in the old sense quiet cloistral inhabiting oldfashioned brick buildings in an oldfashioned large yard looking still like the Illinois of war times more than like the Illinois of the twentieth century retaining all the home ideals of those timesa large interest in feminine accomplishments a strict regard for manners a belief in the value of charm </s>
<s> But here in this quiet nonmetropolitan college so really academic so reallyin the oldestfashioned wayscultural here is a twoyear course in secretarial studies </s>
<s> It is the first time within our knowledge that such a thing has happened in any of the old firstrank women's colleges </s>
<s> The course in secretarial studies at Rockford gives the pupil English Accounts Commerce Commercial Law and Economic History in her first year and Political Science English and Economics in her second year </s>
<s> Shorthand and Typewriting are required in both years and a few hours a week are reserved in each year for elective courses to be chosen by the pupil among offerings in French German Spanish and History </s>
<s> This is a notable concession not only to the increased need of middle class women for occupations other than teaching but also to the increased recognition of those other occupations as being worthy of cultural training </s>
<s> We keep moving forward into an era of trained women as well as trained men </s>
<s> The extraordinary prolongation of mental and financial infancy in the middle class bringing with it an extraordinary postponement of marriage makes this training particularly necessary in the case of the women of that class </s>
<s> But the contraction of the home as a field of adequate employment for daughters exists everywhere increasing the cost of living for the family and driving daughters to supplementing the family income </s>
<s> What futility as well as indignity there is in the idea that the query of support for women gets its full answer in a husband </s>
<s> In the United States in the year 1900 among women twenty years of age and over the married women numbered 13400000 </s>
<s> The unmarried women and the widows together numbered 6900000 </s>
<s> For every two women married there was one woman either single or widowed </s>
<s> If education does not 1 give women a comprehension of the organization of the moneyearning world and 2 train them to one of the techniques which lead to selfsupport in that world it is not education </s>
<s> Just at this point though we encounter a curious conflict in women's education </s>
<s> Just as we see their urgent need of a moneyearning technique we simultaneously hear coming from a corner of the battlefield and swelling till it fills the air with a nationwide battlecry the sentiment The Home is also a technique </s>
<s> All women must be trained to it </s>
<s> At Rockford College illustrating this conflict there exists besides the course in Secretarial Studies an equivalent course in Home Economics </s>
<s> In one photograph in this article we show the tiny children of the Francis Parker School in Chicago taking their first lesson in the technique of the home </s>
<s> In another picture we show the postgraduate laboratory in the technique of the home at the University of Illinois </s>
<s> And the space between the kindergarten and the degree of Doctor of Philosophy threatens to get filled up almost everywhere with courses in cooking sewing chemistry of diet composition of textiles art of marketing and other phases of home management </s>
<s> The moneyearning world a technique </s>
<s> The home a technique </s>
<s> The boy learns only one </s>
<s> Must the girl learn two and be twice a specialist </s>
<s> In the September number Mr. Hard will discuss The Home Economics Movement </s>
<s> VOL. XXIII September 1910 NO </s>
<s> 3 Law and Order By O </s>
<s> HENRY AUTHOR OF THE FOUR MILLION THE HEART OF THE WEST STRICTLY BUSINESS ETC </s>
<s> I found myself in Texas a recently revisiting old places and vistas </s>
<s> At a sheepranch where I had sojourned many years ago I stopped for a week </s>
<s> And as all visitors do I heartily plunged into the business at hand which happened to be that of dipping the sheep </s>
<s> Now this process is so different from ordinary human baptism that it deserves a word of itself </s>
<s> A vast iron cauldron with half the fires of Avernus beneath it is partly filled with water that soon boils furiously </s>
<s> Into that is cast concentrated lye lime and sulphur which is allowed to stew and fume until the witches' broth is strong enough to scorch the third arm of Palladino herself </s>
<s> Then this concentrated brew is mixed in a long deep vat with cubic gallons of hot water and the sheep are caught by their hind legs and flung into the compound </s>
<s> After being thoroughly ducked by means of a forked pole in the hands of a gentleman detailed for that purpose they are allowed to clamber up an incline into a corral and dry or die as the state of their constitutions may decree </s>
<s> If you ever caught an ablebodied twoyearold mutton by the hind legs and felt the 750 volts of kicking that he can send through your arm seventeen times before you can hurl him into the vat you will of course hope that he may die instead of dry </s>
<s> But this is merely to explain why Bud Oakley and I gladly stretched ourselves on the bank of the nearby charco after the dipping glad for the welcome inanition and pure contact with the earth after our muscleracking labors </s>
<s> The flock was a small one and we finished at three in the afternoon so Bud brought from the morral on his saddle horn coffee and a coffeepot and a big hunk of bread and some side bacon </s>
<s> Mr. Mills the ranch owner and my old friend rode away to the ranch with his force of Mexican trabajadores </s>
<s> While the bacon was frizzling nicely there was the sound of horses' hoofs behind us </s>
<s> Bud's sixshooter lay in its scabbard ten feet away from his hand </s>
<s> He paid not the slightest heed to the approaching horseman </s>
<s> This attitude of a Texas ranchman was so different from the oldtime custom that I marveled </s>
<s> Instinctively I turned to inspect the possible foe that menaced us in the rear </s>
<s> I saw a horseman dressed in black who might have been a lawyer or a parson or an undertaker trotting peaceably along the road by the arroyo </s>
<s> Bud noticed my precautionary movement and smiled sarcastically and sorrowfully </s>
<s> You've been away too long said he </s>
<s> You don't need to look around any more when anybody gallops up behind you in this state unless something hits you in the back and even then it's liable to be only a bunch of tracts or a petition to sign against the trusts </s>
<s> I never looked at that hombre that rode by but I'll bet a quart of sheep dip that he's some doubledyed son of a popgun out rounding up prohibition votes </s>
<s> Times have changed Bud said I oracularly </s>
<s> Law and order is the rule now in the South and the Southwest </s>
<s> I caught a cold gleam from Bud's pale blue eyes </s>
<s> Not that I I began hastily </s>
<s> Of course you don't said Bud warmly </s>
<s> You know better </s>
<s> You've lived here before </s>
<s> Law and order you say </s>
<s> Twenty years ago we had 'em here </s>
<s> We only had two or three laws such as against murder before witnesses and being caught stealing horses and voting the Republican ticket </s>
<s> But how is it now </s>
<s> All we get is orders and the laws go out of the state </s>
<s> Them legislators set up there at Austin and don't do nothing but make laws against kerosene oil and schoolbooks being brought into the state </s>
<s> I reckon they was afraid some man would go home some evening after work and light up and get an education and go to work and make laws to repeal aforesaid laws </s>
<s> Me I'm for the old days when law and order meant what they said </s>
<s> A law was a law and a order was a order </s>
<s> But I began </s>
<s> I was going on continued Bud while this coffee is boiling to describe to you a case of genuine law and order that I knew of once in the times when cases was decided in the chambers of a sixshooter instead of a supreme court </s>
<s> You've heard of old Ben Kirkman the cattle king </s>
<s> His ranch run from the Nueces to the Rio Grande </s>
<s> In them days as you know there was cattle barons and cattle kings </s>
<s> The difference was this when a cattleman went to San Antone and bought beer for the newspaper reporters and only give them the number of cattle he actually owned they wrote him up for a baron </s>
<s> When he bought 'em champagne wine and added in the amount of cattle he had stole they called him a king </s>
<s> Luke Summers was one of his range bosses </s>
<s> And down to the king's ranch comes one day a bunch of these Oriental people from New York or Kansas City or thereabouts </s>
<s> Luke was detailed with a squad to ride about with 'em and see that the rattlesnakes got fair warning when they was coming and drive the deer out of their way </s>
<s> Among the bunch was a blackeyed girl that wore a number two shoe </s>
<s> That's all I noticed about her </s>
<s> But Luke must have seen more for he married her one day before the caballard started back and went over on Canada Verde and set up a ranch of his own </s>
<s> I'm skipping over the sentimental stuff on purpose because I never saw or wanted to see any of it </s>
<s> And Luke takes me along with him because we was old friends and I handled cattle to suit him </s>
