<s> VOL. XXIII September 1910 NO </s>
<s> 3 Lassoing Wild Animals In Africa By GUY H </s>
<s> SCULL Field Manager of the Buffalo Jones African Expedition Editor's Note The wild animals of Africa have been hunted with firearms for many a year and photographed by more than one marksman of the lens </s>
<s> But here is the truly unique expedition into the jungle </s>
<s> The idea that any one should seriously contemplate a journey to Africa for the purpose of lassoing such creatures as sportsmen either shoot or photograph at the longest range possible seems quite absurd </s>
<s> But an American frontiersman has done it with American cowboys cowponies and huntingdogs and with wonderful moving pictures to prove it </s>
<s> It is a fine evidence of the sporting qualities of both parties to the undertaking that Colonel C </s>
<s> J </s>
<s> Jones a Western plainsman could so completely interest Mr. Charles S </s>
<s> Bird an Eastern manufacturer in the fantastic plan as to command his backing </s>
<s> And if there is such a thing as the glow of adventure by proxy it must have been felt in the Nassau Street law office where the Buffalo Jones African Expedition had its headquarters when the cablegram from Nairobi announced that lion and rhino had been lassoed and that the moving pictures were a complete success </s>
<s> IT was a special trainloaded to capacity with horses and dogs camp baggage movingpicture cameras cowboys photographers and porters and when it pulled out of the Nairobi station on the way to the up country of British East Africa the period of preparation passed away and the time of action began </s>
<s> As the faces of the people on the platform glided by the window of the slowly moving carriage there was good will written on all of them but also unbelief </s>
<s> There was no doubt as to what they thought of Buffalo Jones's expedition that was setting out to rope and tie and photograph the wild animals of the East African Veldt </s>
<s> How are you going to hold a rhino that weighs two tons and a half </s>
<s> What are you going to do when the lion charges </s>
<s> Such were the questions asked us by the hunters of the country </s>
<s> They further took pains to explain that a rhino charges like a flash and that a lion can catch a horse within a hundred yards </s>
<s> These items of information however were well known to Buffalo Jones before the expedition was organized in New York and his preparations to meet the difficulties had been made accordingly </s>
<s> Colonel C </s>
<s> J </s>
<s> Jones is tall and spare with a strong rugged face and keen blue eyes </s>
<s> During his sixtyfive years of life he has roped and tied often singlehanded every kind of wild animal of consequence to be found in our western country and his experience with these has led him to believe implicitly that man is the master of all wild beasts </s>
<s> He has climbed trees after mountain lions and with a lasso over a branch has hauled grizzlies up into the air by one hind leg </s>
<s> And once he set out alone to journey over a country that no white man had ever traveled before to reach the land of the muskox on the border of the Arctic Circle </s>
<s> The story is told of how he met a trapper on the way and how these two in the face of the hostility of all the Indian tribes the wolves and the cold of the northern winter eventually came to the muskox and captured five calves </s>
<s> Then deserted by their Indian guide they started to return with their prizes got lost in the wilderness and fought the wolves till their cartridges ran out </s>
<s> And when at last they reached safety and fell asleep exhausted the Indians obeying the laws of their religion stole upon them in the night and killed the calves </s>
<s> But the success he had achieved with the mountain lions of the Southwest the muskox of the North and the grizzly bears of the Rockies was not enough </s>
<s> For twenty years it had been the one ambition of his life to take an outfit to British East Africa to try his hand with the more ferocious big game of that country </s>
<s> But in his Western experience Colonel Jones had learned something else besides the mastery of man over beast </s>
<s> Precisely how an American cowboy was going to hold a rhinoceros that weighed two tons and a half was purely a matter of speculation </s>
<s> Yet of one thing the Colonel was certainthe experiment would result in a moving picture that would be well worth the taking </s>
<s> For this reason what afterward came to be known as the picture department was added to the makeup of the expedition </s>
<s> The preparations extended over a considerable length of time and were carried on in various places </s>
<s> Unquestionably the most important part of the outfit was the horses </s>
<s> It was absolutely essential that they should be Western cowponies fast well trained and reliable in every way </s>
<s> The Colonel who best of all could foresee the nature of the work they would have to do selected them himself ten in all from the ranches of New Mexico and shipped them to New York </s>
<s> The American dogs to be used for trailing were likewise chosen by the Colonel </s>
<s> Some of them belonged to him personally and had been thoroughly tried out </s>
<s> The rest had reputations of their own </s>
<s> Of the two cowboys who were to act as his assistants Marshall Loveless had worked with the Colonel before and knew his methods and Ambrose Means came highly recommended for skill and daring from one of the largest ranch owners in the West </s>
<s> When at the last moment the writer of these articles was introduced to the expedition in the capacity of acting field manager the preparations were well under way </s>
<s> The horses and dogs had been already shipped en route to Africa in charge of the cowboys and the date of our sailing for London had been fixed for the following day </s>
<s> The meeting was held at a luncheon in the Railroad Club in New York </s>
<s> There were present Colonel Jones Mr. F </s>
<s> W </s>
<s> Bird son of Charles S </s>
<s> Bird[1] who financed the expedition Mr. W </s>
<s> G </s>
<s> Sewall of the Boma Trading Company of Nairobi and myself </s>
<s> After certain matters of business had been disposed of the talk at the luncheon table drifted to the probabilities and possibilities of success to lions rhinos elands and cheetahs to cowboys horses and dogs </s>
<s> But the Colonel would hear of no possibilities or even probabilities of failure </s>
<s> He was peculiarly insistent upon this point </s>
<s> And when the hour of the business man's lunch time came to an end and the room began to empty Mr. Sewall said to me across the corner of the table Of course every one in Nairobi will think all of you either fakers or crazy </s>
<s> I know you're no fakers </s>
<s> I don't know whether you're crazy or not </s>
<s> But there is one thing in your favor The Colonel's unshaken belief that the thing can be done will probably pull it through </s>
<s> [1] EAST WALPOLE MASS </s>
<s> July 8 1910 </s>
<s> Mr. GUY H </s>
<s> SCULL </s>
<s> MY DEAR SCULL It has been asked by some what the object of the Buffalo Jones African Expedition was </s>
<s> I will tell you </s>
<s> You know my friend Colonel C </s>
<s> J </s>
<s> Jones broke his rifle a generation or so ago and vowed he would never again kill game save for food or in selfdefense </s>
<s> Since taking that oath he has subdued and captured all kinds of wild animals in North America including the muskox buffalo grizzly bear and cougar </s>
<s> I discovered that it was his dream to go to East Africa to prove that with American cowboys horses and dogs he could lasso and capture the savage animals of that country as readily as he has the wild animals of our country </s>
<s> As a sporting proposition it seemed to me unique and fascinating and so as a small tribute to Colonel Jones I volunteered to finance the expedition </s>
<s> I somewhat doubt whether there is another man in the world who has the courage skill and determination to do what he has done in the animal kingdom and he well deserves to be called The Preserver of the American Bison </s>
<s> I want to acknowledge our indebtedness to Mr. Arthur A </s>
<s> Fowler of New York for his assistance in helping us outfit the expedition in London and Nairobi and to you and the others who have helped to make the expedition a success </s>
<s> Very truly CHARLES S </s>
<s> BIRD </s>
<s> On our arrival in London about the middle of January of this year the work of preparation was continued at once </s>
<s> Outside of the minor details of the outfit such as personal equipment saddlery medicines bandages and so forth the first matter to receive attention was the organization of the picture department </s>
<s> Mr. Cherry Kearton was sought to take charge of this branch of the expedition </s>
<s> Keartona powerfully built Yorkshiremanis an experienced cinematograph photographer and a naturalist of no small reputation </s>
<s> He had taken moving pictures in Africa before and so he knew the climatic conditions therethe heat radiation and the different intensities of light </s>
<s> He also knew the animals the Colonel was going to rope </s>
<s> But besides being a cinematograph expert and a naturalist he was also a sportsman </s>
<s> When Kearton learned of the nature of the undertaking he was skeptical </s>
<s> He had no more than a slight acquaintance with the Colonel then and only a vague hearsay knowledge of what the American Cowboy could do </s>
<s> Evidently his mind was divided by the dictates of common sense and the sporting instinct </s>
<s> On many occasions during this time he questioned the feasibility of the experiment in the light of what he knew of the African beasts </s>
<s> The agreement in documentary form was spread out on the table in the Boma Trading Company's London office when he finally wanted to know how in Heaven's name we thought this thing could be done </s>
<s> We'll do it the Colonel said quietly </s>
<s> That was all </s>
<s> Well there's a picture in it anyway said Kearton and signed the papers </s>
<s> With his assistant David Gobbet two cinematograph machines and tripods hand cameras and developing apparatus he set sail immediately for Africa leaving an order for thirty thousand feet of film to be divided between two manufacturers and to be forwarded as soon as possible </s>
<s> In the meantime Colonel Jones was hard at work collecting a rather unusual assortment of articles </s>
<s> The experience of a lifetime enabled him to foresee what kind of materials were absolutely necessary and what kind might prove useful on the present expedition </s>
<s> Naturally the articles required were not usually in stock but the London shopkeeper is proverbially obliging and imperturbable </s>
<s> One rainy morning the Colonel walked into a hardware store and asked to see some handcuffs </s>
<s> A pair was shown him </s>
<s> Not large enough said the Colonel </s>
<s> How large would you want them sir </s>
<s> Twice that size </s>
<s> May I ask for what purpose you require them sir </s>
<s> For lions said the Colonel </s>
<s> Precisely handcuffs for lions yes you need large ones </s>
<s> I am afraid I have none in stock just now but I can have them made for you within a few days </s>
<s> It was the same with almost everything the Colonel wanted to purchase everything had to be made especially for him after his own descriptionhandcuffs collars and belts chains branding irons a block and fall muzzles of different sizes corkscrew picketpins for holding the turn of a rope and a nondescript article shaped like a huge pair of tongs for which I feel sure there is no name in any trade but which looked to be a handy implement for clamping the jaws of a beast </s>
<s> To have these things made according to specifications took time and an endless amount of running about </s>
<s> Besides there was the more ordinary part of the equipment to procure English dogs both foxhounds and terriers horseblankets extra ropes horseshoes and so on </s>
<s> When the last of the expedition sailed from Southampton there were fortyeight pieces of baggage on the list </s>
<s> This last contingent reached Nairobi at noon on March 3 and for the first time then all the members of the expedition met together </s>
<s> Loveless proved to be a man a little below the medium height he held himself very erect walked with quick energetic steps and wore a blond mustache </s>
<s> He made polite inquiries as to our voyage out commented on the hot weather and fully explained the condition of the horses and dogs </s>
<s> Means was taller </s>
<s> He carried his head slightly forward and wore his black hair brushed low down over his forehead </s>
<s> He stood slumped on one hip so that one shoulder also was lower than the other </s>
<s> Please' to meet you he said </s>
<s> On our arrival at Nairobi the first matter to be decided was the district to be worked </s>
<s> The choice lay between the Sotik and the Kapeti Plains </s>
<s> According to the usual batch of contradictory stories in such cases the game was said to be equally plentiful or equally scarce in both districts </s>
<s> Both had been shot over considerably of late and anyhow no one could really tell us where the most game was to be found because as one informant explained the game everywhere shifted so frequently and so fast </s>
<s> But the Sotik and the country approaching itthe Kedong and Rift Valleys and the Mauwere reported to be more or less free from ticks and as the health of the horses was of the gravest importance to us we determined to work this district first </s>
<s> The Colonel and his two cowboys Loveless and Means were ready to start at once </s>
<s> Eight out of the ten horses were in fine condition </s>
<s> With but one exception the dogs had come through safely though all were suffering somewhat from distemper </s>
<s> It was concluded however that they would recover just as rapidly in the open country as they would in Nairobi </s>
<s> Kearton and Gobbet were ready </s>
<s> Kearton had built a dark room in Nairobi because his earlier experience had taught him that the pictures could not be developed with any degree of satisfaction in the field </s>
<s> His four special porters to carry the cameras and tripodsporters he had trained on previous safariswere only waiting for the word to move </s>
<s> Mr. Ray Ulyate the white hunter to the expedition had already gone to Kijabe to prepare his oxwagons against our coming and the Boma Trading Company had engaged a special train to leave Nairobi on the fifth </s>
<s> On the morning of that day we held the customary procession of an outgoing safari down the main street of Nairobi to the waiting train </s>
<s> The Colonel rode first with the assorted pack of dogs at his horse's heels </s>
<s> Then came the cowboys with the led horses then the picture department then the long single line of black porters bringing up the rear </s>
<s> Above the loads on the porters' heads two flags flashed their colors in the sunlightthe stars and stripes and the house flag of the company with the white buffalo skull against the red background and underneath the motto Sapiens qui Vigilat </s>
<s> The night had already fallen black and cold when the special train crested the top of the divide and coasted down grade into Kijabe </s>
<s> The most imposing structure in the place is the railroad station with its red wooden building propped up on piles its tin guesthouse alongside and the neat gravel platform growing a clump of trees </s>
<s> The rest of Kijabe is composed of four other houses the goodsshed an openfaced Indian booth the postoffice and the watertank </s>
<s> Ulvate met us with a lantern for the station lights are dim and we detrained in the face of the high wind that always blows there from sunset to dawn and picketed the horses among the trees of the station platform </s>
<s> Because a large part of the revenue of the country is derived from the visiting hunters a safari is accorded privileges out of the ordinary </s>
<s> So as a matter of course we took possession of the station and camped in the tin guesthouse for the night </s>
<s> The morning came clear and hot and still </s>
<s> The railroad at Kijabe runs along the face of the hills so that the land drops down abruptly to the plains below and you can look away for miles over the Kedong and Rift valleys with the two sentinel extinct volcanoes rising black against the heatblurred sky The floors of the valleys are laid with volcanic ash </s>
<s> But on first appearances the land looks much the same as the regulation veldt or certain parts of our own Western plains </s>
<s> It is only by the fineness of the dust that hangs about the horses' feet and the peculiar quality of the thirst that dries in the throat that you know this is no ordinary soil </s>
<s> The sun was high in the heavens before we finally started from Kijabe and descended the rough road to the level ground with the brakes on the oxwagons squealing harshly and the horses treading silently in the dust </s>
<s> We had planned to camp at Sewell's farm that night </s>
<s> It was only about four hours away but a short trek the first day is always a good rule to follow </s>
<s> It gives every one a chance so to speak to shake down well into the saddle </s>
<s> We had gone but a short distance however when one thing became strikingly apparent Gobbet did not know how to ride </s>
<s> He was mounted on a white African pony that we had found it necessary to add to our string </s>
<s> The pony was stolid lazy and easygaited but Gobbet's unfamiliar attitude toward his mount was unmistakable </s>
<s> Now it is a delicate matter in any country to broach the question of a man's horsemanship but presently Gobbet introduced the subject of his own accord </s>
<s> Of course I can't ride a horse he said </s>
<s> Have never been on one before </s>
<s> When Mr. Kearton spoke to me about coming out here with him he just asked me if I could ride and I told him surely I could ridebut I didn't tell him I meant a bicycle </s>
<s> After all the matter was of no great importance </s>
<s> Gobbet was young and thin and active with sharp black eyes and the work that lay ahead of us would probably teach him to ride in short orderand it did </s>
<s> We had little expectation of finding either a lion or a rhino on that first day's trip </s>
<s> We were traveling on a regular road making a kind of initial march </s>
<s> The fringe of scrub at the beginning of the valley had been left behind some three or four miles when Ulyate suddenly reined in his horse and pointed to three black dots on the veldt about half a mile away </s>
<s> The black dots proved to he only warthogs but we wanted them and so long as there was little chance of our finding any of the more important species of game we took the opportunity that offered </s>
<s> The Colonel and the two cowboys tightened their cinches and then rode out to the westward to round up the beasts </s>
<s> Drive 'em back to us Kearton called after them and Means waved his hand by way of answer </s>
<s> Behind us the line of porters was coming up along the road </s>
<s> They were straggling badly broken up into little sections of threes and fours so that the last of them were not yet in sight </s>
<s> Gobbet was sent back to hurry forward the four special porters with the cameras and when these finally arrived upon the scene their faces covered with dust and sweat the horsemen had dwindled to dots only a little larger than the hogs themselves </s>
<s> Kearton placed the cameras a few yards apart and there we waited watching the distant specks </s>
<s> Two of the riders disappeared into a far patch of scrub </s>
<s> The third began swinging to the southward </s>
<s> His horse was galloping after something we could not see </s>
<s> In the meantime the safari was coming up and as each section arrived it was halted and the porters put down their loads and sat on them </s>
<s> Some of them turned their backs upon the scene in total indifference as to what was coming next others regarded the cameras with expressions of mild curiosity </s>
<s> Little by little the third horseman had swung round so that he was headed due east riding straight at us </s>
<s> Rapidly the speck grew larger and the two other riders came out of the scrub and joined the chase </s>
<s> Nearer and nearer they came with the dust cloud swirling behind them </s>
<s> Gobbet began turning the handle of his camera and the whir of the machine sounded loud in the stillness </s>
<s> One or two of the porters jumped to their feet and pointed </s>
<s> Kearton waited </s>
<s> I hope they won't come straight into the lens he said </s>
<s> If they do it won't make a good picture </s>
<s> They ought to come at an angle </s>
<s> So he explained placing his hand obliquely to the line of focus </s>
<s> Then he bent over laid his eye to the gunsight of the machine and likewise began turning </s>
<s> The thunder of the chase could be heard now and we could see that it was Loveless leading on his black with Means and the Colonel close behind and the warthog some forty yards ahead </s>
<s> The beast was running strong </s>
<s> His huge snout was thrust forward and his upturned tusks gleamed in the sunlight </s>
<s> But gradually the black horse gained on him and Loveless loosened the rope from his saddle and began swinging the long noose round and round his head </s>
<s> On came the warthog straight for Kearton's camera </s>
<s> Kearton straightened up above the machine and waved his helmet frantically </s>
<s> Give over give over </s>
<s> he shouted </s>
<s> You're driving him right into the picture </s>
<s> It's no good </s>
<s> Give over </s>
<s> The chase never swerved an inch and Kearton bent to his work again cursing in wellselected periods </s>
<s> The next moment the hog drove past him </s>
<s> At the same instant Loveless threw his rope and caught the beast by one hind leg </s>
<s> The black horse stopped fore feet planted firmly and the dust cloud swept across and hid the scene </s>
<s> When the dust cleared away the hog was lying across the road blowing comfortably with the rope leading from his hind leg to the horn of Loveless' saddle </s>
<s> Loveless laughed </s>
<s> There's the first one for you he said </s>
<s> And my can't he run </s>
<s> Gobbet however was indignant </s>
<s> It's no use he complained </s>
<s> To bring an object that way straight into the lens is against the first principles of cinematography </s>
<s> It's no use I tell you </s>
<s> Means sat half slumped in his saddle with his reeking horse panting heavily </s>
<s> Well well well he finally drawled </s>
<s> And didn't Mr. Pig come abending across that prairie </s>
<s> He most certainly come abending </s>
<s> The porters gathered around and looked long at the beast some of them spoke a few words in low tones and the others nodded their heads and smiled </s>
<s> Sometimes a warthog will act nasty and his lower tusks are sharp as razors but when this one was released he walked out of the circle of grinning natives slowly quietly and apparently thoroughly disgusted </s>
<s> At Sewell's farm there is a pan of water made by a dam across an almost waterless brook and alongside of this pan we pitched our camp </s>
<s> When the sun set the high wind rose again whirling up the dust in heavy clouds and sending the sparks from the fire scurrying over the ground </s>
<s> But the Kedong Valley wind is more or less a phenomenon of the country </s>
<s> You can count upon it absolutely for every one of its disagreeable qualities </s>
<s> I think the citizens of Africa are a little proud of it </s>
<s> There was now a fair chance that on our way into the Rift Valley we should flush one or another of the larger animals </s>
<s> Preparations for such a contingency were accordingly made before starting from Sewell's farm </s>
<s> Canteens and iron drums were filled with water because the next camp would be a dry one </s>
<s> The cinematograph cameras and all the extra boxes were loaded with films the evening before and the four special camera porters were given strict orders to keep well up with the advance of the safari </s>
<s> The liontaming outfitthe tongs muzzles chains and collarswas stowed on the first wagon on top of the load where it could be got at readily in case of need </s>
<s> The Colonel rode ahead with the two cowboys close behind all three ropers mounted on their best horsesthe Colonel on the paint Loveless on his black and Means on the bigboned bay </s>
<s> Every member of the party was especially cautioned to keep a sharp lookout on both sides of the road </s>
<s> Just as the day before the morning came hot and still and for hour after hour the straggling safari crawled slowly over the long waves of the undulating veldt </s>
<s> The road was a wagon track always vanishing in front toward the head of the valley </s>
<s> The land lay silent beneath the glaring sunlight </s>
<s> We outspanned at noon for an hour </s>
<s> Over the country here grew small scattered thorn trees thick with thorns but with scarcely any leaves so that the shade beneath them was thin and could shelter no more than one horse </s>
<s> The water in the canteens cold at the start had become warm now </s>
<s> When we mounted again the sweat had dried on the horses and the boots felt stiff on our feet </s>
<s> The line of the road still stretched away its interminable length until it disappeared in the distance </s>
<s> And then as we crawled sleepily ahead over the rises the Colonel was the first to notice the lion spoor in the dust </s>
<s> With sudden animation the safari awoke from the lethargy of the hot monotonous march </s>
<s> The spoor was judged to be at least four hours old so there was no use putting the dogs on it </s>
<s> Then presently it disappeared </s>
<s> On the dead grass of the bordering veldt there was nothing to show which way the lion had gone </s>
<s> But there was a chancea small one yet still a chancethat the beast was lying up near by in the shade of a thorn tree </s>
<s> So all the horsemen spread out over the veldt to obtain a wider scope of vision and for mile after mile the company moved forward sweeping the immediate country </s>
<s> Proceeding in this manner through the afternoon we eventually crested a slightly higher rise and looked down into a shallow valley that was greener than the rest of the veldt </s>
<s> A few fullsized trees were growing in the bottom and there were a number of outcroppings of rock </s>
<s> Large herds of antelope were grazing there </s>
<s> The Colonel called a halt </s>
<s> There is no lion anywhere hereabouts he said because the game are grazing peacefully </s>
<s> But there is a bunch of eland yonder </s>
<s> We might as well round them up while the light lasts </s>
<s> The plan of operation was quickly made </s>
<s> The cameras were stationed about a mile to the southeast partly concealed by the bole of a tree and the bunch of eland were skillfully rounded up and a good specimen was singled out </s>
<s> Everything was working to perfection </s>
<s> The three horsemen drove the eland toward the camerasnot directly at them but a little to one side at an angle as Kearton wanted it done </s>
<s> At the proper moment Loveless roped the animal by the forelegs and neck and threw it down </s>
<s> Loveless jumped from his horse and was running forward to tie the prize when somethingthe smell of the strange beast perhapsstarted the black horse bucking </s>
<s> With the rope made fast to the saddle and the eland acting as a pivot the black went careering round and round </s>
<s> Both the Colonel and Means tried to rope him and missed and finally Loveless on foot caught him by the dangling reins </s>
<s> Of course such a thing might have been readily foreseen but somehow it came as a surprise and opened up grave possibilities </s>
<s> That night in camp at Rugged Rocks we were gathered about the cook s fire for the warmth it gave when the Colonel spoke of the affair </s>
<s> Everything was going great till that horse started bucking the Colonel remarked </s>
<s> We've got to teach our horses not to mind the smell of these strange animals out here </s>
<s> We've got to be able to depend absolutely on our horses </s>
<s> Of course that eland wasn't dangerous </s>
<s> But when we tackle something else and a horse acts that way it might be bad </s>
<s> But Gobbet said it was good action anyway and would look fine when thrown on the screen </s>
<s> March 8 was a day of disappointments </s>
<s> Between sunrise and sunset we traveled fifteen miles to the Wangai River and hunted in turn a pair of lions a cheetah and a rhinocerosand lost them all </s>
<s> Two circumstances were held accountable one was the necessity of getting the horses to water and the other was the fact that it was just a bad luck day all through </s>
<s> We came upon the lions early in the morning close to the base of the southern volcano </s>
<s> This particular pair of lions must have been shot over at one time or another for they did not wait to satisfy any curiosity as to our intentions but fled at once for the safety of the mountain </s>
<s> Although we gave chase immediately their lead was so great and the distance to the mountains so short that they were soon lost to us in the gullies and crevices of the foothills </s>
<s> It was while we were trying to pick up the lost trail of the lions that we flushed a cheetah out of one of the dongas.[2] It broke away along the foothills and finally stopped at bay in a district where the going was so bad for the horses that we had to give up the attempt </s>
<s> [2] Donga.a gully </s>
<s> With the rhinoceros we had scarcely any chance whatsoever </s>
<s> The Colonel who was scouting the country to the northward of the line of march caught a glimpse of the beast in the adjacent valley </s>
<s> By the time he had come back to get us and we had ridden in pursuit the rhino had disappeared </s>
<s> We found his trail leading still farther to the northward and dismounted and looked down at it in silence </s>
<s> No comments were made </s>
<s> No comments were necessary </s>
<s> Every one knew that for lack of water the horses were too done up to follow </s>
<s> Means had dismounted a little to one side of the group and for a while he stood there with his arms resting on his saddle gazing back over the way we had come </s>
<s> Presently he remarked to the world at large Excitement has certainly been runnin' high all day </s>
<s> We mounted then and instead of hunting the rhino farther we rode the jaded horses slowly into camp and put a proper finish to a bad luck day by holding a consultation </s>
<s> The Wangai River is no river at all merely a small spring in the shadow of the range that crosses the head of the valley </s>
<s> But the spring could supply sufficient water for all our needs </s>
<s> Also the problem of transportation demanded that Ulyate should return to Kijabe and bring up another wagon with supplies before the journey over the Mau into the Sotik could be undertaken </s>
<s> Then too here in the Rift Valley we had seen both lion and rhino and there was always the chance of finding them again </s>
<s> The consultation resulted in the decision to make a permanent camp here and hunt the neighboring country until Ulyate should return </s>
<s> For the succeeding three days the Colonel laid out a plan of campaign simple but effective and limited only by the necessity of keeping within reasonable distance of the water </s>
<s> The plan consisted of a series of drives one in a northeasterly one in an easterly and one in a southeasterly direction </s>
<s> By this means we would cover in turn all the territory at the head of the valley </s>
<s> The Colonel was anxious to try again for the rhino he had seen on the march the day before and for this reason the drive to the northeast was inaugurated first </s>
<s> Every member of the expedition took part in these drives </s>
<s> The Colonel and the writer at one end and the two cowboys at the other occupied the extreme positions </s>
<s> Between the right and left wings stretched a long line of porters under the command of two escaris and with Kearton and Gobbet in the center with the cameras </s>
<s> The dogs on leash and the saises carrying water for the horses brought up the rear </s>
<s> When finally formed the line of the drive extended approximately five miles and the cameras and the dogs were so placed that they could be brought to either end of the line with the utmost despatch </s>
<s> Two shots fired in quick succession would be the signal to gather </s>
<s> That first day's drive brought little success </s>
<s> To begin with we were late in starting so that the sun had already risen before we moved out of camp and besides the porters were new at that kind of work and had to be halted and reformed many times before they understood what was wanted </s>
<s> The land across which we were driving lay at the very edge of the valley and was consequently somewhat broken into small hills and hollows </s>
<s> By the time we came to the old rhino trail the day was well advanced </s>
<s> But no fresh tracks were to be found up and down the entire length of the hollow nor was anything to be seen of the beast from the next hill to the northward which we climbed to search the country ahead </s>
<s> There was only a large herd of hartebeests grazing on the plains below </s>
<s> The Colonel retreated halfway down the hill and fired two shots from his revolver </s>
<s> Somewhere beyond our range of vision we heard the two shots repeated and at the end of a little more than half an hour all the members of the drive were gathered on the hillside below the crest </s>
<s> Then the Colonel explained the reason for his signal </s>
<s> The rhino was not there </s>
<s> We might still find him and we might not </s>
<s> The chances were now that we should not </s>
<s> He had probably left the country for good and was already miles away </s>
<s> In the meanwhile a good opportunity offered for rounding up the herd of hartebeests in the plain below and driving them up the hillside to the cameras </s>
<s> On top of the hill was a small clearing the edges of which were fringed with scrub </s>
<s> While the Colonel and the cowboys maneuvered to circle the herd Kearton placed the cameras in the clearing with the northern line of scrub as a background for the intended picture </s>
<s> For a long time there was silence </s>
<s> Then suddenly the scrub sprang into life and the next instant the herd dashed into the clearing in a cloud of dust that was pierced by a hundred startled eyes and tossing horns </s>
<s> At the sight of the cameras the herd broke and scattered in every direction but the horsemen pressing them close roped one in the open and held him to have his picture taken and then let him go </s>
<s> On the second drive over the lowlands to the east the porters worked better but although we covered a far greater territory the total result was the roping and photographing of a servalcat that we flushed on the way back to camp </s>
<s> The third drive carried us well out toward the southern volcano where we had seen the lions on the march from Rugged Rocks but this time there was no trace of them anywhere in the land </s>
<s> Means however found a cheetah and the two faint reports of his signal brought us together on the run </s>
<s> We came upon Means seated on his horse in a bit of the veldt that was covered all over with tufts of rank grass so that it looked like a swamp that had been dry for ages </s>
<s> Near by ran a small shallow donga </s>
<s> When the rest of us rode up to him he merely pointed at one of the tufts of grass behind which the cheetah lay crouched </s>
<s> There followed a brief delay while a plan of maneuver was made and expounded while the tripods were set up the cameras screwed on and the ropers moved out to their appointed places </s>
<s> Then all at once the cheetah started and instead of breaking away as we had calculated he would he doubled on his tracks and made for the shelter of the donga </s>
<s> It was a quick sharp raceand the cheetah won </s>
<s> He hid in the scrub at the bottom of the ditch </s>
<s> The native porters collected there and complacently regarded the scene and the members of the drive ranged themselves on either bank and offered innumerable suggestions as to what had better be done next </s>
<s> But in the midst of it all the Colonel put an emphatic end to the discussion </s>
<s> He rode into the donga with his rope swinging free and when the cheetah failed to spring at him he dropped the noose over the animal's head and dragged him out on to the open veldt where his picture could be properly taken </s>
<s> The black porters looking on commenced speaking in low tones in their native tongue and nodded and grinned at each other as they had done before </s>
<s> But this time Mac was among them </s>
<s> Mac was Kearton's tentboy </s>
<s> He originally came from Somaliland and spoke English </s>
<s> He was called upon to explain what the porters said </s>
<s> Please he began </s>
<s> They are very bad men these people but don't be sorry </s>
<s> They saythey say that of course the white gentlemen are able to do what they want to do but just the same they are all crazy </s>
<s> That night we held our second consultation </s>
<s> Ulyate had returned from Kijabe with the extra wagonload of supplies which placed us in a position to move again immediately </s>
<s> The question now arose as to whether it would be best to remain where we were a few days longer to gain more experience or to trek at once over the Mau with a chance at giraffe on the way and so on into the Sotik country with its alluring promises of both rhino and lion </s>
<s> By this time we had hunted the Rift Valley thoroughly </s>
<s> During the seven days since we had left Kijabe the expedition had roped and photographed a cheetah a servalcat a hartebeest an eland and a warthog </s>
<s> Although we had been given no opportunity yet to find out how we were going to hold a rhino or what we would do when the lion charged still in addition to our success with the lesser animals we had acquired something else of value </s>
<s> All the members of the expedition had learned to work well togetherin all the usual emergencies each man knew what was expected of him and could likewise make a ready guess as to what the others intended doing </s>
<s> Thus in spite of the fact that on an expedition of this kind it is the unexpected that always happens our experience only added to our confidence that when we eventually encountered one of the larger beasts we should get him </s>
<s> The consultation ended with the unanimous decision to start for the Sotik at dawn </s>
<s> In the October number Mr. Scull will relate the adventures of the Buffalo Jones African Expedition in Lassoing Giraffe and Rhinoceros </s>
<s> VOL. XXIII September 1910 NO </s>
<s> 3 THE WOMEN OF TOMORROW page 368379 part 2 </s>
<s> By WILLIAM HARD II THIS IS A VERY IMPORTANT SUBJECT </s>
<s> Dear General Reader please let that sentence stand for the thousand words much like those of a competent barker at the door of a showtent which you usually oblige an author to expend on enticing you into reading his article </s>
<s> Think how much time you save by walking straight into the tent and observing that THE First International Congress on Domestic Science and Arts was held in 1908 at Freiburg in Switzerland </s>
<s> It as no improvised amateur uplift privatetheatricals affair </s>
<s> The head of the organizing committee was M. Python president of Freiburg's State Council </s>
<s> Seventytwo papers on technical topics were printed and circulated beforehand </s>
<s> The participating members numbered seven hundred </s>
<s> The discussions developed the characteristic points of the three rival breeds of householdarts instructionthe German the Swiss and the Belgian </s>
<s> Visits were made to the normal schools of Freiburg Berne and Zurich in each of which there is an elaborate system for the training of householdarts teachers </s>
<s> In the end in order that facts and ideas about the education of girls for their duties as housekeepers might be more rapidly circulated it was voted to establish at some place in Switzerland a Permanent International Information Committee </s>
<s> Thus in an age in which the productive tasks of the home have almost all been surrendered to the factory in an age in which even cooking and sewing last puny provinces of a once ample empire are forever making concessions of territory to those barbarian invaders the manufacturers of readytoeat foods and readytowear clothes in an age in which home industry lies fainting and gasping while Mrs. Charlotte Perkins Gilman begs the spectators to say thumbsdown and let her put it out of its agony altogetherin such an age there comes at Freiburg in this First International Congress on Domestic Science and Arts the most serious the most notable recognition </s>
<s> ever given in any age to the home's economic value </s>
<s> A real paradox </s>
<s> Well at any rate it gives wings to the fluttering thought that theories of industrial evolution one's own as well as Mrs. Gilman's are a bit like automobilesnot always all that they are cranked up to be </s>
<s> Certainly the revival of the home seems to attract larger crowds to the mourners' bench every year </s>
<s> At the University of Missouri the first crop of graduates in Home Economics was gathered this last spring </s>
<s> They were seven </s>
<s> And as most of them took likewise a degree in Education it may be assumed that they will go forth to spread the gospel </s>
<s> Their preceptress Miss Edna D </s>
<s> Day who next year will head the justorganized Department of Home Economics in the University of Kansas is a novel type of new woman in that she has earned the degree of Doctor of Philosophy in Woman's Sphere </s>
<s> She took graduate work in the Department of Home Administration in the University of Chicago and achieved her doctorate with an investigation into The Effect of Cooling on the Digestibility of Starch </s>
<s> What she found out was subsequently printed as a bulletin by the United States Department of Agriculture </s>
<s> In the midst of the festivities at the wake held over The Home it perplexes the mourners to learn that some of those domestic science bulletins of the United States Department of Agriculture excite a demand for a million copies </s>
<s> It is a wake like Mike McCarthy's </s>
<s> Mike was lookin' iligant As he rested there in state </s>
<s> But When the fun was at its height McCarthy sat up straight </s>
<s> The ballad one of the most temperately worded of literary successes goes on to say that the effect was great </s>
<s> So it has been in this casegreat enough to be felt all the way around the world </s>
<s> It is being felt in the Island Empire of the East </s>
<s> Miss Ume Tsuda's Institute at Tokyo which stands so high that its graduates are allowed to teach in secondary schools without further government examination has installed courses in English domestic science as well as in the domestic science of Japan </s>
<s> It is being felt in the Island Empire of the West </s>
<s> King's College of the University of London has organized a threeyear course leading to the degree of Mistress of Home Science and has also established a PostGraduates' Course in Home Science in which out of fourteen students in this its first year of existence four are graduates of the courses of academic study of Oxford or Cambridge </s>
<s> It is being felt in the United States at every educational level </s>
<s> It has familiarized us with household arts in the public schools and we are not astonished to learn that in the public schools of Boston in every grade above the third there is sewing or cooking or both for 120 minutes every week for every girl </s>
<s> It has accustomed us to such news as that in Illinois there are fiftyeight public high schools in which instruction is offered in one or more of the three following subjects Food Clothing or The Home </s>
<s> It has brought us to the point of expecting domestic science in all schools of agriculture and of regarding it as natural for the legislature of Montana to appropriate 50000 to the State Agricultural College for a woman's dormitory </s>
<s> It has cushioned the shock of the tidings from the University of California to the effect that entrance credit will this fall be given for high school domestic science work </s>
<s> We are reduced to equanimity in the face of the fact which might have frenzied Alexander Hamilton that Columbia University through its Teachers College is offering courses in Elementary Cookery in Shirtwaists in Domestic Laundering and in Housewifery </s>
<s> And at last when we see the resuscitated home making its way even into the reallytruly morethanmasculinely academic Eastern women's colleges we rush up to the Mike McCarthy of this case and assure him warmly that we were not deceived for a moment by his apparent demise having just learned that President Hazard of Wellesley College in her latest commencement address said I hope the time may soon come when we can have a department of domestic science which shall give a sound basis for the problems of the household What does it all mean </s>
<s> FellowCitizens said the colored orator reported by Dr. Paul Monroe of Columbia what am education </s>
<s> Education am the palladium of our liberties and the grand pandemonium of civilization </s>
<s> But it does mean something this Home Economics disturbance </s>
<s> AND SOMETHING VERY DIFFERENT FROM WHAT IT SEEMS TO </s>
<s> II Mr. Edward T </s>
<s> Devine </s>
<s> of the New York Charity Organization Society has distinguished himself in the field of economic thought as well as in the field of active social reform </s>
<s> Among his works is a minute but momentous treatise on The Economic Function of Women </s>
<s> It is really a plea for the proposition that today the art of consuming wealth is just as important a study as the art of producing it </s>
<s> If acquisition says Mr. Devine has been the idea which in the past history of economics has been unduly emphasized expenditure is the idea which the future history of the science will place beside it </s>
<s> We have used our brains while getting hold of money </s>
<s> We are going to use our brains while getting rid of it </s>
<s> We have studied banking engineering shop practice cost systems salesmanship </s>
<s> We are going to study food values the hygiene of clothing the sanitary construction and operation of living quarters the mental reaction of amusements the distribution of income the art of making choices according to our means from among the millions of things harmful and helpful ugly and beautiful offered to us by the producing world </s>
<s> Mr. Devine ventures to hope that we may look for a radical improvement in general economic conditions from a wiser use of the wealth which we have chosen to produce </s>
<s> This enlarged view of the economic importance of Consumption brings with it a correspondingly enlarged view of the economic importance of the Home </s>
<s> If the Factory says Mr. Devine has been the center of the economics which has had to do with production the Home will displace the Factory as the center of interest in a system which gives due prominence to Enjoyment and Use </s>
<s> There will result continues Mr. Devine an increased respect on the part of economists for the industrial function which woman performs for there is no economic function higher than that of determining how wealth shall be used so that even if man remain the chief producer of wealth and woman remain the chief factor in determining how wealth shall be used the economic position of woman will not be considered by those who judge with discrimination to be inferior to that of man </s>
<s> Mr. Devine then lays out for the economist a task in the discharge of which the innocent bystander will sincerely wish him a pleasant trip and a safe return </s>
<s> It is the present duty of the economist says Mr. Devine to accompany the wealth expender to the very threshold of the home that he may point out with untiring vigilance its emptiness caused not so much by lack of income as by lack of knowledge of how to spend wisely </s>
<s> Mr. Deville's proposition therefore would seem finally to sanction some such conclusion as this Physical science and social science and common sense are making such important contributions to the subject of the rearing of children and to the subject of the maintenance of wholesome and beautiful living conditions and to the subject of the use of leisure that while the home woman has lost almost all of the productive industries which she once controlled she has simultaneously gained a whole new field of labor </s>
<s> Consumption has ceased to be merely PASSIVE and has become ACTIVE </s>
<s> It has ceased to be mere ABSORPTION and has become CHOICE </s>
<s> And the active choosing of the products of the world both spiritual and material in connection with her children her house and her spare time has developed for the home woman into a task so broad into an art so difficult as to require serious study </s>
<s> We have quoted at length from Mr. Devine's discourse because it is recognized as the classic statement of the case and because it is warmly commended by such women as Mrs. Ellen H </s>
<s> Richards of the Massachusetts Institute of Technology whose skill as scientist and vision as philosopher have made her the most authoritative personality in the American Home Economics Association </s>
<s> That association by the way has some fifteen hundred duepaying members </s>
<s> The scales fall from our eyes now and we see at least one thing which we had not seen before </s>
<s> We had supposed that sewing and cooking were the vitals of the Home Economics movement </s>
<s> Not at all </s>
<s> The home woman might cease altogether to sew and to cook just as she has ceased altogether to spin weave brew etc </s>
<s> without depriving the Home Economics movement of any considerable part of its driving power </s>
<s> Sewing and cooking are productive processes </s>
<s> They add economic value to certain commodities namely cloth and food </s>
<s> But it is not Production it is Consumption which the Home Economics movement is at heart devoted to </s>
<s> This is plainly set forth by some of its most zealous workers </s>
<s> Thus Edna D </s>
<s> Day at the Lake Placid Conference on Home Economics in 1908 was more or less sorry that domestic science has come to be so largely sewing and cooking in our schools was quite willing to look at the white of the eye of the fact that more and more we are buying readymade clothes and readycooked foods and marked out the policy of her Survey Course in Home Economics at the University of Missouri in the statement that sewing and cooking are decreasingly home problems while the problems of wise buying of adjusting standards of living to income and of developing right feelings in regard to family responsibilities are increasingly difficult </s>
<s> To choose and use the world's resources intelligently on behalf of family and communityin this Mr. Devine sees a new field of action in this Mrs. Richards sees a new field of education </s>
<s> Women will train themselves for their duties as consumers or else continue to lie under the sentence of condemnation pronounced upon them by Florence Nightingale </s>
<s> Threefourths of the mischief in women's lives said she arises from their excepting themselves from the rule of training considered necessary for men </s>
<s> But what in this case is the training proposed </s>
<s> The answer to that question will cause some more scales to fall from our eyes </s>
<s> Just as we have seen that Home Economics does not consist essentially of sewing and cooking we shall see that Consumption is not at all a specialized technique in the sense in which electrical engineering department store buying railroading cotton manufacturing medicine and the other occupations of the outside world are specialized technigues </s>
<s> Home Economics will not narrow women's education but in the end will enlarge it because Consumption instead of being a specialty is a generality so broad as almost to glitter </s>
<s> III AT Menomonie Wisconsin Mr. L </s>
<s> D </s>
<s> Harvey lately president of the National Education Association has established a Homemakers' School </s>
<s> It does not turn out teachers </s>
<s> Its course of instruction is solely for the prospective housewife </s>
<s> The first grand division of study is The House </s>
<s> We here observe that the housewife is going to be something of a Sanitary Engineer since she studies Chemistry Physics and Bacteriology in their application to such subjects as the heating lighting ventilation and plumbing of a house </s>
<s> It is thought that knowledge of this sort will go a long way toward improving the health conditions of the country </s>
<s> We also observe that the housewife is going to be something of an Interior Decorator since she studies design color house planning and furnishing </s>
<s> She also acquires some skill as Purchasing Agent Bookkeeper and Employer of Labor when she takes the course on Household Management and studies the proper apportioning of income among the different lines of home expenditures the systematizing and keeping of household accounts and the question of domestic service </s>
<s> The second grand division is Food Study and Preparation </s>
<s> Here the housewife becomes to some extent a Dietitian studying the chemical processes in the preparation and digestion of foods and considering the question how she shall secure for the family the foods best suited to the various activities of each individual </s>
<s> Here likewise she makes a start toward being a Pure Food Expert through a study of physical and chemical changes induced in food products by the growth of molds yeasts and bacteria and a start toward being a Health Officer through a study of bacteria in their relation to disease sources of infection personal and household disinfection </s>
<s> Nor does she omit to acquire some of the technique of the Physical Director through a course in Physiology bearing on digestion storage of energy rest sleep exercise and regularity of habits </s>
<s> Of course in her work in cookery she pays some attention to special cookery for invalids </s>
<s> The third grand division that of Clothing and Household Fabrics produces a Dressmaker a Milliner and an Embroiderer as well as a person trained to see to it that the expenditure for clothing shall be correct in proportion to the expenditure for other purposes </s>
<s> The fourth grand division the Care of Children is of course limitless </s>
<s> The rearing of the human young is as we all know and as Mr. Eliot of Harvard has insisted the most intellectual occupation in the world </s>
<s> Here the homemaker applies all the knowledge she has gained from her study of the hygiene of foods and of the hygiene of clothes and also makes some progress toward becoming a Trained Nurse and a Kindergartner by means of researches into infant diseases and emergencies the stages of the mental development of the child the child's imagination with regard to truthtelling and deceit the history of children's books and the art of storytelling </s>
<s> Passing over the fifth grand division Home Nursing and Emergencies in which the pupil learns simply the use of household remedies the care of the sickroom etc </s>
<s> we come to the wide expanse of the sixth grand division Home and Social Economics </s>
<s> The work in this division begins with a study of the primitive evolution of the home and comes on down to the present time when the passing of many of the former lines of woman's work into the factory has brought to many women leisure time which should be spent in social service </s>
<s> Note that last fact carefully </s>
<s> Home Economics is no attempt to drive women back into home seclusion </s>
<s> On the contrary it is an attempt to bring the home and its occupants into the scientific and sociological developments of the outside world </s>
<s> For this reason in traversing the division of Home and Social Economics the pupil encounters an attempt to determine problems in civic life which seem to be a part of the duties of women </s>
<s> Seventhly and lastly there is a division dedicated to Literature in which a systematic course in reading is carried on through the two years </s>
<s> Indispensable </s>
<s> No degree of proficiency at inserting calories in correct numbers in to Little Sally's stomach could atone for lack of skill at leading Little Sally herself in morning strolls through the Child's Garden of Verses with trowel in hand to dig up the gayest plants and reset them in the memory </s>
<s> Which brings us back to the observation that the Consumption of Wealth is a generality </s>
<s> The homemaker may happen to be a specialist in some one direction but it is clear that she cannot simultaneously know as much about food values as the real dietitian as much about the physical care of her child as the real trained nurse as much about the wholesomeness of her living arrangements as the real sanitarian as much about music as the Thomas Orchestra as much about social service as Mr. Devine and as much about poems as Mr. Stevenson </s>
<s> Her peculiar equipment if she is a good homemaker is a round of experience and a bent of mind which make it possible for her to cooperate intelligently with the dietitian the trained nurse the sanitarian the Thomas Orchestra Mr. Devine Mr. Stevenson and the various other representatives of the various other specialized techniques of the outside world </s>
<s> It follows that her school discipline cannot be too comprehensive </s>
<s> No other occupation demands such breadth of sense and sensibility </s>
<s> One could make a perfectly good cotton manufacturer on the basis of a very narrow training </s>
<s> One cannot make a good consumer without a really LIBERAL EDUCATION </s>
<s> For this reason it becomes necessary to resist certain narrownesses in certain phases of Home Economics </s>
<s> One of these narrownesses is the assumption that because a thing happens to be close to us it is therefore important </s>
<s> We have heard lecturers insist that because a house contains drainpipes a woman should learn all about drainpipes </s>
<s> But why </s>
<s> In most communities drainpipes are installed and repaired and in every way controlled by gentlemen who are drainpipe specialists </s>
<s> The woman who lives in the house has no more real need of a knowledge of the structural mysteries of drainpipes than a reporter has of a knowledge of the structural mysteries of his typewriting machine </s>
<s> The office mechanic fixes all that for him and so far as his efficiency as a reporter is concerned an investigation of his faithful keyboard's internal arrangements would be in most cases an amiable waste of time </s>
<s> Another possible narrowness is the attempt to manufacture cultural backgrounds for various important but quite safeandsane household tasks </s>
<s> For instance in the books and in the courses of instruction of college grade on The House we have sometimes observed elaborate accounts of the evolution of the human home beginning with the huts of the primitive Simianians </s>
<s> And in pursuing the very essential subject of Clothes and Fabrics we have not infrequently found ourselves in the midst of spacious preliminary dissertations on the structure of the loom beginning with that which was used by the Anthropenguins </s>
<s> Now we would not for the world speak disparagingly of looms or huts </s>
<s> We have ourselves examined some of them in the Hull House Museum in Chicago and in the woods of Canada and have found them instructive </s>
<s> We suggest only that college life is short that the college curriculum is crowded and that except possibly for those students who are especially interested in anthropology or in industrial evolution it would surely be a misfortune to learn the Simianian hut and to miss Rossetti's House of Life or to get the impression that as a cultural background for shirtwaists the Anthropengruinian loom can really compete with Carlyle's Sartor Resartus </s>
<s> If this occasional tendency toward exaggerating the importance of drainpipes windowcurtains and doormats were to grow strong and if girls as a class should be required to spend any large proportion of their time on the specialized history and sociology of feminine implements and tasks while the boys were still in the current of the affairs of the race we should indeed want President Thomas of Bryn Mawr to repeat on a thousand lecture platforms her indignant assertion of the fact that nothing more disastrous for women or for men can be conceived of than specialized education of women as a sex </s>
<s> These parenthetical observations however amount simply to the expression of our personal opinion that Home Economics like every new idea carries with it large quantities of dross which will have to be refined out in the smelter of trial </s>
<s> The real metal in it is its attempt to establish the principle that intelligent Consumption is an important and difficult task </s>
<s> For that reason it will not only desire but demand the utmost equality of educational opportunity </s>
<s> And women like men will continue to get their cultural backgrounds in the great achievements of the whole race where they can hold converse with Lincoln and Darwin and the makers of the Cologne Cathedral and George Meredith and Pasteur and Karl Marx and Whistler and Joan of Arc and St. John </s>
<s> The woman voiced a great truth who said that the soul which can irradiate the numberless pettinesses of home management and it is folly to deny that there ARE numberless pettinesses in it is the soul nourished elsewhere </s>
<s> Think it over </s>
<s> It tells the story </s>
<s> Whether that elsewhere is the deep recesses of her own religious nature or the wide stretches of the great arts and sciences it is always an elsewhere </s>
<s> Let that be granted as it must be granted </s>
<s> Let us say that there shall be no abridgment of the offerings of socalled academic education </s>
<s> What does a course of study like that of Mr. Harvey's Homemakers' School attempt to add to academic education </s>
<s> Principally three things </s>
<s> First Certain manual arts </s>
<s> Second Certain domestic applications of the physical and sociological sciences </s>
<s> Third Money Sense in Expenditure in the course on Household Management </s>
<s> The last of these three things is appearing in many places </s>
<s> At the University of Illinois for instance Professor Kinley now delegate from the United States to the PanAmerican Congress has given courses in Home Administration for women which he has regarded as of equal importance with his courses in Business Administration for men </s>
<s> At the University of Chicago in the Department of Household Administration Course 44 is on The Administration of the House and includes the proper apportionment of income </s>
<s> The business man says My sales cost or my manufacturing cost or my officeforce cost is such and such a per cent </s>
<s> of my total cost </s>
<s> When it goes above that I want to know why and I find out and if there isn't a mighty good reason for its going up I make it go down again to where it was </s>
<s> Shall we come to the day when in spending the money which has been earned in business we shall say Such and such a per cent </s>
<s> to food and such and such a per cent </s>
<s> to clothes and such and such a per cent </s>
<s> to shelter and such and such a per cent </s>
<s> to health and recreation and such and such a per cent </s>
<s> to good works and such and such other per cents </s>
<s> to various other purposes </s>
<s> Shall we come to the day when we shall consume wealth with as much forethought and with as much balance of judgment between conflicting claims as we now exhibit in acquiring wealth </s>
<s> They are trying to develop this Costs System for Home Expenditures in many of the schools and departments of Home Economics today </s>
<s> They believe that most people because of not looking ahead and because of not making definite plans based on previous experience come to the contemplation of their bills on the first of each month with every reason to confess that they have bought those things which they ought not to have bought and have left unbought those things which they ought to have bought </s>
<s> But it is not only a matter of reaching a systematic instead of a helterskelter enjoyment of the offerings of the world </s>
<s> It is also a matter of reaching by study of money values a mental habit of economy </s>
<s> And it comes at a time when that habit is needed </s>
<s> We are just beginning to realize in the United States that we cannot spend all our annual earnings on living expenses and still have a surplus for fresh capital for new industrial enterprises </s>
<s> We are on the point of perceiving that we are cramping and stunting the future industrial expansion of the country by our personal extravagance </s>
<s> We shall soon really believe Mr. James J </s>
<s> Hill when he says that every dollar unprofitably spent is a crime against posterity </s>
<s> When international industrial competition reaches its climax that nation will have an advantage whose people feel most keenly that the wise expenditure of income is a patriotic as well as a personal duty </s>
<s> But is this a matter for women alone </s>
<s> Do not men also consume </s>
<s> Are there no vats in Milwaukee no stills in Kentucky no factories wrapping paperrings around bunches of dead leaves at Tampa </s>
<s> Are there no men's tailors gents' furnishing shops luncheons clubs banquets athletics celebrations </s>
<s> And as for home expenditures themselves is the man simply to bring the plunder to the door get patted on the head and trot off in search of more plunder </s>
<s> We must doubt if economy will be reached by such a route </s>
<s> We find ourselves agreeing rather with the Home Economics lecturer who said There never yet was a family income really wisely expended without cooperation in all matters between husband and wife </s>
<s> The Massachusetts legislature has passed a law looking toward the teaching of Thrift in the public schools </s>
<s> Boys and girls need it equally </s>
<s> And we venture to surmise that in so far as the new art and science of Consumption is concerned with wise spending the bulk of its teachings ultimately will be enjoyed by both sexes </s>
<s> It will not be to any great extent a specialized education for women </s>
<s> So much for the Money Sense in Expenditure which a full Home Economics course adds to academic education </s>
<s> The more we admit its value the more convinced we must be that it ought to include every kind of expenditure and both kinds of human being </s>
<s> A precisely similar conviction arises with regard to those domestic applications of the physical and sociological sciences which a full Home Economics course adds to an academic education </s>
<s> Those domestic applications are most of them broadly human applications </s>
<s> They bear on daily living exercise fresh air personal cleanliness diet sleep the avoidance of contagion methods of fighting off disease general physical efficiency </s>
<s> They all amount to what Mrs. Ellen H </s>
<s> Richards calls Right Living </s>
<s> She would have four R's instead of three Reading Riting Rithmetic and Right Living </s>
<s> Now is Right Living to be only for girls </s>
<s> Mr. Eliot of Harvard does not think so </s>
<s> In a recent Survey of the Needs of Education he said Public instruction in preventive medicine must be provided for all children and the hygienic method of living must be taught in all schools </s>
<s> . . . To make this new knowledge and skill a universal subject of instruction in our schools colleges and universities is by no means impossibleindeed it would not even be difficult for it is a subject full of natural history as well as social interest </s>
<s> . . . American schools of every sort ought to provide systematic instruction on public and private hygiene diet sex hygiene and the prevention of disease and premature death not only because these subjects profoundly affect human affections and public happiness but because they are of high economic importance </s>
<s> A large part of Home Economics is simply Living Conditions </s>
<s> It is simply the lessons of Bacteriology Chemistry Physiology and Sociology about the common facts of daily physical and social existence </s>
<s> It may very well be therefore that what Mr. Eliot had in mind will not only come to pass but will even exceed his expectations </s>
<s> It may very well be that the educational policy of the future was correctly searchlighted by Miss Henrietta I </s>
<s> Goodrich who used to direct the Boston School of Housekeeping before it was merged into Simmons College when she said We need to have courage to break the present courses in household arts and domestic science into their component parts and begin again on the much broader basis of a study of living conditions </s>
<s> Our plea would be this that instruction in the facts of daily living be incorporated in the state's educational system from the primary grades through the graduate departments of the universities with a rank equal to that of any subject that is taught AS REQUIRED WORK FOR BOTH BOYS AND GIRLS </s>
<s> We revert now finally to the manual arts which a full course in Home Economics adds to an academic education </s>
<s> In this matter just as in the matter of Money Sense in Expenditure and in the matter of Right Living we observe that the ultimate issue of the movement is not so much a specialized education for women as a practical efficiency in the common things of life for men and women both </s>
<s> A reasonable proficiency in manual arts will some day be the heritage of all educated people </s>
<s> Mr. Eliot in his Survey of the Needs of Education speaks appreciatingly of his father's having caused him to learn carpentry and woodturning </s>
<s> He goes on to say This I hold to be the great need of education in the United Statesthe devoting of a much larger proportion of the total school time to the training of the eye ear and hand </s>
<s> It follows then that cooking and sewing for girls in the elementary schools must be made just as rigorous a discipline for eye and hand as woodworking is for boys </s>
<s> It even follows that boys and girls will often get their manual training together </s>
<s> It will not be a case of household drudgery for the girls while the boys are studying civics </s>
<s> Somewhere in this article and as close to this paragraph as we can get the Art Director to put it the reader will find a picture of the living room of the model house of the WashingtonAllston Elementary School in Boston </s>
<s> The boys and girls of graduating grade in that school give four hours a week to matters connected with the welfare of that house </s>
<s> They have furnished it throughout with their own handiwork the girls making pillowcases wallcoverings windowcurtains etc </s>
<s> and the boys making chairs tables cupboards etc </s>
<s> Succeeding classes will furnish it again </s>
<s> THE REASON WHY MR. CRAWFORD THE MASTER OF THE SCHOOL CHOSE TO HAVE A HOUSE FOR A MANUAL TRAINING LABORATORY WAS SIMPLY THAT A HOUSE OFFERS AMPLER OPPORTUNITIES THAN ANY OTHER KIND OF PLACE FOR INSTRUCTION IN THE PRACTICAL EFFICIENCIES OF DAILY LIVING FOR BOTH SEXES </s>
<s> The system will be complete when the girls get a bigger training in design by making more of the chairs and when the boys get a bigger training in diet by doing more of the cooking </s>
<s> IV LAST month's article ended with the inquiry whether the new education for homemaking would clash seriously with the modern young woman's necessary education for moneyearning </s>
<s> We conclude that it will not </s>
<s> Such developments as the long specialized fouryear course in Household Economics at Simmons College in Boston are not here in point </s>
<s> That Simmons course is more than an education for homemaking </s>
<s> It is an education for earning money by teaching homemaking or by becoming among other things a dietitian in a hospital or a manager of a lunchroom or an interior decorator </s>
<s> Our subject is not Home Economics as a moneyearning occupation for a few women but Home Economics as part of the education of all women </s>
<s> In that aspect it does not seem likely to result in any special feminine education of such bulk as to withdraw women in any serious degree from the general education of the race </s>
<s> This is undeniably true provided our observations have been correct that 1 </s>
<s> Home Economics is at heart Consumption and must be so because the home woman is more and more purely a consumer </s>
<s> 2 </s>
<s> Consumption is the broadest of generalities requiring the broadest of liberal educations </s>
<s> 3 </s>
<s> So far as manual arts are concerned the nonacademic cookery of the girl is balanced by the nonacademic carpentry of the boy </s>
<s> 4 </s>
<s> Right Living and Wise Spending will to a great extent get diffused throughout the whole educational system for boys and girls men and women alike </s>
<s> If there remains and there does remain certain further specialization which the average girl needs in order to be a good wife mother and homemaker she will get it in finishing courses furnished at the various levels of the educational system when she leaves school or else better still she will get it in continuation schools for adults to which she may resort when she is actually going to be a wife mother or homemaker </s>
<s> Why learn really technical specialized things years and years before they are needed </s>
<s> Why learn them at a time when it is not certain that they will be needed at all </s>
<s> The modern postponement of marriage is here a controlling element </s>
<s> The fact that in Boston among women from thirty to thirtyfour years of age 297 out of every 1000 more than a quarter are still unmarried is usually put down to a scarcity of men </s>
<s> That scarcity is exaggerated </s>
<s> Observe the comparative numbers of unmarried women and of unmarried men in that ageperiod in Boston Unmarried Women 8081 Unmarried Men 10651 </s>
<s> Observe further The total number of men of all conjugal conditions in the ageperiod in question is 28603 </s>
<s> A little work with pencil and paper will now still further weaken the scarcity theory by revealing the fact that in Boston among men from thirty to thirtyfour years of age 372 out of every 1000 are still single </s>
<s> Social conditions in rural communities tend to approach those of urban communities </s>
<s> Social conditions in the West tend to approach those in the East </s>
<s> Boston is not eccentric </s>
<s> It is only ahead </s>
<s> Continuation School instruction in Home Economics for engaged and married women is a form of education beginning to appear in every part of the world </s>
<s> But it lies beyond the woman's period of moneyearning </s>
<s> How long is that period </s>
<s> And what are the social and racial consequences of the fact that speaking generally the more highly prepared modern men and women are to transmit intelligence to posterity the more steadily do they tend to give their most vigorous years to singleness </s>
<s> I'LL NIVER GO HOME AGAIN </s>
<s> By ARTHUR STRINGER I'll niver go home again Home to the ould sad hills Home through the ould soft rain Where the curlew calls and thrills </s>
<s> For I thought to find the ould wee house Wid the moss along the wall </s>
<s> And I thought to hear the cracklegrouse And the braebirds call </s>
<s> And I sez I'll find the glad wee burn And the bracken in the glen And the fairythorn beyont the turn And the same ould men </s>
<s> But the ways I'd loved and walked avick Were no more home to me Wid their sthreets and turns av starin' brick And no ould face to see </s>
<s> And the ould glad ways I'd helt in mind Loike the home av Moira Bawn And the ould green turns I'd dreamt to find They all were lost and gone </s>
<s> And the bairns that romped by Tullagh Burn Whin they saw me sthopped their play Through a mist av tears I tried to turn And ghostlike creep away </s>
<s> And I'll niver go home again </s>
<s> Home to the ould lost years Home where the soft warm rain Drifts loike the drip av tears </s>
