<s> By WILLIAM HARD III LOVE DEFERRED Mary felt she would wait for John even if instead of going away on a career he were going away on a comet </s>
<s> She waited for him from the time she was twentytwo to the time she was twentysix and would have waited longer if she hadn't got angry and insisted on marrying him </s>
<s> Into why she waited and why she wouldn't wait any longer chance put most of the simple plot of the commonplace modern drama Love Deferred </s>
<s> It is so commonplace that it is doubtful if any other drama can so stretch the nerves or can so draw from them a thin high note of fine pain </s>
<s> We will pretend that John was a doctor </s>
<s> No that's too professional </s>
<s> He was a civil engineer </s>
<s> That's professional enough and more commercial </s>
<s> It combines Technique and Business which are the two big elements in the life of Modern Man </s>
<s> When they got engaged Mary was through college but John had one more year to go in engineering school </s>
<s> How the preparation for life does lengthen itself out </s>
<s> When Judge Story was professor at Harvard in the thirties of the last century he put the law into his pupils' heads in eighteen months </s>
<s> The present professors require three years </s>
<s> In 1870 the Harvard Medical School made you attend classes for four months in each of three years </s>
<s> It now makes you do it for nine months in each of four years </s>
<s> As for engineering the University of Wisconsin gave John a chill by informing him in its catalogue that it is coming to be generally recognized that a fouryear technical course following the highschool course is not an adequate preparation for those who are to fill important positions and the University would urge all those who can afford the time to extend their studies over a period of five or six years </s>
<s> John compromised on five </s>
<s> This gave him a few Business courses in the College of Commerce in addition to his regular Technique courses in the College of Engineering </s>
<s> He was now a Bachelor of Science </s>
<s> He thereupon became an apprentice in the shops of one of the two biggest electrical firms in the United States </s>
<s> He inspected the assembling of machines before they were shipped and he overheard wisdom from foremen and superintendents </s>
<s> His salary was fifteen cents an hour </s>
<s> Since he worked about ten hours a day his total income was about forty dollars a month </s>
<s> At the end of the year he was raised to fifty </s>
<s> This was the normal raise for a Bachelor of Science </s>
<s> The graduates of Yale and Harvard in the bright colonial days of those institutions married almost immediately on graduation </s>
<s> John didn't </s>
<s> He didn't get married so early nor become a widower so often </s>
<s> He didn't carry so many children to the christening font nor so many to the cemetery </s>
<s> Look at the dark as well as the bright side of colonial days </s>
<s> Pick out any of the early Harvard classes </s>
<s> Honestly and truly at random run your finger down the column and pick any class </s>
<s> The class of 1671 </s>
<s> It had eleven graduates </s>
<s> One of them remained a bachelor </s>
<s> Don't be too severe on him </s>
<s> He died at twentyfour </s>
<s> Of the remaining ten four were married twice and two were married three times </s>
<s> For ten husbands therefore there were eighteen wives </s>
<s> Mr. G </s>
<s> Stanley Hall President of Clark University very competently remarks The problem of superfluous women did not exist in those days </s>
<s> They were all needed to bring up another woman's children </s>
<s> The ten husbands of the Harvard class of 1671 with their eighteen wives had seventyone children </s>
<s> They did replenish the earth </s>
<s> They also filled the churchyards </s>
<s> TWENTYONE OF THOSE SEVENTYONE CHILDREN DIED IN CHILDHOOD </s>
<s> This left fifty to grow up </s>
<s> It was an average of five surviving children for each of the ten fathers </s>
<s> But it was an average of only 2.7 for each of the eighteen mothers </s>
<s> In commending the colonial family one must make an offset for the unfair frequency with which it had more than one wifeandmother to help out its fertility record </s>
<s> And in commending the era of young wives and numerous children one must make an offset for the hideous frequency with which it killed them </s>
<s> Turn from Harvard to Yale </s>
<s> Look at the men who graduated from 1701 to 1745 </s>
<s> The girls they took in marriage were most of them under twentyone and were many of them down in their 'teens sometimes as far down as fourteen </s>
<s> May we observe that they were not taken in marriage out of a conscious sense of duty to the Commonwealth and to Population </s>
<s> They were taken because they were needed </s>
<s> The colonial gentleman had to have his soapkettles and candlemolds and looms and smokehouses and saltingtubs and spinningwheels and other industrial machines operated for him by somebody if he was going to get his food and clothes and other necessaries cheap </s>
<s> He lost money if he wasn't domestic </s>
<s> He was domestic </s>
<s> Our young engineering friend John when HE looked forward to HIS future domestic establishment saw no industrial machines in it at all except a needle and a saucepan </s>
<s> Consequently he had very little real use for a wife </s>
<s> What he wanted was money enough to give Mary a home </s>
<s> Marriages are more uncertain now </s>
<s> And fewer of them are marriages of mere convenience </s>
<s> It is both a worse and a better state of things </s>
<s> On the one hand John didn't marry Mary so soon </s>
<s> On the other hand he was prevented from wanting anything in his marriage except just Mary </s>
<s> The enormous utility of the colonial wife issuing in enormous toil complicated by unlimited childbearing had this kind of result Among the wives of the 418 Yale husbands of the period from 1701 to 1745 there were Thirtythree who died before they were twentyfive years old Fiftyfive who died before they were thirtyfive years old Fiftynine who died before they were fortyfive years old </s>
<s> Those 418 Yale husbands lost 147 wives before full middle age </s>
<s> It ceases therefore to be surprising though it remains unabatedly sickening that the stories of the careers of colonial college men of the bestbred men of the times are filled with such details as First wife died at twentyfour leaving six children </s>
<s> Eight children born within twelve years two of them feebleminded </s>
<s> First wife died at nineteen leaving three children </s>
<s> Fourteen children </s>
<s> First wife died at twentyeight having borne eight children in ten years </s>
<s> From that age of universal early marrying and of promiscuous early dying we have come in two centuries to an age of delayed and even omitted marrying and of a settled determination to keep on living </s>
<s> The women's colleges are so new and they attracted in their early days so unaverage a sort of girl that their records are not conclusive </s>
<s> Nevertheless here are some guiding facts from Smith College of Northampton Massachusetts We are taking college facts not because this article is confined in any respect to college people but merely because the matrimonial histories in the records of the colleges are the most complete we know of </s>
<s> In 1888 Smith College in its first ten classes had graduated 370 women </s>
<s> In 1903 fifteen years later among those 370 women there were 212 who were still single </s>
<s> This record does not satisfy Mr. G </s>
<s> Stanley Hall who figured it out </s>
<s> The remaining facts however might be considered more cheering The 158 Smith women who had married had borne 315 children </s>
<s> This was two for each of them </s>
<s> And most of them were still in their childbearing period </s>
<s> Compare this with the colonial records </s>
<s> But don't take the number of children per colonial father </s>
<s> Be fair </s>
<s> Take it per mother </s>
<s> We have the matrimonial histories of colonial Yale and Harvard men grouped and averaged according to the decade in which they graduated </s>
<s> We will regard the graduates of each decade as together constituting one case </s>
<s> In no case does the average number of children per wife go higher than 3.89 </s>
<s> In one case it goes as low as 2.98 </s>
<s> Perhaps the modern wife's habit of going on living and thereby protracting her period of childbearing will in time cause her fertility record to compare not unfavorably with that of the colonial wife who made an early start but a quick finish </s>
<s> In the year 1903 among all the 370 Smith graduates in those first ten classes only twentyfour had died </s>
<s> And among all the 315 children only twentysix had died </s>
<s> On the whole between being the wife of a Yale or Harvard colonial graduate and being a member of one of the first ten Smith classes a modern girl might conclude that the chances of being a dead one matrimonially in the latter case would be more than offset by the chances of being a dead one actually in the former </s>
<s> This deplorable flippancy would overlook the serious fact that permanent or even prolonged celibacy on the part of large numbers of young men and young women is a great social evil </s>

<s> Very well </s>

<s> Getting married early is imputed unto us for actual personal righteousness by innumerable clergymen essayists and editorial writers </s>

<s> One hundred and fifteen more out of every thousand </s>

<s> Here's Bailey's book on Social Conditions Live in England and be a girl and belong to the class of people that miners come from Your age at marriage will be on the average twentytwo </s>
<s> But belong to the class of people that professional men come from Your age at marriage will be on the average twentysix </s>

<s> It is in the direct line of social and economic development </s>
<s> The professional man is a farther developed type of man than the miner </s>
<s> It takes him longer to get through his educational infancylonger to arrive at his mental and financial maturity </s>
<s> The professional man's wife is a farther developed type than the miner's wife </s>
<s> She has much more economic value if she works before marriage and much LESS economic value in any case after marriage </s>
<s> Where these two lines of development male and female come to a meeting point where the man's infancy is longest and the woman's economic value as a wife is least there is necessarily altogether apart from personal preferences the greatest postponement of marriage </s>
<s> The United States except possibly in certain sections has not come to the end of its growth toward postponed marriage </s>
<s> It is true that in Massachusetts within the past fortyfive years the average age of women at marriage has risen from 20.7 to 24.6 </s>
<s> That is a very modern and developed marriage age </s>
<s> But many of the older countries surpass it </s>
<s> In Belgium for instance which is a most intensely industrialized country the average age of women at marriage is 28.19 </s>
<s> It is hard indeed to look at the advancing marriage age and to compare its varying rate of progress in different continents different countries different localities and different social circles without admitting that whatever whirling nebulous mists of personal preferences it may create and carry with it its nucleus is purely economic </s>
<s> Early marriage was made by economic advantages </s>
<s> It was destroyed by economic changes </s>
<s> It will not be restored except by economic adjustments </s>
<s> Nevertheless said Mary I want John </s>
<s> John had finished being engineer for the electric railway company </s>
<s> Out of his two years' experience he had saved a few hundred dollars </s>
<s> No he hadn't </s>
<s> That isn't probable </s>
<s> The way he made his start into the next phase of his career was not by having any ready money </s>
<s> Having ready money is far from being characteristic of the young man of today </s>
<s> John opened his office as a consulting electrical engineer not on his own resources but as an agent for an electrical supply company </s>
<s> Being agent for that company assured him enough money to pay the office rent and stenographer </s>
<s> For the rest for his meals and his bed he depended on his clients </s>
<s> Whom he didn't have </s>
<s> But he started out to get them </s>
<s> He opened his office in the city in which Mary was </s>
<s> And then a strange but normal thing occurred </s>
<s> They spent enough money on theatres and boat rides and candy in the next three months to have paid the rent on a flat </s>
<s> It is true John's net income was too small and uncertain to have justified the founding of a family </s>
<s> But it was also true that they spent every cent they had </s>
<s> The celibate life is an extravagant life </s>
<s> One of the innumerable sources of modern extravagance is found just there </s>
<s> Mary reflected on it </s>
<s> She didn't like it </s>
<s> And she began to see other things she didn't like in this protraction of the period of singleness </s>
<s> Her work for the Bureau of Labor had taken her into many places among all sorts of women </s>
<s> She began to observe the irregular living which is inevitably associated with a system of late marriages </s>
<s> Mr. Lester F </s>
<s> Ward has learnedly and elaborately informed us that if we go back to the origin of life on this planet we shall find that the female was the only sex then existent being original life itself reproducing itself by division of itself and that the male was created as an afterthought of nature's for the purpose of introducing greater variation into the development of living things </s>
<s> The male to begin with had only one function </s>
<s> That was to be a male </s>
<s> He was purely a sexthing </s>
<s> Whether this biological theory stands or falls it is certain that it squares with the present character of the sexes </s>
<s> The sex which originated as a sexthing remains the more actively sexed </s>
<s> There was once a very good sociologist called Robert Louis Stevenson who made many researches into the psychology of the human race </s>
<s> While on his Inland Voyage he observed in this matter that it is no use for a man to take to the woods we know him Anthony tried the same thing long ago and had a pitiful time of it by all accounts </s>
<s> But there is this about some women that they suffice to themselves and can walk in a high and cold zone without the countenance of any trousered being </s>
<s> The celibate life is more possible for most of them by nature </s>
<s> If it were not for that fact the postponement of marriage would by this time have demolished the ethical code </s>
<s> Even as things stand Mary was quite willing to admit when she saw it that there are two kinds of women greatly increasing in modern days </s>
<s> Both have always existed but now they are increasing very rapidly and in parallel lines of corresponding development </s>
<s> In one column is the enormous army of young women who remain unmarried till twentyfive till thirty till thirtyfive </s>
<s> Even at that latter age and beyond it in a welldeveloped city like say Providence Rhode Island in the age period from thirtyfive to fortyfive twenty out of every hundred women are still single </s>
<s> In the other column is the enormous army of young women who outside of the marriage relation altogether lead a professional sex life venal furtive ignoble and debasing an army which has existed since the beginning of time but which every postponement of the age of marriage causes to increase in relative numbers and to gain new strength for poisoning the blood of life </s>
<s> Love denied at the front door flies in by the cellar window </s>
<s> Angel or bat it is always with us </s>
<s> Our only choice is between its guises </s>
<s> Mary looked at the army of women celibates in offices and in stores and in their apartments and in their boarding houses women celibates five and ten and fifteen and twenty years into the period when nature has by irrepealable edict ordained love </s>
<s> It was surely unnatural for the mass of them </s>
<s> They were not vowed nuns </s>
<s> They were not devoted to any Great Cause </s>
<s> They were just ordinary normal young women thousands and thousands and thousands and thousands of them </s>
<s> Then on the other side Mary looked at the great army of women in the midnight restaurants in the streets in their segregated quarterswomen who however they may be sentimentalized about and however irresponsible they may be for their own condition are as a matter of fact ignorant stupid silly and dirty </s>
<s> Yet on them was squandered the emotional life of millions of young men </s>
<s> On the one sideintelligent capable effective young women leading lives of emotional sterility </s>
<s> On the other sideinferior women blasted and withered by their specialization in the emotional life of youth </s>
<s> The connection between postponement of marriage and irregularity of living will be admitted by everybody who is willing to face facts and who is optimist enough to believe that if instead of letting facts lie we face them and fight them we can make a better race </s>
<s> The great Russian scientist Metchnikoff successor to Pasteur in the Pasteur Institute mentions the postponement of marriage as one of the biological disharmonies of life </s>
<s> It is a disharmony that among highly civilized peoples marriage and REGLULAR unions are impossible at the RIGHT TIME </s>
<s> And Mr. A </s>
<s> S </s>
<s> Johnson writing in the authoritative report of the Committee of Fifteen on the Social Evil notes the parallel increase of young unmarried men and of a city's volume of vice </s>
<s> He goes on to make without comment a statement of the economic facts of the case </s>
<s> As a rule he says the income which a young man earns while sufficient to secure a fair degree of comfort for himself does not suffice for founding a family </s>
<s> He cannot found a family at the right time </s>
<s> He goes unmarried through the romantic period of his development when the senses are at their keenest and when the other sex in its most vividly idealized perfection is most poignantly desired </s>
<s> Then later on he may begin to get a larger income </s>
<s> Then marriage may become more feasible </s>
<s> But then romance is waning </s>
<s> Then as Mr. Johnson says his standard of personal comfort rises </s>
<s> Romance has been succeeded by calculation </s>
<s> Accordingly he postpones marriage to a date in the indefinite future or abandons expectation of it altogether </s>
<s> Celibacy through the age of romance </s>
<s> It's emotionally wrong </s>
<s> Sexlessness for a score of years after sex has awakened </s>
<s> It's biologically wrong </s>
<s> It's a defiance of nature </s>
<s> And nature responds as she does to every defiance with a scourge of physical and social ills </s>
<s> But what of all that </s>
<s> thought Mary </s>
<s> Those things are just observations </s>
<s> What I am going to act on is that I want John </s>
<s> At which point she stopped being a typical modern young woman </s>
<s> SHE BECAME A WOMAN OF THE FUTURE </s>
<s> Look here she said to John I'm working </s>
<s> You're working </s>
<s> We're single </s>
<s> Very well </s>
<s> We'll change it </s>
<s> I'm working </s>
<s> You're working </s>
<s> We're married </s>
<s> Have we lost anything </s>
<s> And we've gained each other </s>

<s> She couldn't operate soapkettles and candlemolds and looms and smokehouses and saltingtubs and spinningwheels for him </s>
<s> But she brought him an equivalent of it in money </s>

<s> Sometimes she had to contribute some of her own money to his expense accounts </s>

<s> They had not postponed their love till with a settled income John could support her in comfort and they could look back like Browning's middleaged estranged lovers to say We have not sighed deep laughed free Starved feasted despairedbeen happy </s>
<s> It used to take two to start a home in colonial days Mary would say </s>

<s> People risk too much when they start a family before they become sufficiently used to marriage and to each other to know that they can keep on loving each other and to know that they have in them through their mutual continued happiness the power to make a happy home a noble home for children to live in </s>
<s> As for the number of children she will havewe reserve that subject to a future article </s>
<s> We call attention here only to this That the facts which were cited from the Smith College records are harmonious with many other facts and records tending to show that the fertility of the modern wife has been considerably underrated just as the fertility of the colonial wife has been considerably exaggerated </s>
<s> And this That Mary got to her childbearing period sooner than she would have if she hadn't insisted on marrying John before he was ready to support her </s>
<s> Those two years would have been childless years in any case </s>
<s> But they would probably if it hadn't been for Mary's money have been lengthened into four or five </s>
<s> Of course later marriages in themselves tend to reduce the number of children </s>
<s> As to quality however the evidence is not clear </s>
<s> There is even some reason to think that a moderate postponement is conducive to an improvement in quality </s>
<s> Did you ever read Havelock Ellis's book called A Study of British Genius </s>
<s> He made a list of the most distinguished of Eminent British Persons and studied everything about them from their religious opinions to the color of their hair </s>
<s> In the matter of the age of their parents he finds that the average age of the father at the birth of the person of genius was thirtyseven years while the average of the mother was thirtyone </s>
<s> His conclusion is On the whole it would appear so far as the evidence goes that the fathers of our eminent persons have been predominantly middleaged and to a marked extent elderly at the time of the distinguished son's birth while the mothers have been predominantly at the period of greatest vigor and maturity and to a somewhat unusual extent elderly </s>
<s> There has been a notable deficiency of young fathers and still more notably of young mothers </s>
<s> And did you ever see the study which Mr. R </s>
<s> S </s>
<s> Holway made for the Department of Education of Leland Stanford University on The Age of Parents Its Effects upon Children </s>
<s> His conclusions are In most physical qualities the children of mature parents tend to come out best </s>
<s> In mental ability the children of young parents show best at an early age but rapidly lose their precocity </s>
<s> The elder children who show best tend to be the children of mature and old parents </s>
<s> The children of elderly mothers show a tendency to superiority throughout </s>
<s> Mary did not know about all this but she had a very strong opinion to the effect that in so far as the quality of her children could be affected by their home training she was glad she had spent at least a few years earning her living </s>
<s> Every woman said Mary ought to have some little time for developing into an individual </s>
<s> Home won't do it altogether </s>
<s> Not nowadays </s>
<s> The colonial home did being part of the working world </s>
<s> But what is the modern home </s>
<s> It is a nest an eddy a shelf a nook </s>
<s> It's something apart from the world </s>
<s> If a woman is going to prepare her son for a knowledge of the real world if she's going to be able to give him a training which has in it an understanding and an appreciation of the real world if she's going to be able to educate him into real living she must nowadays and increasingly in the future have some experience of her own on her own account in the real world before she becomes a mother </s>
<s> There's no getting away from that </s>
<s> A reasonable postponement of motherhood till the future mother becomes a competent individual is a good thing </s>
<s> The trouble about that said John is that it makes you too independent of me </s>
<s> Your proposition is to start in and earn your living till you're pretty good at it </s>

<s> Something exquisitely gratifying in being certain CERTAIN that it isn't just necessity that keeps her a home woman </s>
<s> If I were a man living in wedlock said Mary I should want the door of the cage always wide open with my mate fluttering straight by it every minute to still nestle by me </s>
<s> And I should want her wings to be strong and I should want her to know that if she went through the door she could fly </s>

<s> We want them </s>

<s> Mr. H </s>
<s> G </s>
