<s> Vol. XXIII October 1910 No </s>
<s> 4 The Poison Bugaboo pages 518525 By SAMUEL HOPKINS ADAMS AUTHOR OF THE GREAT AMERICAN FRAUD THE MYSTERY WITH STEWART EDWARD WHITE ETC </s>
<s> ROMANCE revels in the peril of the unknown </s>
<s> Lapped about with the armorplate of civilization the modern citizen muses relishingly like a child beguiling himself with ogre tales upon the terrors which lie just beyond his ken </s>
<s> To his mind A stone's throw out on either hand And all the world is wild and strange </s>
<s> Avid for sensation he peoples the remoteness of forest and mountain with malign and destructive creatures whence has grown up an extensive and astonishing literature of snake and insect poison lore </s>
<s> Deadly is the master word of the cult </s>
<s> The rattlesnake is deadly </s>
<s> The copperhead and moccasin are deadly </s>
<s> So is the wholly mythical puff adder </s>
<s> In hardly less degree is the tarantula deadly while varying lethal capacities are ascribed to the centipede the scorpion the kissingbug and sundry other forms of insect life </s>
<s> The whole matter is based upon the slenderest foundations </s>
<s> I don't mean by this that these illfamed species are wholly innocuous </s>
<s> It would be highly inadvisable to snatch a kiss from a copperhead or to stroke a tarantula's fur the wrong way </s>
<s> But one could do it and live to boast of the achievement </s>
<s> Pseudoscience to the contrary notwithstanding there is no living thing within the boundaries of the United States of America whose bite or sting is sure death or with one possible exception even probable death </s>
<s> There are five varieties of venomous serpents in this country three of them Crotalids and two belonging to the Elaps family </s>
<s> The Elaps are rather rare </s>
<s> The Crotalids rattlesnake moccasin and copperhead are common and of the widest geographical distribution </s>
<s> Yet on the basis of actual evidence the amazing fact stands out that only about eighty persons so far as is ascertainable have ever died from snake bite in the United States </s>
<s> Nowhere in the Civil War records does a death from this cause appear though hundreds of thousands of men were living on the country and at a time when the serpent clan was much more numerous than now </s>
<s> Estimates vary as to the proportion of deaths to bites </s>
<s> Prentiss Willson believes that something over ten per cent </s>
<s> of all persons bitten by venomous snakes in the United States die </s>
<s> As to how many of these succumb not to the venom but to the misdirected efforts of misguided friends at treatmentan extremely important differentiationhe lacks the data upon which to base a reckoning </s>
<s> S </s>
<s> Weir Mitchell's figures indicate 8.7 per cent </s>
<s> mortality for rattlesnake bite </s>
<s> This would make the venom about as dangerous as the toxin of typhoid fever which is not generally regarded as a necessarily deadly disease </s>
<s> Other writers go as high as fifteen per cent </s>
<s> for the rattlesnake and as low as one per cent </s>
<s> for the copperhead </s>
<s> All general estimates seem to me to leave one basic element out of considerationthe unnoted nonfatal snake bites </s>
<s> That a bite resulting in death will eventually get itself reported is reasonably certain </s>
<s> On the other hand I am satisfied from talking with plantation owners in the South with ranchmen in the West and with woodsmen and hunters all over the country that in the remoter regions many instances of poisoning by copperheads and the smaller rattlesnakes never attain the dignity of being listed so insignificant are they in their effects </s>
<s> Were all these to be recorded I believe that the mortality ratio would fall notably </s>
<s> Although I have been interested in the subject for many years I have never met a man who has seen a fatal case of snake bite </s>
<s> More than this my friend Mr. Stewart Edward White a noted hunter and explorer of untrodden ground in regions infested by reptiles has known of but one case terminating in death which he believes to be authentic </s>
<s> Dr. J </s>
<s> A </s>
<s> Mitchell of Victoria Texas one of the most experienced of field observers has never met with an instance of fatality from this cause </s>
<s> Dr. Mitchell believes that horses always and dogs almost always recover from rattlesnake bite </s>
<s> He confirms from observation the mysterious fact that hogs exhibit absolute immunity from the venom </s>
<s> WHISKY VS. SNAKEBITE Be it remembered always that death following snake bite is not necessarily the same thing as death from snake bite </s>
<s> Error in treatment plays no small part in vitiating the statistics </s>
<s> For error read whisky </s>
<s> Whoever is primarily responsible for the hoary superstition that liquor in huge doses is useful in snake poisoning has many a life to answer for </s>
<s> Apart from any adventitious aid whatsoever whether from a snake or any other source a whole bottle of raw whisky forced down the throat of a man unaccustomed to alcohol is pretty likely to kill him and is absolutely certain to cause grave poisoning </s>
<s> Add to this that it is given often in such a manner that the reaction from it comes contemporaneously with the heart collapse caused by the venom and a telling commentary upon the method is suggested </s>
<s> It is a question whether alcohol should ever be given in such cases without the advice of a physician </s>
<s> Certain it is that it should not be poured into the victim in quantities limited only by the flaskcontents of the bystanders </s>
<s> Several years ago I saw two interestingly contrasted cases of copperhead bite </s>
<s> The first patient was a powerful fullblooded temperate Irish daylaborer who while roadmending was bitten on the back of the hand between two fingers </s>
<s> His fellows hustled him off to a room over a neighboring saloon where they proceeded to administer the classic treatment </s>
<s> Before the doctor arrived they had introduced a quart and a half of whisky into a stomach unused to anything stronger than beer in small quantities </s>
<s> Six hours later when I saw the man through the wreckage of chairs tables and bedding four battered friends were trying to hold him down </s>
<s> They thought he was having convulsions from the snake venom </s>
<s> He wasn't </s>
<s> He was having delirium tremens from the whisky </s>
<s> His arm and shoulder were purple and swollen </s>
<s> Later he collapsed </s>
<s> Will he die </s>
<s> I asked the doctor </s>
<s> He won't die of the bite but I think he will of the whisky replied the disgusted practitioner </s>
<s> But he didn't </s>
<s> His splendid physique pulled him through </s>
<s> It was long however before he wholly recovered from the effects of the two poisons </s>
<s> This was in a Hudson River town </s>
<s> Only a few miles away a negro boy shortly after was struck by a copperhead on the bare leg </s>
<s> The wound was a deep doublefanged puncture </s>
<s> While the boy's father rushed for whisky his mother ran for the doctor </s>
<s> The doctor got there first </s>
<s> He opened up the wound and rubbed in permanganate of potash to oxidize the venom and destroy its toxic properties </s>
<s> When I talked with the boy two days later he was hobbling about on a crutch and the swelling had almost subsided </s>
<s> Setting the boy's lesser age and resistant power against the fact of the laborer's being bitten in a worse place for crotaline venom is much more effective in an upper limb or extremity than in a lower we have a fairly illustrative instance of the relative merits of alcoholic and nonalcoholic measures </s>
<s> WHEN RATTLESNAKES KILL Thirteen cases of death following rattlesnake and copperhead bite in which satisfactory clinical data were obtainable are given by Prentiss Willson </s>
<s> Of the victims five were young children one was a fourteenyearold boy one a chronic drunkard and one a leper who submitted to the stroke of a captive rattlesnake in the mad hope that it would cure his affliction </s>
<s> It didin twentyfour hours </s>
<s> Of the remaining five three were dosed with alcohol in large quantities </s>
<s> In several of the cases notably those of the children there seemed to be at least an even chance of recovery when the ligatures binding the affected limb were loosened to relieve the pain with quickly fatal results </s>
<s> Two of the fatalities were attributed not immediately to the venom but to the secondary bloodpoisoning this being the case with the only copperhead bite in the list </s>
<s> Death resulting typically from crotaline poisoning occurred in two instances one the fourteenyearold boy who was struck by a large rattlesnake and died in six hours despite skilled and prompt medical attendance the other a Dr. Post into whose veins it would appear the poison entered immediately since a jet of blood spurted from the wound inflicted by the captive rattlesnake </s>
<s> The man passed from great agony into coma from which he never rallied death ensuing in five hours after the bite </s>
<s> There is nothing in these data to indicate that a fullgrown man in normal health and with proper treatment will succumb to crotaline poisoning unless the venom enters a vein direct </s>
<s> In the matter of the comparative potency of snake poisons there are apparent contradictions </s>
<s> In the order of recorded fatalities the rattlesnake ranks easily first with the water moccasin a rather distant second and the copperhead a very poor third </s>
<s> Yet experiments upon animals indicate that moccasin venom is five times as powerful as rattlesnake though only three times as powerful as copperhead </s>
<s> Taking the cobra as the basis of estimate it requires only twice as much moccasin venom as it does cobra poison to kill a guinea pig whereas it requires six times as much copperhead and ten times as much rattlesnake virus </s>
<s> Why then is the rattler preeminent over its more virulent cousins </s>
<s> Probably for two reasonsthe greater amount of venom secreted and the superior power with which the rattler drives its fangs home </s>
<s> NO VIPERS IN THIS COUNTRY Fully as much terror attaches in the country districts to the puff adder or sand viper as to the rattlesnake or copperhead </s>
<s> This is a suggestive bit of superstition since there's no such thing as an adder or viper on the Western hemisphere and never has been one unless it came carefully pickled in a jar </s>
<s> What passes for the supposedly deadly reptile is the common hognosed or bull snake </s>
<s> It is about as dangerous as an infuriated rabbit </s>
<s> But it puts up one of the best bluffs known to natural history </s>
<s> When caught at its favorite occupation of basking in the open without convenient avenue of escape it flattens its head and strikes right and left blowing and hissing with an aspect much more terrifying than that of the truly venomous species </s>
<s> Then when the objects of its fury have taken to trees or adjacent fences it glides quietly away into the grass and effaces itself </s>
<s> Any one who has the nerve to look it between the eyes may uncover its pretense </s>
<s> For by this token may be known the real Crotalids from the mock a small but distinct pit between eye and nostril </s>
<s> Lacking this mark no ventral crawler in the land of the free need cause a flutter in the most timid breast with one notable exception </s>
<s> BEWARE THE ELAPS Shun as you would a rabid dog a pretty little redandblack banded serpent about as thick as your thumb </s>
<s> If any living creature whose habitat is the United States deserves the epithet deadly it is the Elaps </s>
<s> Two species are known the harlequin snake which ranges throughout the Gulf states to Texas and up the Mississippi River to Ohio and the Sonoran coral snake found in the Southwest only </s>
<s> By a strange perversion of facts while the harmless hognosed snake enjoys a repute of terror the Elaps most dangerous of all American reptiles is commonly regarded as harmless </s>
<s> Partly this is due to its slight and graceful prettiness partly to its innocentappearing head which shows no flattening the popularly understood mark of the venomous species and partly to its lethargic and peaceful disposition </s>
<s> Experimenters wishing to secure the venom of the Elaps often find it difficult to rouse the snake to striking wrath </s>
<s> Very few instances are known of Elaps bite but those few unquestionably set this ornamental creature in a class by itself among American Ophidia for results </s>
<s> Out of eight wellauthenticated cases of Elaps bite six of the victims died </s>
<s> This is believed to indicate a falsely large percentage however the scientific estimate of mortality being somewhere between twentyfive and fifty per cent </s>
<s> A government scientist tells me of a curious result from coralsnake bite which came under his notice </s>
<s> The victim who was handling the reptile preparatory to photographing it apparently overstepped the bounds of its habitual forbearance for it fastened upon his finger with such determination that it had to be pried off </s>
<s> The man soon became unconscious but rallied and after three days of dubious condition recovered </s>
<s> Every year since at about the anniversary of the bite an ulcer forms upon the finger and the nail sloughs off </s>
<s> I have heard of similar recurrent effects from crotaline poisoning but none scientifically attested as is this phenomenon </s>
<s> Before passing from the subject of snakes let me make one point clear </s>
<s> While the venomous snakes of this country are by no means deadly in the ordinary sense of the term their bite is always serious both in its immediate effects and in the possibility of after effects </s>
<s> The bitten person should get to a physician at once </s>
<s> The immediate treatment is prompt incision and sucking of the wound </s>
<s> Permanganate of potash for rubbing into the bitten place should always be carried by persons traveling in a snakeinfested country </s>
<s> If the bite is on a limb a light ligature will check the spread of the venom </s>
<s> Use whisky sparingly if at all and then only in case of complete collapse </s>
<s> The local treatments are most effective while the venom is still around the site of the bite and will reduce the injurious effects considerably </s>
<s> But after half an hour or so the absorption of the venom becomes more general and the local treatments ineffective </s>
<s> When the venom once enters into general circulation no chemicals or medication can neutralize its effects except a specific antivenin such as has been prepared by Dr. Noguchi at the Rockefeller Institute in New York </s>
<s> Antivenin is the only antidote that can counteract the action of venom anywhere in the body </s>
<s> It finds the venom wherever it is present and neutralizes it there without producing any ill effects on the system </s>
<s> GILA MONSTER NOT SO MONSTROUS Dissension and discussion have raged for years about the hideous head of the Gila monster </s>
<s> This great lizard of the Southwest has been pronounced absolutely deadly by one set of partisans and absolutely harmless by another </s>
<s> Somewhere between lies the truth </s>
<s> If any human being has actually been bitten by a heloderma the event has either escaped notice or has been so hedged about with obstructive legend as to have forfeited scientific credence </s>
<s> But the saurian itself has been studied and dissected and its venom has been analyzed </s>
<s> The venom is related to snake poison but is neither crotaline nor elapine </s>
<s> From animal experiments it is thought that it might be fatal to man under unfavorable conditions </s>
<s> There are no fangs proper </s>
<s> The poison gland is in the lower jaw instead of in the upper as in snakes and its product is projected through small ducts which open in the gums outside the teeth </s>
<s> The Gila monster has the grip of a bulldog </s>
<s> Torture will not loosen its hold once fastened on </s>
<s> It is through this intimate contact that the venom works into the wounds </s>
<s> Fortunately the lizard is slow to anger and prefers flight to battle so it is likely to be long before science has an opportunity of studying the effect of its envenomed jawclamp upon man </s>
<s> There are a few vaguely rumored reports of prospectors having perished in the desert of Gila monster poison but these are so confused with symptoms suspiciously resembling alcoholic poisoning as to lead Dr. R </s>
<s> W </s>
<s> Shufeldt an authority upon the Reptilia to remark that a quart of raw whisky practically given at one dose may prove more fatal than the bite of ten helodermas </s>
<s> Almost any kind of an insect bite or sting MAY prove fatal </s>
<s> So may a pin scratch if the blood of the subject be in bad enough condition </s>
<s> There is a wellsubstantiated case of a trained nurse who died from blood poisoning following a mosquito bite </s>
<s> Ant bite has resulted fatally as has a single sting from the common wasp </s>
<s> No one however considers these everyday insects as deadly </s>
<s> But substitute scorpion for ant and centipede for wasp and shrieks of dismay rise from the general throat </s>
<s> Yet perhaps there is no other variety of harmful creature whose reputation rests upon so meager a foundation as that of these two </s>
<s> True an El Paso report claims that a man stung by a whip scorpion died in twelve hours but the details are so vague as to be in a high degree unconvincing </s>
<s> Dr. Eugene MurrayAaron a witness of unimpeachable scientific competency describes the sting after several personal encounters with the vigorous tropical species as no worse than that of a large hornet </s>
<s> Dr. L </s>
<s> B </s>
<s> Rowland of Florida says My wife has been stung several times [by the common scorpion] </s>
<s> It is like a wasp sting only </s>
<s> THE SCORPION'S STING The Mexican scorpion enjoys an evil repute which from personal observation I consider greatly exaggerated </s>
<s> Stewart Edward White was so obliging as to afford me excellent opportunity of judging in the course of a recent hunting trip which we took together in a hot and remote Mexican desert </s>
<s> Mr. White in the process of disrobing sat down upon a brown scorpion an inch and a half long </s>
<s> The scorpion punctured Mr. White twice </s>
<s> I noted his symptoms </s>
<s> They were chiefly surprise and indignation </s>
<s> Within half an hour he was asleep and on the following day he was riding a mule </s>
<s> The scorpion however died </s>
<s> With respect to the centipede satisfactory data are difficult to obtain </s>
<s> Some scientists whose observations are worthy of note state that the legs of this curious creature secrete a poison and that their trail over human flesh is marked by a sort of rash sometimes followed by fever </s>
<s> As showing that this is not an invariable phenomenon I may set the circumstantial account given me by Captain Robert Kemp Wright who at his place at Pitch Lake Trinidad saw a goodsized centipede crawl across the forehead of his sleeping son </s>
<s> Not daring to make a move as the centipede is supposed to strike very swiftly Captain Wright was compelled to stand still while it slowly made its way to the pillow and thence to the floor where it was killed </s>
<s> The boy who had neither waked nor moved showed absolutely no trace of the reptile's course </s>
<s> THE DEADLY TARANTULAIN PRINT The only direct evidence which has come to me regarding the bite of the hundredlegged crawler was from an English naturalist whom I met in Venezuela </s>
<s> He was bitten on the ankle by a centipede nearly a foot long </s>
<s> So severe was the laceration that his sock was clotted with blood before he could get it off </s>
<s> The two punctures were marked </s>
<s> Almost immediately the ankle began to swell </s>
<s> The pain he describes as being equal to a bad toothache </s>
<s> It kept him awake all that night </s>
<s> He had some fever which however he attributes rather to the loss of sleep than to any specific action of the poison as there were no other general symptoms </s>
<s> In the morning the pain had abated a good deal and he believes that he could have gone about his pursuits had he been able to get his sock and shoe on </s>
<s> He noted some discoloration about the wound </s>
<s> Late in the afternoon he was hobbling about </s>
<s> A week in a carpet slipper was the extent of disability which he suffered </s>
<s> On these evidences it would seem just for the present to set down the scorpion and the centipede as painful rather than dangerous assailants </s>
<s> Diseased imagination could invent no creature more horrific of appearance than the tarantula </s>
<s> Its bristling and hostile aspect the swift ferocity of its rush its great size and its enthusiastic preference for combat as against flight are sufficient to account for the fear and respect in which it is generally held </s>
<s> But though several species of the huge spider are native to the United States and others frequently drop out of banana bunches from South or Central America to the discomfiture of the unsuspecting grocer no authentic instance of death from tarantula poison in this country is obtainable </s>
<s> St. Louis papers please copy particularly that one which several years ago announced in appropriately black headlines IN TWO WEEKS Three Men Have Died From Bites of Tarantulas proceeding to explain that the victims were banana handlers in the wholesale fruit district </s>
<s> No names were supplieda common phenomenon in this class of obituary notice </s>
<s> Search in the coroner's records failed to bring to light any case of the sort and an exhaustive inquiry in the fruit district was equally unproductive </s>
<s> The report was a pure fake </s>
<s> Apparently of the same nature is the news story of a Californian who presumably mistaking a tarantula for a fragrant floweret was bitten on the nose and died in great agony </s>
<s> That of course is the proper way to die under such circumstances </s>
<s> They all do itin print </s>
<s> Now let us see about the agony </s>
<s> Herbert H </s>
<s> Smith the naturalist and collector saw a man bitten on the bare foot by a tarantula Mygale so hard as to draw blood </s>
<s> There was very little swelling and the man paid no heed to the occurrence but went on with his work </s>
<s> I have talked with a Southern Pacific Railroad fireman who was jabbed on the wrist by a large tarantula </s>
<s> Some years before he had been stung on the cheek by a bald hornet </s>
<s> He wasn't inclined to make any choice between the two except that the tarantula not the wound looked a dsight more scary </s>
<s> He didn't let the bite interfere with his job even for the day </s>
<s> On the other hand Dr. MurrayAaron records serious symptoms following two bites upon the hand by a large female trapdoor tarantula pain comparable to that of the worst earache involuntary twitching of arms legs lips and tongue great swelling and discoloration of the hand and forearm and considerable suffering for four days with occasionally recurrent pains for a month </s>
<s> This however was in Haiti </s>
<s> And even there he believes death never follows tarantula bite unless the subject is in a depleted state of resistance from blooddisease or other cause </s>
<s> Under the heading Fatal Spider Bite there is a considerable and interesting newspaper bibliography </s>
<s> The details do not analyze well </s>
<s> Often the name of the supposed victim doesn't appear and where names and specifications are given the evidence is hardly sufficient as a rule to convict the insect of any crime more serious than mayhem </s>
<s> For example a young woman in Brooklyn awoke one morning to find a swollen spot on her body </s>
<s> On the bed was according to allegation a spider </s>
<s> Some ten days later she died </s>
<s> For a long period she had been in ill health </s>
<s> Yet the death was credited to the spider though specific symptoms of venomous poisoning were lacking </s>
<s> The instance of a young woman in an Eastern state is significant </s>
<s> Thrusting her foot into an old slipper she felt a sharp jab upon the point of her index digit </s>
<s> Upon hasty removal of the footgear she saw or supposed she saw a large and ferocious spider dart forth </s>
<s> This to her mind was evidence both conclusive and damning </s>
<s> Seizing upon the carving knife she promptly cut off her perfectly good toe bound up the wound and sent for the doctor thereby blossoming out in next day's print as a Heroine who had Saved her own life by her Marvelous Presence of Mind </s>
<s> The thoughtful will wonder however whether the lady wouldn't have got at the real root of the matter by cutting off her head instead of her toe </s>
<s> SPIDER HYSTERIA Imagination and terror undoubtedly account for certain general symptoms in this class of injury </s>
<s> Colonel Nicholas Pike a competent observer records a case of a man slapping his hand down upon a window sill and feeling a lively stab in the palm </s>
<s> At the same moment a small spider ran across the back of his fingers and was captured </s>
<s> There was a distinct puncture in the hand </s>
<s> Here then was a definite case where the wound and the insect were both in evidence </s>
<s> But examination of the arachnid's fangs satisfied Colonel Pike that they were far too small and weak to penetrate the tough skin where the wound was </s>
<s> Meantime the victim exhibited the classic symptoms of venomous poisoning numbness nausea chills and threatened collapse </s>
<s> A physician being summoned examined both the victim and the accused and took Colonel Pike's view that the spider was innocent </s>
<s> The man was wrathful with the indignation of terror </s>
<s> He said he guessed he knew whether he was bitten or not and that the physician's business was to eschew idle speculations and go ahead and save his life if it wasn't already too late </s>
<s> Thereupon the doctor opened up the wound and extracted a section of a fine needle </s>
<s> The other half was found sticking in the window sill where a careless seamstress had fixed it </s>
<s> The spider had been a fortuitous arrival </s>
<s> The man made one of the quickest recoveries recorded </s>
<s> THE REDSPOTDANGEROUS Strangely enough the one really dangerous spider on the American continent is small obscure and practically unknown to popular or journalistic hysteria </s>
<s> Latrodectus mactans is its scientific name </s>
<s> It is about the size of a large pea black with a red spot on the backa useful danger signaland spins a small web in outhouses or around woodpiles </s>
<s> So far as is known its poison is the most virulent and powerful drop for drop secreted by any living creature </s>
<s> Cobra virus in the minute quantity which the Latrodectus's glands contain would probably have no appreciable effect upon man whereas the tiny spider's venom in the volume injected by the cobra's stroke would slay a herd of elephants </s>
<s> Were this littleknown crawler as large as the common black hunting spider of our gardens and lawns its bite would be almost invariably fatal </s>
<s> Happily the redspot's fangs being small and weak can with difficulty penetrate the skin and are able to inject venom in dangerous quantity only when the bite is inflicted upon some tenderskinned portion of the body </s>
<s> Nevertheless fatalities consequent upon the bite of this insect are sufficiently well attested to take rank as established scientific facts </s>
<s> One of the most detailed comes from an intelligent farmer of Greensboro North Carolina </s>
<s> A workman in his employ while hauling wood brushed at something crawling upon his neck and felt a sharp stinging sensation </s>
<s> He found a small black spider with a red spot </s>
<s> This was at 8.30 A.M. Presently ten small white pimples appeared about the bitten spot though no puncture was visible and there was no swelling </s>
<s> The pain soon passed but returned in three hours and became general finally settling in the abdomen and producing violent cramps </s>
<s> At one o'clock the man had a spasmodic attack </s>
<s> Two hours later he had so far recovered as to be able to go back to work for an hour </s>
<s> Then the spasms took him again he sank into coma and died between ten and eleven o'clock that evening about fourteen hours after the bite </s>
<s> At no time were there local symptoms or swelling other than the slight eruption but the neck left arm and breast are reported as having assumed a stonelike hardness </s>
<s> The same farmer had seen three years previous a negro who had been bitten upon the ankle by a redspot and who suffered from diminishingly severe spasmodic attacks for three weeks </s>
<s> The white pimples appeared in this case also </s>
<s> The negro recovered but the eruption reappeared for years thereafter whenever he was overheated </s>
<s> Recoveries from Latrodectus bite are much more common in the records than deaths </s>
<s> Dr. Corson of Savannah Georgia reports six cases characterized by agonizing pains spasmodic contractions like those of tetanus and grave general symptoms </s>
<s> All recovered </s>
<s> From Anaheim California a fatal case is reported by Dr. Bickford death occurring twenty hours after the bite </s>
<s> William A </s>
<s> Ball of San Bernardino California gives a vivid account of his sensations after being bitten on the groin by a redspotted spider the data being attested by his physician </s>
<s> Shortly after being bitten he began to suffer great agony with convulsive contractions of the muscles </s>
<s> The pains in my hipjoints chest and thighs grew rapidly more violent until it seemed that the bones in these parts of my body were being crushed to fragments </s>
<s> He was seriously ill for ten days </s>
<s> WORSE TEXAN THE DEADLY COPPERHEAD It may be that only under certain uncomprehended conditions is the venom of the Latrodectus effective </s>
<s> Inoculation of guinea pigs with the poison has been without any resultant symptoms </s>
<s> Scientific experimenters have suffered themselves to be bitten and have experienced no ill effects </s>
<s> The foreign cousins of the American species however have as evil a repute as the mactans </s>
<s> The katipo found in sedges on the beach of New Zealand is dreaded by the Maoris who traditionally refuse to sleep nearer than half a stone's throw from the water that being the extent of range of the spider </s>
<s> The Latrodecti of Corsica Algeria and France are infamous in the lore of the country folk which fact must be regarded as strongly evidential when their insignificant appearance is taken into account </s>
<s> Only in America is there no popular fear of this really formidable little creature </s>
<s> Yet it is found in almost every part of the United States though by no means one of the commoner spiders </s>
<s> In the past five years I have seen two specimens at my country place in central New York and have heard of a dozen others </s>
<s> If people understood generally that this rather ornamental insect is both more perilous to life and health and rather more prone to attack human beings than the superstitiously dreaded deadly copperhead there would probably be a heavy mortality in the Latrodectus family at the hands of energetic housecleaners </s>
<s> THE RISE OF THE KISSINGBUG Years ago the United States Bureau of Entomology received from an exasperated clergyman in Georgia a dead insect enclosed in this note Prof </s>
<s> Riley What is this devil </s>
<s> He sailed down on my hedge </s>
<s> I took hold of his lone front leg and as quick as lightning he speared me under my thumb nail and I dropped him </s>
<s> My thumb and whole arm are still paining me . . . The miscreant was a fine specimen of Reduvius personatus the conenosed bloodsucker soon thereafter to achieve heights of newspaper notoriety together with its cousin Melanolestes picipes as the kissingbug </s>
<s> How many persons died in type from kissingbug bites in the year of enlightened civilization 1899 will never be known </s>
<s> But from far and near from California and Connecticut and the Carolinas from Minnesota and Maryland and Maine came startling reports of this hitherto unfamed creature's depredations upon the human countenance </s>
<s> Thereby the spider family was relieved of much unmerited odium for it is more than suspected by entomologists that a large proportion of socalled spider bites are really the work of the more vicious but less formidableappearing kissingbug as is often evidenced by the nature of the puncture </s>
<s> The kissingbug is about half an inch in length flatbacked shaped in geometrically regular angles and armed with a large hard beak </s>
<s> It is this beak which does the damage for the kissingbug is a fighter and will risk a prod at anything that gives it cause of offense </s>
<s> Testimony is not lacking that it sometimes punctures the human epidermis with a view to obtaining blood at first hand instead of from its natural prey </s>
<s> But the curious feature of the kissingbug's bite is its after effect </s>
<s> Neither the southern Reduvius nor the northern Melanolestes possesses any venom apparatus </s>
<s> Now an insect without fangs or sting duct and poison gland can no more envenom the object of its attack than a fish can kick a man to death </s>
<s> Yet we find such authorities as Dr. L </s>
<s> O </s>
<s> Howard the United States Entomologist Professor Le Conte Mr. Charles Drury of Cincinnati and others including a mass of medical witnesses declaring from firsthand observation that the kissingbug bite causes much swelling and severe pain </s>
<s> Le Conte indeed compares the effect to snake bite and states that people are seriously affected for a week </s>
<s> A case is recorded from Holland South Carolina where there were vomiting and marked weakness </s>
<s> Mr. Schwartz an expert of the Bureau of Entomology at Washington was bitten twice upon the hand and testifies to the painful effects </s>
<s> In 1899 when the species was very common in Washington the Emergency Hospital had a long list of patients who appeared on the records under the heading Insect Bite </s>
<s> THE DECLINE OF THE KISSINGBUG Thus was started the general scare a reporter with a keen nose for news having made a legitimate sensation from the repeated entries on the hospital roster </s>
<s> From Washington it spread over the country and became the topic of the day until any insect bite or stingmosquito hornet bedbug or whatnotwas magnified by the hysteria of the patient and the credulousness of the public into a dangerous instance of kissingbug poisoning </s>
<s> Reports of fatal cases however invariably proved to be canards </s>
<s> For explanation of the marked local symptoms resultant upon attack by the insect science has been hard put to it </s>
<s> The general symptoms observed in a few cases where violent may probably be ascribed to shock and nervousness </s>
<s> But the marked swelling and pain cannot be thus dismissed </s>
<s> Medical men believe that the insect in its various prowlings for food thrusts its exploring beak into decaying animal and vegetable matter and thus in a sense so poisons it that when it comes into contact with human blood a rapid local infection is set upnot through any specific poison as in spider bite or bee sting but by the agency of the putrefactive germs collected on the weapon </s>
<s> Not the least interesting phase of the kissingbug scare is the rapidity and completeness of its decadence </s>
<s> It is but ten years ago that the newspapers rang with it that victims of the bite in every city were fleeing whitefaced and racked with forebodings to doctor or hospital </s>
<s> Today both the Melanolestes and the conenose are abroad in the land </s>
<s> Doubtless upon provocation they are spearing others as they speared the outraged clergyman </s>
<s> But that's all </s>
<s> The bepunctured ones do not seek the consolations of medical or journalistic attention </s>
<s> They put a little wet mud or peroxide on the place and let it go at that </s>
<s> Exit another bogy </s>
<s> OUR REAL POISON PERIL One venomous creature there is in this country which may justly be termed a public peril in the widest sense </s>
<s> Proportionately to population more victims fall to it yearly in the United States than to the dreaded cobra in India </s>
<s> Some twelve thousand Americans are killed every year by its bite </s>
<s> Three hundred thousand more are made seriously ill from the after effects </s>
<s> Unfortunately the virus works so slowly that alarm is stilled </s>
<s> The victims do not sicken at once </s>
<s> The bite is forgotten but ten days or two weeks after the subject falls into a fever </s>
<s> His blood is poisoned within him </s>
<s> Eventually in extreme cases he becomes delirious succumbs to a stupor and dies </s>
<s> Yet because there is nothing horrific to the sensationloving imagination in the malariabearing mosquito public inertia or ignorance tolerates it with a grin and permits it to breed in city and country alike throughout the length and breadth of the nation </s>
<s> Compared with it as a real menace all the combined brood of snakes scorpions centipedes tarantulas and other pet bugaboos of our childish romanticism are utterly negligible are as figment to reality as shadow to substance </s>
<s> It is perhaps characteristic of our wryly humorous American temperament that we should have invested the unimportant danger with all the shuddering attributes of horror and have made of the real peril a joke to be perennially hailed with laughter in a thousand thoughtless prints </s>
<s> Vol. XXIII October 1910 No </s>
<s> 4 Lassoing Wild Animals In Africa pages 526538 By GUY H </s>
<s> SCULL Field Manager of the Buffalo Jones African Expedition II SOMEHOW everything seemed to happen on moving day with the Buffalo Jones Expedition in East Africa </s>
<s> Exactly why this should have been it is impossible to tell </s>
<s> Perhaps the reason may be found in the fact that a considerable part of our time was occupied in moving </s>
<s> No doubt the circumstance could be traced to some such perfectly reasonable cause </s>
<s> But we chose to look upon it otherwise </s>
<s> When an outfit like ours has been working for a while in the open countryespecially when the undertaking has no precedent and the outcome is decidedly uncertainthe little happenings of each day gradually grow to have a peculiar significance of their own and finally a brandnew set of superstitions is formed and half jokingly believed in by every one concerned </s>
<s> In this way an expedition comes to be regarded as lucky or unlucky or lucky on certain days or at certain hours of the day or at certain periods of the moon </s>
<s> The wide reaches of the African veldt have something to do with it perhaps </s>
<s> These superstitions are temporary local and often purely personal affairs </s>
<s> Means being a cowboy believed that when he rode his bigboned bay the drive would be successful </s>
<s> The native dogboy insisted that when the longeared bloodhound and the little white terrier were coupled together on the march the rest of the pack would come through without mishap </s>
<s> Loveless swore by a particular piece of rope and Macwhich is short for Mohammeddiscovered propitious omens on every conceivable occasion </s>
<s> It was on the first day's march into the Kedong Valley that we had roped the warthog </s>
<s> On the journey from Sewell's Farm to Rugged Rocks we had rounded up and photographed the eland </s>
<s> Again it was on the trek of March 8 to the Wangai River that we had caught our only glimpses of rhinoceros and lionfaint chances of making a capture but still chances and better than no signs at all </s>
<s> And thus merely because it had turned out so in the past every member of the expedition had come to entertain a semiserious belief that something momentous was bound to happen on moving day </s>
<s> A general feeling of expectancy pervaded the entire safari when we broke camp at the Wangai River at dawn of a hazy morning </s>
<s> The sky was clear of clouds but behind the hills of the Mau escarpment a veldt fire had been burning for several days so that a veil of smoke was seen hanging in the air as the dawn broadened into day </s>
<s> The smell of the burning veldt and the nearness of the fire lent an oppressive warmth to the still morning </s>
<s> You two boys had better carry your heavy ropes the Colonel said at starting </s>
<s> We might meet something </s>
<s> We had finished with the Kedong and Rift valleys </s>
<s> We had hunted every corner of the district within striking distance of the water </s>
<s> And we had had success of a kind </s>
<s> Cheetah eland hartebeest and servalcat we had roped and tied and photographed </s>
<s> But the really big game had so far escaped us </s>
<s> For this reason we had decided to take the road over the Mau where the smoke haze hung heavy and so on into the Sotik country where both lion and rhino were said to abound </s>
<s> For the first ten miles of the march our way led across untraveled country toward the two deep ruts in the veldt that were known as the wagon road </s>
<s> We had an extra oxwagon with us now in charge of Mr. Curry an Africander who lived with his partner on a farm on the border of the Sotik and who on his return journey home with his wagon had agreed to help us carry supplies </s>
<s> Curry was slight and roundshouldered with light yellow hair </s>
<s> His face was burned a bright red excepting his nose which was white where the skin was peeling </s>
<s> He had a peculiar slow drawling way of talkingwhen he talked at all which was seldom </s>
<s> Being an inhabitant of the district into which we were going he was naturally subjected at first to a number of questions in regard to the big game there </s>
<s> Plenty of rhino in your part of the world I suppose </s>
<s> Yas drawled Curry </s>
<s> And lion too I imagine </s>
<s> Yas </s>
<s> Ought to get some giraffe on the way hadn't we </s>
<s> Yas </s>
<s> Rhino pretty scarce just now though aren't they </s>
<s> Yas Curry answered placidly </s>
<s> Thus it soon became apparent that Curry's chief ambition was to agree pleasantly with whatever anybody said which tended to discredit any information he had to impart </s>
<s> So as a matter of course the questions ceased and when no more were asked him Curry's conversation ceased also </s>
<s> It was rough going for the oxwagons those first ten miles and they made slow time of it along the base of the hills </s>
<s> According to our custom on the march the Colonel and the two cowboys the picture department composed of Kearton and Gobbet and Ulyate the white hunter and myself rode in a widely extended line in front of the safari sweeping the country for game </s>
<s> It was hot at the base of the hillsso hot that when your bridle hand dropped inadvertently to the pommel of the saddle the brass mounting there seemed to burn you </s>
<s> Not a breath of air was stirring and the sun shone down blazing through the wisps of smoke haze and the heat waves rose from the dead parched veldt so that the distant southern volcano looked all quivering </s>
<s> Then from out the blurred vista in front little by little a clump of comparatively large trees began to take definite shape </s>
<s> Another half mile farther and we saw that something was moving among the trees as high up as the topmost branches </s>
<s> Giraffe said Ulyate and no sooner had he spoken the word than the great towering animals wheeled and fled from their shelter with that longlegged gallop of theirs which looks so easy and slow but which carries them over the ground as fast as a speedy horse can run </s>
<s> The Colonel and the two cowboys set off at a hand gallop in a vain attempt to round them up and drive them back to the cameras </s>
<s> The race was a hopeless one for the horsemen from the start </s>
<s> But according to the general method of operations adopted by the Colonel from the very beginning no chance of a capture however slim it might appear was to remain untried so long as men and horses could endure </s>
<s> The two ruts of the wagon road led close by the grove of trees and when the rest of us reached this spot and dismounted to await results the three leading horsemen had disappeared long ago into the scrubgrown country to the south </s>
<s> As noon approached the heat became more and more oppressive </s>
<s> The cameras had been screwed to the tripods and covered with our coats to protect them from the sun </s>
<s> The horses grazed near by </s>
<s> Mac was sent up one of the trees to warn us of the approach of anything like a giraffe and the rest of us sat on the ground round the bole in the small circle of thin shade and lazily watched the black ants always crawling and climbing and zigzagging back and forth over the network of fallen twigs and leaves </s>
<s> It was too hot to talkit was too hot to sleep or think </s>
<s> And by and by the oxwagons came up and the oxen brought the flies </s>
<s> For a time then the only sounds were the slow crunching of the feeding horses and an occasional inarticulate snarl from some one or other who foolishly tried to brush the flies away from his face </s>
<s> Eventually after a long time had passed Means rode into the grove of trees unheralded by Mac and alone </s>
<s> The bay horse had fallen badly wrenching his rider's back where once he had been hurt before </s>
<s> Means took his saddle off threw it on the ground and sat on it </s>
<s> He dropped into a pig hole he explained an' hopped out again as neat as could be </s>
<s> But in hoppin' out he hopped into another an' that just naturally discouraged him an' he come down with me </s>
<s> No comments were made nor did Means expect any </s>
<s> But evidently he had considered it only justice to the bay that the mishap should receive from him the proper explanation </s>
<s> Then Loveless returned also alone </s>
<s> He made a few grumbling remarks about its being all nonsense to run the horses to death when there was no chance at all </s>
<s> But as his listeners showed not the slightest interest in the matter he too relapsed into silence </s>
<s> The Colonel was the last to come in </s>
<s> He rode straight to the tree where the company were gathered dismounted and sat down </s>
<s> Then he spoke to the world at large </s>
<s> They must be about here somewhere he said </s>
<s> And being about here somewhere we'll get 'em yet </s>
<s> When the shadow beneath the tree began to lengthen toward the east the safari shook itself together and prepared to move on once more </s>
<s> But this time instead of occupying his customary position at the head of the column the Colonel lagged behind </s>
<s> Immediately after leaving the grove of trees the road commenced to climb the first rises of the Mau escarpment </s>
<s> As we mounted higher up the hillside the view behind us opened out into a grand panorama of the two valleys and their sentinel volcanoes with the smoke haze hanging over all </s>
<s> For a time those of us who were in front rode half sideways in the saddle looking back over the way we had come and over the district we had grown to know so well </s>
<s> Then we crossed a small level park that formed the crest of the first hill and as we moved down the western slope the view behind us disappeared and the new country spread before us </s>
<s> Kearton was riding with his head sunk on his chest like a sick man </s>
<s> Gobbet asked if anything was wrong with him </s>
<s> Nothing bad too much heat this morning likely </s>
<s> Want to hunt a bit of shade and lie up awhile </s>
<s> No I'll go on </s>
<s> Gobbet shrugged his shoulders </s>
<s> You're the judge he said </s>
<s> Hill after hill stretched away in front to the one upstanding kopje that marked the top of the Mau </s>
<s> The district was wooded with small twisted trees and the fire had crossed here so that the ground was black and the air smelled stronger of burning </s>
<s> Presently Means stopped </s>
<s> I'd better wait till the Colonel comes along he explained </s>
<s> The Colonel don't carry any weapons </s>
<s> Loveless stopped with him and as Ulyate was somewhere behind with the oxwagons and porters this left Kearton Gobbet and myself to ride on by ourselves </s>
<s> For a mile or more the road lifted and dipped with monotonous regularity and the burnt land was still on either hand without a sign of life anywhere to be seen </s>
<s> So when the sun really began to decline toward the west Gobbet who had once been assistant manager of the Alhambra Music Hall in Brighton told the story of Harry Lauder and the liquid air biscuits and it seemed to do Kearton good </s>
<s> Kearton had just told Gobbet to quit his lying when all three of us realized that for the last half minute we had been unconsciously listening to the beat of a galloping horse on the road behind </s>
<s> The next instant Ulyate pulled up in a cloud of dust </s>
<s> Colonel wants you he said </s>
<s> They've rounded up a giraffe </s>
<s> We wheeled the horses and started back on the run </s>
<s> Aboutthreemiles </s>
<s> Leftof theroad </s>
<s> Ulyate shouted after us </s>
<s> There were various reasons that called for haste </s>
<s> How long the ropers could keep the giraffe rounded up was especially uncertain and then besides it was near the end of the day and soon the light would be too far gone for a picture </s>
<s> We met the line of porters and they scattered right and left </s>
<s> Farther on the oxteams crowded one side to give us room </s>
<s> Then we came upon the four special porters with the cameras </s>
<s> Kearton took his machine on the saddle with him and Gobbet caught up the tripod from another pair of outstretched arms </s>
<s> When we reached the bit of clearing and looked to the left of the road we saw the long neck and head of a giraffe sharply outlined against the sky </s>
<s> The giraffe stood motionless </s>
<s> His feet were spread a little apart as though he was prepared to dash away again at the first opportunity and he gazed in a curious way first at one then at another of the three ropers that surrounded him and now sat their horses waiting </s>
<s> There was still enough light left for a picture but Kearton was nearly done </s>
<s> Give him a minute's breather said the Colonel </s>
<s> We'll hold the critter till he's ready </s>
<s> We took Kearton off his horse and stretched him on the ground and poured the lukewarm water from a canteen on his head </s>
<s> Meanwhile Cobbet screwed the camera to the tripod and set it up </s>
<s> By the time Gobbet had finished Kearton was on his feet again </s>
<s> From his position near by Means ventured the opinion that it was too much excitement that had knocked him over and Kearton swore back at him pleasantly and went to work </s>
<s> A highpitched yell from the Colonel sent the giraffe away across the open with that clumsylooking powerful gallop that is all his own and with his long neck plunging slowly back and forth </s>
<s> Loveless's black one of the fastest horses in the string had hard work to gain on the giraffe expecially as the animal swerved quickly at the last moment and fled down the eastern slope of the hill through the scrub where the going was none too good </s>
<s> It was a difficult throwand a new one for a Western cowboyto send the noose so far up into the air over the head perched high on the long swaying neck </s>
<s> But at the first attempt Loveless succeeded and then reined in gently so as not to throw the beast because a giraffe would fall heavily and would very likely break his neck or a leg if tumbled over </s>
<s> Finally he was brought to a standstill his feet spread apart as before and for a while the two stood facing each otherthe cowboy and the towering giraffe with the rope from the saddle horn leading up at a considerable angle to the shoulders of the prize </s>
<s> The rest of the hunt soon gathered about them </s>
<s> Although the light was rapidly failing Kearton finished what was left of his roll of film </s>
<s> The whir of the camera ended with a peculiar flapping sound </s>
<s> That's all said Kearton and sank down on a nearby stone </s>
<s> But Loveless and the giraffe continued to face each other undisturbed </s>
<s> Well </s>
<s> said Loveless presently </s>
<s> Well </s>
<s> echoed the Colonel </s>
<s> Well how are we going to take this rope off him </s>
<s> We've got none to spare you know </s>
<s> Get a ladder suggested Means </s>
<s> No we won't need a ladder said the Colonel seriously but we'll have to throw him after all </s>
<s> We can do it gently I guess without hurting him </s>
<s> Accordingly Means roped the giraffe by one hind leg and pulled it out from under him so that he sank easily to the ground and both the ropes were loosened and freed </s>
<s> The sun had set and the short twilight was rapidly deepening </s>
<s> The oxwagons and porters were several miles ahead </s>
<s> So we packed up the camera coiled up the ropes mounted and rode away and the giraffe raised himself on his haunches among the bushes and watched us go </s>
<s> We camped at a water hole that night and started on again the next morning in the darkness before the dawn with a porter ahead carrying a lantern to show the way </s>
<s> With oxwagons it is a three days' journey from that water hole to the Guas Nyiro River at the border of the Sotik </s>
<s> The country through which we passed continued to be the same as that of the Mau escarpmenta succession of low hills and shallow valleys covered with the small twisted trees </s>
<s> And there was plenty of water on the way </s>
<s> But there was no game in the district </s>
<s> We had been told before starting that we need not expect to see anything on the way because antelope zebra and such like animals avoid the wooded section so as not to be caught unaware by lions and since the prey seek the safety of the open plains the lions are compelled to follow </s>
<s> In spite of this fact and although the dense woods and broken ground generally forced the safari to keep to the road the cowboys were always ready and the cameras always loaded with film </s>
<s> But the land on either side remained silent and deserted </s>
<s> And each day's journey was the same as the one before the start in the gray of the morning the long hot ride with the road gently rising and falling over the hills and the sudden cool of the evening when the sun went down </s>
<s> At times the camera department would take moving pictures of the wagons and porters crossing a river where an especially picturesque bit of scenery offered an attractive setting </s>
<s> Occasionally Means as he rode along would commence singing one of the songs of our Western plains verse after verse seemingly without end recounting in detail some local historical event such as an Indian attack on an army post a shooting affair at a dance or a trainrobber's hanging </s>
<s> He would sing more to himself than to anybody else and if this began to bore him at all he would stop in the middle and leave the story untold </s>
<s> Then sometimes when we outspanned for an hour at noon the four special camera porters would give imitations of Kearton and Gobbet taking pictures of Loveless shoeing horses or of Means in the act of roping </s>
<s> And in the evenings when the day's march was done and the outpost fires had been lighted the talk of the company would turn to our chances of finding luck in the Sotik country that lay ahead </s>
<s> In the afternoon of March 16 we reached Webb's Farm in the Guas Nyiro valley which lies at the edge of the big plains </s>
<s> In this neighborhood there were three farmsWebb's Curry's and Agate'sand on the evening of our arrival some of their men paid a visit to the camp </s>
<s> They had heard of the expedition and each in turn examined the horses the dogs the ropes and the saddles and then like the hunters at Nairobi asked the inevitable question But how are you going to do it </s>
<s> Oh we'll do it somehow the Colonel replied goodnaturedly </s>
<s> And the visitors shook their heads a little and smiled and changed the subject </s>
<s> But to attempt to rope a rhinoceros or a lion required fresh horses and ever since we had left Nairobi nearly a fortnight ago we had worked our horses hard every day </s>
<s> Now that we had reached the land of the big game the Colonel for the first time called a day of rest </s>
<s> So we loafed about camp from sunrise to sunset and by evening were heartily sick of it all </s>
<s> Perhaps we had expected too much of this Sotik country perhaps the expedition was running temporarily in a streak of bad luck but the fact remains that when we resumed hunting on March 18 disappointment only followed disappointment </s>
<s> As we had done in the Rift Valley so here we adopted the method of sweeping the country with a widely extended line </s>
<s> The first day we rode far to the southward to the Hot Springs and back and found nothing and an unreasoning depression settled upon the expedition </s>
<s> The next day we rode still farther to the westward this time and again found nothing and so the depression deepened </s>
<s> Also on the afternoon of this day it rained heavily and Curry agreed with Ulyate that this probably meant the beginning of the rainy season which was already overdue </s>
<s> That night at the supper table the Colonel spoke his mind </s>
<s> The rain was dripping through the canvas fly overhead and the Colonel wore his broadbrimmed hat to help keep the water off his plate </s>
<s> There's no use hanging round here any longer he said not a bit of use </s>
<s> We haven't seen anything nor a sign of anything </s>
<s> When the rains begin in earnest this ground will soften fast an' the horses will get bogged an' we'll have to quit </s>
<s> So from now on we've got to work fast </s>
<s> Now Ulyate says there's water about twelve miles from here to the northcalled the Soda Swamp </s>
<s> We'll start for the Soda Swamp in the morning </s>
<s> Again it was moving day </s>
<s> The morning dawned fine after the rain and the air was clear and the country looked greener and fresher than it had ever looked before </s>
<s> By the time the sun rose the first wagon was packed so the safari set out on the journey leaving the second wagon to load and follow our tracks for there was no road to the Soda Swamp </s>
<s> At the last moment the Colonel decided that he and the cowboys might just as well make a circuit to the westward of the line of march on the off chance of finding game </s>
<s> We covered that district pretty thoroughly yesterday he said </s>
<s> But still you never can tell </s>
<s> Yet nobody thought it worth while for the camera department to go with them and so Kearton and Gobbet and the four special porters trailed along with the slow plodding wagon </s>
<s> In the first place the wagons would follow the shortest route and the horses would be none the worse for an easy day in the second if by the remotest chance the Colonel flushed anything worth while he could more easily find the cameras </s>
<s> Curry had remained behind to bring on the second load and soon Ulyate left us to make a detour past Agate's farm to procure another sack of rice that was badly needed </s>
<s> Ours was a large safari and the details of transportation required close attention </s>
<s> The morning wore on </s>
<s> The sky remained clear and the heat became intense </s>
<s> The direction in which we were traveling led us along the border of the plains through small green parks scattered groves of trees and scrub </s>
<s> So far as the mounted men were concerned the march was a succession of rides and halts </s>
<s> The heavily laden oxwagon traveled slowly and it soon became our custom to dismount in a bit of shade and let the wagon pass ahead about a mile when we would mount again and catch up with it and then repeat the process </s>
<s> At one of these places there was a grassgrown mound against which we sat leaning comfortably and speculated on the distance we had come and the distance we had to go </s>
<s> When after a while it became evident that we should never agree in the matter the conversation altered to a sort of spasmodic affair </s>
<s> I thought this district was so full of big game that you couldn't sleep at night for the lions roaring around you Gobbet remarked lazily </s>
<s> Wait till you get among them said Kearton </s>
<s> Sais keep that horse farther away he'll be walking on us next </s>
<s> Well I haven't been kept awake any yet Gobbet replied </s>
<s> I wonder where that wagon's got to and Kearton raised himself on one elbow and peered ahead from beneath the downtilted brim of his helmet </s>
<s> Then he lay back again and shut his eyes </s>
<s> Means is coming he said </s>
<s> The announcement occasioned no surprise </s>
<s> Undoubtedly Means had some reason for returning over the trail and when he reached the mound we should probably learn what he wanted </s>
<s> Means dismounted and sat down beside us </s>
<s> We've found a rhino over in the next valley yonder he remarked and nodded his head toward the west </s>
<s> A rhino is no matter to joke about said Gobbet </s>
<s> Please remember that in future </s>
<s> I'm not jokin' said Means </s>
<s> Colonel's watchin' him </s>
<s> Loveless stopped halfway here about three miles off </s>
<s> Colonel sent me to bring the rest of you and get the heavy rope </s>
<s> Is that right Means </s>
<s> Kearton asked sharply </s>
<s> Sure </s>
<s> Come on then </s>
<s> In five minutes we had overtaken the wagon and stopped it and while Means clambered up on to the load to hunt for the heavy rope Kearton collected the camera porters and started ahead with them in the direction Means pointed out </s>
<s> But Means could not find the rope he wanted </s>
<s> He threw off half the load without success </s>
<s> It's on the other wagon </s>
<s> There's where it is he finally concluded </s>
<s> No time to wait now </s>
<s> Other wagon likely hasn't started yet </s>
<s> We'll have to do with what we've got </s>
<s> We rode on at an easy jog to keep the horses fresh and at the end of half an hour we came upon Loveless waiting for us just beneath the crest of a rise </s>
<s> He had offsaddled his horse and had turned him loose to graze a bit before the coming work and a few minutes were occupied while Loveless saddled up again and Kearton and Gobbet adjusted their cameras and took them on their horses </s>
<s> Finally every one was ready and we set forth once more on a wide detour to the north to approach the beast from down the wind </s>
<s> Loveless gave us the latest news The Colonel came over the rise a half hour ago and said the rhino was laying down resting quiet </s>
<s> The Colonel went back again at once to keep watch </s>
<s> As we proceeded farther on the circuit and began to ride down the gentle slope into the adjacent valley we slowed down the pace to a cautious walk </s>
<s> No one spoke and on the grass of the veldt the tread of the horses made scarcely any sound </s>
<s> Suddenly the Colonel appeared walking toward us bent low </s>
<s> He had backed out o' his hidingplace behind a clump of scrub </s>
<s> He's laying down over there about a hundred yards away he whispered </s>
<s> Now we want to catch the start of the show </s>
<s> You boys ready </s>
<s> Means tightened his cinch and shook his rope loose and coiled it up again </s>
<s> Loveless said he was ready </s>
<s> One of the saises produced the Colonel's horse from behind another clump of scrub and Kearton dismounted and began creeping forward with his camera </s>
<s> Don't start him up till I get my position he cautioned </s>
<s> I'll wave my hand </s>
<s> On account of the growth of low bushes we could not see the rhino but in silence we watched Kearton tiptoeing farther and farther ahead toward the spot where the Colonel had said the beast was lying down </s>
<s> The time was approximately a little after noon </s>
<s> The wind that was blowing was light and same to us hot over the sunny reaches of veldt </s>
<s> The sky was cloudless </s>
<s> Then the three ropers commenced maneuvering forward swinging out a little to the right </s>
<s> Kearton stopped </s>
<s> He set up his camera and sighted it and took out his handkerchief and carefully wiped the lens </s>
<s> When Kearton waved his hand the Colonel's yell shattered the stillness and the great beast heaved up out of the grass and tossed his head and sniffed the air and snorted </s>
<s> The horsemen rode full tilt at him and with surprising quickness the rhino wheeled and broke away south down the valley </s>
<s> For a good three miles the rhino ran straight and fast </s>
<s> Finally he came into more open country which was dotted here and therewith small thorn trees </s>
<s> Here also in one place there was a fairsized pool of water left over from the rains of the night before </s>
<s> The rhino selected this pool as a good position from which to act on the defensive </s>
<s> He splashed into the water stopped and faced the horsemen </s>
<s> Then followed a few minutes' respite for all concerned </s>
<s> The horses were panting heavily after the sharp run and the rhino's position in the pool rendered it difficult to approach him for a chance to throw a rope </s>
<s> Evidently considering himself safe for the moment the beast rolled once or twice in the water and then stood on guard as before but with his black sides dripping </s>
<s> We've got to get him out of that said the Colonel </s>
<s> A horse wouldn't stand a show there </s>
<s> Now when I get him to charge me you boys stand by </s>
<s> Before the Colonel finished speaking he was already edging toward the pool </s>
<s> For fifteen yards the rhino watched him coming </s>
<s> Then with a great snort he charged out of the water sending the white spray flying in every direction and the Colonel had to ride hard to keep ahead of the tossing horn </s>
<s> But Means was after the rhino like a flash and with a quick throw caught him round the neck </s>
<s> The big bay fell back on his haunches and the rope snapped like twine </s>
<s> We'll miss that heavy rope today Means said </s>
<s> We'll tie him up with what we've got the Colonel replied </s>
<s> Only we've got to tire him out some first </s>
<s> What we'll do is to make him charge us one after the other so he'll run three times to the horses' running once </s>
<s> It was a full half hour before the next attempt was made to throw a rope </s>
<s> Time after time the rhino came plunging out of the water to charge the nearest horseman </s>
<s> Our Western horses proved to be only just a trifle faster than the rhino so that each time the beast nearly caught them </s>
<s> Besides here and there the ground was bad with antbear holes which had to be avoided for a fall would mean disaster </s>
<s> But little by little it became apparent that the rhino's continual charging was beginning to produce an effect </s>
<s> In the meanwhile the rest of the chase was coming up </s>
<s> In the distance we could see them hurrying down the valleyhorsemen and porters considerably scattered as if each one followed a route of his own choosing Kearton led on his big chestnut </s>
<s> He was carrying the heavy camera under his arm the tripod over his shoulder </s>
<s> The reins were hanging loose over his saddle horn his heels were thumping the horse's sides and the perspiration was streaming down his face </s>
<s> We lost you he panted </s>
<s> How's it going </s>
<s> What a picture </s>
<s> Mac the Mohammedan and Aro the Masai warrior took the apparatus from him and he dismounted and went to work </s>
<s> At the second attempt to rope the beast Loveless caught him by one hind leg and the rhino decided to shift his base of operations to an anthill in the neighboring clearing </s>
<s> His mode of progression was to walk on three legs and to drag the black horse after him with the other </s>
<s> He reached the anthill and demolished it and paused for a breathing spell </s>
<s> The chase followed after and Kearton went into action on the north and Gobbet on the south near a small thorn tree with a negro porter beside him </s>
<s> The rhino caught sight of Gobbet's camera and charged </s>
<s> The porter went up the tree like a flash </s>
<s> Gobbet was bent over looking through his viewfinder which of course gave him no idea of how fast the beast was bearing down on him nor how close he had already come </s>
<s> Look out </s>
<s> yelled the Colonel </s>
<s> Gobbet glanced up over the top of the camera and made a jump for the tree </s>
<s> But the porter was already in the branches and the tree was so small there was not room for two and Gobbet had to run for it </s>
<s> The next second with a powerful upward stroke of his horn the rhino sent the apparatus flying </s>
<s> Then Means succeeded in attracting his attention and he charged the horseman instead </s>
<s> Gobbet picked up the debris found that the tripodhead was split clean in two as with an axe found the camera itself undamaged found there was enough head left to support the camera quickly mounted his machine again and was just in time to catch the end of the rhino's chase after Means </s>
<s> And all the while Kearton had his camera trained upon the scene in which his assistant was playing the conspicuous part </s>
<s> I hope I got that good he said it'll make fine actionfine </s>
<s> From one position to another from anthill to thorn tree and back to anthill once more the fight went on through the long hot afternoon </s>
<s> Ropes were thrown and caught and broken mended and thrown again </s>
<s> The horses were pulled all standing one way and another </s>
<s> Rolls of film were exposed and replaced by fresh ones </s>
<s> The rhino sulked and stormed and charged in turn </s>
<s> At the end of the fourth hour Loveless had one short length of light line left </s>
<s> The rest of the ropes were dangling broken from the rhino's legs and neck as he stood at bay over the ruins of the anthill </s>
<s> The sun was rapidly canting toward the west </s>
<s> The continual work in the intense heat without food or water was beginning to tell on both horses and men </s>
<s> The rhino was weakening faster </s>
<s> But only one hour of daylight remained and if the beast could hold out till dark we should lose him </s>
<s> There was the dead stump of a tree with the roots protruding lying in the grass near by </s>
<s> The Colonel told Means to fasten the stump to the last piece of line and Loveless rode toward Kearton's machine past the rhino dragging the stump behind him </s>
<s> As the Colonel had foreseen the beast charged at the stump and the loose ropes hanging from him became entangled in the roots </s>
<s> So on they went at a run first Loveless then the stump bounding over the ground then the charging rhino headed straight for Kearton's camera </s>
<s> The Masai warrior stood by the tripod with his long spear poised high and Kearton turned the handle and shouted at Loveless How many times have I got to tell you not to come straight into the lens </s>
<s> Bring him on at an angle </s>
<s> . . . I don't want to be unreasonable he added when the rhino stopped but you ought to have learned better by this time </s>
<s> Then by hauling in gently Loveless succeeded in recovering two of the ropes and they were pieced together and thrown again catching the rhino by one hind leg </s>
<s> Both the cowboys put their horses to work pulling forward on the rope and they lifted that one hind leg ahead </s>
<s> The tired beast shifted his great body after it and thus step by step the horses dragged him up to a tree where Loveless passed the end of the rope two turns around the bole and made it fast </s>
<s> The rhino charged once just before the knot was tied and Loveless had to jump into the branches through the thorns to escape </s>
<s> He charged again rather feebly this time trying to get free but the rope held well and tripped him up </s>
<s> After that he stood quietly at the end of his tether watching the camera in a sullen way while Kearton took his picture with the last few feet of film </s>
<s> By this time the light was almost gone the films were finished horses and men were nearly done and besides it was moving day and high time we resumed the march </s>
<s> In the November number Mr. Scull will relate the adventures of the Buffalo Jones African Expedition in Lassoing Lion </s>

<s> 5 NOVEMBER 1910 The Homely Heroine pages 602608 By EDNA FERBER MILLIE WHITCOMB of the fancy goods and notions beckoned me with her finger </s>
<s> I had been standing at Kate O'Malley's counter pretending to admire her new basketweave suitings but in reality reveling in her droll account of how in the train coming up from Chicago Mrs. Judge Porterfield had worn the negro porter's coat over her chilly shoulders in mistake for her husband's </s>
<s> Kate O'Malley can tell a funny story in a way to make the afterdinner pleasantries of a Washington diplomat sound like the clumsy jests told around the village grocery stove </s>
<s> I wanted to tell you that I read that last story of yours said Millie sociably when I had strolled over to her counter and I liked it all but the heroine </s>
<s> She had an `adorable throat' and hair that `waved away from her white brow' and eyes that `now were blue and now gray.' Say why don't you write a story about an ugly girl </s>
<s> My land </s>
<s> protested I </s>
<s> It's bad enough trying to make them accept my stories as it is </s>
<s> That last heroine was a raving beauty but she came back eleven times before the editor of Blakely's succumbed to her charms </s>
<s> Millie's fingers were busy straightening the contents of a tray of combs and imitation jet barrettes </s>
<s> Millie's fingers were not intended for that task </s>
<s> They are slender tapering fingers pinktipped and sensitive </s>
<s> I should think mused she rubbing a cloudy piece of jet with a bit of soft cloth that they'd welcome a homely one with relief </s>
<s> These goddesses are so cloying </s>
<s> Millie Whitcomb's black hair is touched with soft mists of gray and she wears lavender shirtwaists and white stocks edged with lavender </s>
<s> There is a Colonial air about her that has nothing to do with celluloid combs and imitation jet barrettes </s>
<s> It breathes of dim old rooms rich with the tones of mahogany and old brass and Millie in the midst of it graygowned a soft white fichu crossed upon her breast </s>
<s> In our town the clerks are not the pert and gumchewing young persons that storywriters are wont to describe </s>
<s> The girls at Bascom's are institutions </s>
<s> They know us all by our first names and our lives are as an open book to them </s>
<s> Kate O'Malley who has been at Bascom's for so many years that she is rumored to have stock in the company may be said to govern the fashions of our town </s>
<s> She is wont to say when we express a fancy for gray as the color of our new spring suit Oh now Nellie don't get gray again </s>
<s> You had it year before last and don't you think it was just the least leetle bit trying </s>
<s> Let me show you that green that came in yesterday </s>
<s> I said the minute I clapped my eyes on it that it was just the color for you with your brown hair and all </s>
<s> And we end by deciding on the green </s>
<s> The girls at Bascom's are not gossipsthey are too busy for thatbut they may be said to be delightfully well informed </s>
<s> How could they be otherwise when we go to Bascom's for our wedding dresses and party favors and baby flannels </s>
<s> There is news at Bascom's that out daily paper never hears of and wouldn't dare to print if it did </s>
<s> So when Millie Whitcomb of the fancy goods and notions expressed her hunger for a homely heroine I did not resent the suggestion </s>
<s> On the contrary it sent me home in thoughtful mood for Millie Whitcomb has acquired a knowledge of human nature in the dispensing of her fancy goods and notions </s>
<s> It set me casting about for a really homely heroine </s>
<s> There never has been a really ugly heroine in fiction </s>
<s> Authors have started bravely out to write of an unlovely woman but they never have had the courage to allow her to remain plain </s>
<s> On Page 237 she puts on a black lace dress and red roses and the combination brings out unexpected tawny lights in her hair and olive tints in her cheeks and there she is the same old beautiful heroine </s>
<s> Even in the Duchess books one finds the simple Irish girl on donning a green corduroy gown cut square at the neck transformed into a wildrose beauty at sight of whom a ballroom is hushed into admiring awe </s>
<s> There's the case of Jane Eyre too </s>
<s> She is constantly described as plain and mouselike but there are covert hints as to her gray eyes and slender figure and clear skin and we have a sneaking notion that she wasn't such a fright after all </s>
<s> Therefore when I tell you that I am choosing Pearlie Schultz as my leading lady you are to understand that she is ugly not only when the story opens but to the bitter end </s>
<s> In the first place Pearlie is fat </s>
<s> Not plump or rounded or dimpled or deliciously curved but FAT </s>
<s> She bulges in all the wrong places including her chin </s>

<s> It bothers me </s>
<s> But she says you have to do these things when you have a genius in the house and cites the case of Kipling's Recessional which was rescued from the depths of his wastebasket by his wife </s>
<s> Pearlie Schultz used to sit on the front porch summer evenings and watch the couples stroll by and weep in her heart </s>

<s> But a fat girl with a thin girl's soul is a tragedy </s>
<s> Pearlie in spite of her two hundred pounds had the soul of a willow wand </s>

<s> Pearlie sitting alone on the porch in the dark listened to these things and blushed furiously </s>

<s> In the daytime Pearlie worked as public stenographer at the Burke Hotel </s>
