<s> VIII Trotter shut in the VicePresident's private office paid little attention to his surroundings </s>
<s> He did not even know that the desk on which he wrote was of mahogany </s>
<s> He did not notice the imported Daghestan under his feet </s>
<s> He was unconscious of the orchids in the low deskvase of French silver </s>
<s> He was oblivious of the onyx and marble elegance that surrounded him </s>
<s> All he knew was that he had paper and ink in plenty and the Greatest Story of the Age to write </s>
<s> All he knew was that time was precious that two trusted messengers stood before him to deliver his copy that presses in the lower part of the city waited like hungry animals to gulp down his story and that before nightfall a million eyes would widen and half a million hearts would beat a little faster at the words that he was about to write </s>
<s> He pushed back the silver and cutglass desk ornaments the heavy goldframed portrait of a young girl standing beside an opulentbosomed woman in an opera cloak the foolish vase of orchids </s>
<s> He made space for himself and his work </s>
<s> And then he wrote </s>
<s> He wrote with all the rhapsodic passion of a god creating a new world </s>
<s> He began with a preamble that would have broken a copyreader's heart </s>
<s> He followed it up with atmospheric discursiveness that would have worn away an editor's blue pencil </s>
<s> He told how Steam and Steel were supposed to have crushed the Spirit of Romance out of the age </s>
<s> He pointed out how the modern city of stone and concrete seemed no longer to house that wayward and retrospective spirit in which the heart of the poet has forever reveled </s>
<s> Then he sought to demonstrate how true Romance can never die how Wonder is all about even the Wall Street clerk and the fiveo'clock commuter </s>
<s> He put forward the claim that modern New York was as potentially picturesque as alluringly labyrinthine as olden Bagdad itself </s>
<s> He argued that the Thousand and One Tales were nightly recurring in our very midst only we had neither the eyes nor the leisure to observe them </s>
<s> He told of the strange underworlds hidden from the casual eye of subterranean rivers of life which Respectability never sees </s>
<s> He showed how it was only the face of life that had changed </s>
<s> He intimated that Stevenson had unearthed romance enough in an uptodate London that Hugo and Balzac had found it in Paris and he eloquently proclaimed that even today it was to be stumbled across in our city of homes on the Hudson </s>
<s> It was a very rhythmical piece of fine writing and he had his coat off and was working in his shirt sleeves before he had advanced six pages into it </s>
<s> Then he veered about to the story itself </s>
<s> He enlarged on the amount of wealth harbored by a national bank </s>
<s> He explained how this vast wealth was hoarded and protected the massive walls the steel vaults the steam flood pipes the everwatching attendants the tangle of articulate wires that a touch would make garrulous the time locks the floors of cement and railway iron the contact mats which reported the slightest footfall of the trespasser </s>
<s> Then he told how an idea had come to the mind of an idle yegg named Missouri Horton </s>
<s> He told how this wary and cunning and romanticspirited outlaw had planned his attack how he had hired the cellar next to the granitewalled citadel of opulence how he had learned the location of the vaults how he had figured out the thickness of the masonry how he had slowly and quietly prepared for his lonely and Promethean attack </s>
<s> Trotter's sallow young face grew chalkier as he wrote though he was unconscious of either effort or weariness </s>
<s> They brought him luncheon in due time on a napkincovered tray </s>
<s> He lifted the napkin peevishly took a disdainful look at the food gulped down a cup of black coffee and pushed the mess away from him </s>
<s> He had serious work in hand </s>
<s> He wrote on unconscious of time </s>
<s> His mind seemed to sway hypnotically with the reverberations of his own rhetoric </s>
<s> He tossed in a classical allusion or two here and there he left an Old Testament phrase to coruscate along the fringe of his text he even called back one of his copy carriers to revise an unelaborated figure of speech </s>
<s> Then he told how the tunnel was begun how brick by brick and stone by stone a passage was grubbed through every obstacle </s>
<s> He expatiated on the infinite patience of such a man as Horton how Monte Cristo paled beside him how vast difficulties had to be overcome how every stone had to be stowed carefully away in the back of the cellar how in time the mortar and cement had to be ground to a powder and carried secretly away </s>
<s> He told how the tunnel was pushed forward foot by foot how the bank was attacked in its one and only vital spot precisely as a porcupine curled defensively up in the snow is seized by the fishermarten not through open attack but by artfully tunneling up under the quillless belly </s>
<s> Then he retailed how the vast business of this great banking institution went tranquilly and ponderously on how millions were handled and changed and stowed away while all the time the unknown enemy was inch by inch crawling nearer </s>
<s> When a note came up from the Advance office signed by the managing editorthe managing editor who had never been known to praise one of his men in all his twelveyear regimeTrotter took it as a matter of course </s>
<s> Your story is great this note had read </s>
<s> Keep it up </s>
<s> Trotter merely gave the scrawl a second hurried glance </s>
<s> It did not excite him it did not intoxicate </s>
<s> He was already drunk with the wine of creation as delirious as a whirling dervish </s>
<s> And he knew he still had work to do </s>
<s> A whitewhiskered gentleman wearing a pearlbuttoned white waistcoat stepped quietly up to the office door and peered guardedly in over his glasses </s>
<s> Then he tiptoed away unseen with a condoning smile on his astute and thinnosed old face </s>
<s> Trotter had no thought or memory of his surroundings </s>
<s> It was his Story the Story of his life </s>
<s> He sat there entangled and locked together with it unconscious of what it was doing to him oblivious of how like a bloodsucking vampire it was draining the vigor of his youth from him </s>
<s> He was now in the very vortex of his story </s>
<s> He told how he had posted Tiernan at the head of the steps leading down into the plumber's shop </s>
<s> He cunningly enlarged on the huge Irishman's bewilderment his incredulity his blasphemously reiterated demand to know what it was all about </s>
<s> He told how he himself had silently entered the shop how he had crept through to the second door how he had waited for a moment to take out his revolver </s>
<s> He described the hot and reeking air of the tunnel as he crept into its mouth </s>
<s> He pictured the sudden glare of light at the shaft end where Horton stood burning away an outer vault wall with an electrode </s>
<s> He told how the heat and the fumes of that little underground hell bewildered him how he stood gaping at the scene watching the whitehot tongue of fire hissing and licking at its last barrier of steel </s>
<s> He did not neglect to paint how the hardened metal under the electrolyzing current eroding its surface became as chalk decomposing into a charry mass which one blow of a hammer might penetrate </s>
<s> He told how he crept up on the man step by step with his revolver in his hand </s>
<s> He told how he could see the safebreaker's face shining with sweat how he could smell scorching clothing how his eyes began to ache with the lightglare until he threw up a forearm to protect them </s>
<s> He explained how it had been his intention to creep up on the criminal and seize him bodily and how he was defeated in this by a sudden and unlookedfor movement on the part of his unsuspecting enemy </s>
<s> Horton had quickly swung abouthe was in fact groping along the passage floor for a twoquart tin pail partly filled with tap water </s>
<s> The glare had blinded him for the time being and he was in reality feeling for a drink </s>
<s> But the Advance reporter had thought the movement meant that his presence was discovered </s>
<s> And the two men had come together </s>
<s> Trotter told of the fight there hand to hand in the choking tunnel with its tangle of deadly currents </s>
<s> He recounted how the other man's strength had been greater than his own how he felt his breath going how he saw himself being forced closer and closer back on the glaring electrode </s>
<s> He confessed that he had been excited and foolish enough to lose the revolver </s>
<s> He mentioned his indignation when he saw that the other man was actually trying to use his teeth </s>
<s> He described how for the first time it came home to him that he would be killed there that Tiernan could not possibly hear his cries that his heart could not possibly continue to beat without fresh air </s>
<s> Then he had grown desperate </s>
<s> He had apparently gone mad </s>
<s> He had started to use his own teeth </s>
<s> He had set his jaw on the yeggman's hand as it groped for his throat </s>
<s> He had caught the index finger of the other blackened hand and levered it savagely backward backward until the bone broke and it hung limp on the tortured tendon </s>
<s> He had sent the relaxed head skidding against the tunnel wall once twice three times until the sweatstained arms fell away and left him free </s>
<s> He had sat there for many minutes stupidly staring at the unconscious man </s>
<s> Then he had found the revolver at his feet and being too weak to get up he had still sat there contentedly firing a volley of bullets against the steel vault wall until the bank officials were alarmed and an armed guard was sent scurrying about to investigate </s>
<s> And with the timely arrival of Tiernan and that armed guard came an end to the most audacious and staggering criminal coup of the century </s>
<s> It was all very beautiful the very finest of fine writing </s>
<s> Trotter poured his ardent and exultant young soul into it </s>
<s> And when his last page had been written and sent away he sat back in the widearmed moroccoupholstered bankroom chair white with weariness the fires of creation burnt out to the last ember </s>
<s> But one thing sustained and consoled him </s>
<s> He knew as he whisked down to the Advance office in the VicePresident's French touring car that his work was done </s>
<s> He also knew that it was well done </s>
<s> It did not even startle him when Pyott himself held out a coldfingered hand </s>
<s> Good business </s>
<s> was his chief's sardonic commendation </s>
<s> Then I've made good </s>
<s> asked the weary youth without enthusiasm </s>
<s> You've made your TENSTRIKE </s>
<s> was the answer </s>
<s> You're on the city staff at twenty dollars a week </s>
<s> When do I have to go over my proofs </s>
<s> asked the tiredeyed and innocent youth </s>
<s> What proofs </s>
<s> My story proofs </s>
<s> Pyott forced his eyes to meet those of the palefaced boy looking up at him </s>
<s> The managing editor did so without an outward flinch </s>
<s> He was more or less used to such things </s>
<s> You've made good my boy </s>
<s> He casually turned away before he spoke the next sentence </s>
<s> BUT WE'VE HAD TO KILL THAT STORY OF YOURS </s>
<s> Trotter did not move </s>
<s> He did not even gulp </s>
<s> He merely closed his tired eyes and at the same time let his lower lip fall a trifle away from the upper as his breath came brokenly between them </s>
<s> Then he sat down </s>
<s> For they had done more than kill his story </s>
<s> They had killed the spirit of Youth in him </s>
<s> There would be other battles he knew and perhaps other victoriesbut never again that fine careless rapture of Youth </s>
<s> For they had killed his firstborn </s>

<s> 6 AN OPEN MIND WILLIAM JAMES p 800801 By WALTER LIPPMANN Within a week of the death of Professor William James of Harvard University the newspapers had it that Mr. M. S </s>
<s> Ayer of Boston had received a message from his spirit </s>
<s> This news item provoked the ridicule of the people who don't believe in ghosts but the joke was on Mr. Ayer of Boston </s>
<s> When however it was reported that Professor James himself had agreed to communicate with this world if he could and in order to test the reports had left a sealed message to be opened at a certain definite time after his death the incredulous gasped at the professor's amazing credulity </s>
<s> William James wasn't credulous </s>
<s> He was simply openminded </s>
<s> Maybe the soul of man is immortal </s>
<s> The professors couldn't prove it wasn't so James was willing to open his mind to evidence </s>
<s> He was willing to hunt for evidence and to be convinced by it </s>
<s> And in that he was simply keeping America's promise he was actually doing what we as a nation proclaimed that we would do </s>
<s> He was tolerant he was willing to listen to what seems preposterous and to consider what might though queer be true </s>
<s> And he showed that this democratic attitude of mind is every bit as fruitful as the aristocratic determination to ignore new and strangelooking ideas </s>
<s> James was a democrat </s>
<s> He gave all men and all creeds any idea any theory any superstition a respectful hearing </s>
<s> His interest in spiritualism is merely one illustration in a thousand </s>
<s> The hard scientists knew it was a hoax because they couldn't explain it and the sentimentalists knew it was the truth because they wished it to be but James wanted to know the facts </s>
<s> So he went to Mrs. Piper and heard her out </s>
<s> Nay he listened to Palladino and to Munsterberg </s>
<s> They pretended to know and maybe they did </s>
<s> And last year when Frank Harris published his book on Shakespeare to show that the unknown life and character of the poet could be drawn from his works the other professors laughed the theory out of court </s>
<s> James went to Shakespeare and read the plays all over again to test the Harris theory </s>
<s> Maybe the poet could be known by his works </s>
<s> The fact that the theory was revolutionary did not alter the possibility that it might be true </s>
<s> So with religion </s>
<s> A scientist living in an age when science is dogmatically irreligious he turned from its cocksure reasoning to ask for the facts </s>
<s> He went to the lives of the saints </s>
<s> Not to Herbert Spencer you see </s>
<s> When he wanted to study the religious experience he went to the people who had had it to Santa Theresa and Mrs. Eddy </s>
<s> They might know something the professors didn't know </s>
<s> And again at the age of sixtyfive with the whole of New England's individualism behind him he asked about socialism </s>
<s> When he met H </s>
<s> G </s>
<s> Wells he listened to the socialist and as it happens was converted </s>
<s> So he said so </s>
<s> James was no more afraid of a new political theory than he was of ghosts and he was no more afraid of proclaiming a new theory or an old one than he was of being a ghost </s>
<s> I think he would have listened with an open mind to the devil's account of heaven and I'm sure he would have heard him out on hell </s>
<s> James knew that he didn't know </s>
<s> He never acted upon the notion that the truth was his store of wisdom </s>
<s> Perhaps that is why he kept on rummaging about in other people's stores and commending their goods </s>
<s> He seemed to take a delight in writing introductions and appreciations of new books and in going out of his way to listen to a young doctor of philosophy or an undergraduate discussion of pragmatism or the poetry of an obscure mystic </s>
<s> And optimist that he was by virtue of his unceasing freshness of interest there is nothing more openminded in our literature than his chivalrous respect for the pessimism of Francis Thompson </s>
<s> Speak not of comfort where no comfort is Speak not at all can words make foul things fair </s>
<s> Our life's a cheat our death a black abyss Hush and be mute envisaging despair </s>
<s> He felt with all sorts of men </s>
<s> He understood their demand for immediate answers to the great speculative questions of life </s>
<s> God freedom immortality nature as moral or nonmoralthese were for him not matters of idle scientific wonder but of urgent need The scientific demand that men should wait till doomsday or till such time as our senses and intellect working together may have raked in evidence enough for answers to these questions is says James the queerest idol ever manufactured in the philosophic cave </s>
<s> We cannot wait for a final solution </s>
<s> Our daily life is full of choices that we cannot dodge and some guide we simply must have </s>
<s> There can be no loitering at the crossroads </s>
<s> We are busy </s>
<s> We must choose whether we will it or not and where all is doubt who shall refuse us the right to believe what seems most adapted to our needs </s>
<s> Not know you understand but believe </s>
<s> That is the famous position taken in The Will to Believe </s>
<s> As James has once pointed out its real title should have been The Right to Believe </s>
<s> No doctrine in James's thinking has been more persistently misunderstood </s>
<s> Yet it rests on the simplest of insights that atheism and theism are both dogmas for there is scientific evidence for neither that to withhold judgment is really to make a judgment and act as if God didn't exist that until the evidence is complete men have a right to believe what they most need </s>
<s> James has acted upon that right </s>
<s> He has made a picture compounded of the insights of feeling the elaborations of reason and the daily requirements of men </s>
<s> It is a huge guess if you like to be verified only at the end of the world </s>
<s> But it has made many men at home in the universe </s>
<s> And this democrat understood the need of feeling at home in the world and he understood also that the aristocrats are not at home here </s>
<s> Perhaps that's why they are aristocrats </s>
<s> The luxurious classes he says are blind to man's real relation to the globe he lives on and to the permanently hard and solid foundations of his higher life </s>
<s> And he prescribed for themfor their culture I meanthis treatment To coal and iron mines to freight trains to fishing fleets in December to dishwashing clotheswashing and windowwashing to roadbuilding and tunnelmaking to foundries and stokeholes and to the frames of skyscrapers would our gilded youths be drafted off according to their choice to get the childishness knocked out of them and to come back into society with healthier sympathies and soberer ideas </s>
<s> This and thoughts like this and kindnesses like this put James not alone among the democrats of this uncertain world but among the poets also among the poetic philosophers who like Goethe Schopenhauer and Whitman have a sense of the pace of things </s>
<s> Sunlight and stormcloud the subdued busyness of outdoors the rumble of cities the mud of life's beginning and the heaven of its hopes stain his pages with the glad sweaty sense of life itself </s>
<s> It is an encouraging thought that America should have produced perhaps the most tolerant man of our generation </s>
<s> It is a stimulating thought that he was a man whose tolerance never meant the kind of timidity which refuses to take a stand because there is so much to be said on both sides </s>
<s> As every one knows he fought hard for his ideas because he believed in them and because he wanted others to believe in them </s>
<s> The propagandist was strong in William James </s>
<s> He wished to give as well as receive </s>
<s> And he listened for truth from anybody and from anywhere and in any form </s>
<s> He listened for it from Emma Goldman the pope or a sophomore preached from a pulpit a throne or a soapbox in the language of science in slang in fine rhetoric or in the talk of a ward boss </s>
<s> And he told his conclusions </s>
<s> He told them too without the expert's arrogance toward the man in the street and without the dainty and finicky horror of being popular and journalistic </s>
<s> He would quote Mr. Dooley on God to make himself understood among men </s>
<s> He would have heard God gladly in the overalls of a carpenter even though He came to preach that the soul of man is immortal </s>
<s> So openminded was he so very much of a democrat </s>
